# 3.9 SU-MIMO Management

## 3.9.0-3 SU-MIMO Management Document Owner Deputy Vimal Radhakrishnan (ID: 11139199)

## 3.9.1 DL SU-MIMO

### 3.9.1.1 Allowed transmission scheme on physical downlink shared data channel

#### 3.9.1.1.0-1 Allowed transmission scheme on physical downlink shared data channel PDSCH SM scheduling and antPort selection (ID: 11139212)

**3.9.1.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13327686`)

Allowed transmission scheme on physical downlink shared data channel If ( dlMimoMode = 1x1 Single antenna transmission ) any PDSCH for CRNTI transmission shall be scheduled with 1 Layers and precoding W=1.

If **(dlMimoMode is ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_2x2) any PDSCH for CRNTI transmission shall be scheduled with spatial multiplexing & 1 or 2 Layers according to the latest RI and PMI report from the UE.**

Else If (dlMimoMode is OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing_2x2), PDSCH for CRNTI transmission shall be scheduled with spatial multiplexing & 1 or 2 layers according to the latest RI report from the UE.

If **(dlMimoMode is ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_4x4) PDSCH for CRNTI transmission shall be scheduled with spatial multiplexing & up to 4 layers according to the latest RI and PMI report from the UE.**

else if (dlMimoMode is OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing_4x4) PDSCH for CRNTI transmission shall be scheduled with spatial multiplexing & up to 4 layers according to the latest RI report from the UE.

If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO or CL 32x4 MIMO, up to 4 layers according to the latest RI and PMI report from the UE.

For 1RX RedCap UE (5G_UP_10923_replaced([11354642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucJ5ZPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), there is only rank 1 used, also gNB shall assume that UE Rank Indicator (RI) is equal to Rank1 (see 5G_UP_ALG_9657_replaced([11139366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and select PMI accordingly, if any.

While the cell enter into energySavingState = reducedEnergySaving (5G_CP_OTH_9124_replaced([11609773](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y472ifwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the cell keeps all visible indications of its MIMO settings unchanged.

When the cell enter into energySavingState = reducedEnergySaving, PdschPrecodingOption4x4=0,4 (no port selection) and for the case of non-beamforming mode, all DL transmissions shall be limited up to rank 2, L2-PS shall restrict the number of layer > 2 for use. That is,

\- If the reported RI<=2, the rank shall be scheduled based on reported value.

\- else if the reported RI>2, L2-PS shall use rank 2 for schedling independent reported value.

When the cell enter into energySavingState = reducedEnergySaving and for the case of sub-sectorization mode and digital beamforming mode,

-If dlMimoMode is 'OL 2x2 MIMO', rank shall be limited to rank 1.

-If dlMimoMode is 'OL 4x4/4x2 MIMO', rank shall be limited for up to rank 2 in the case of no port selection.

-In the case of port selection (PdschPrecodingOption4x4=1, 5, 2, 6), rank shall be limited to rank 1.

-If dlMimoMode is 'CL 2x2 MIMO', rank shall be limited to rank 1.

-If dlMimoMode is 'CL 4x4/4x2 MIMO', depends on port selection or not.

-In the case of port selection (PdschPrecodingOption4x4=1, 5, 2, 6), rank shall be limited to rank 1.

-In the case of no port selection

 for PDSCH transmissions for C-RNTIs with valid CSI reports, depends on i13:

 i13=0, rank shall be limited to rank 1.

 I13 !=0, rank shall be limited to up to rank 2.

 Otherwise: rank shall be limited to rank 1.

If dlMimoMode is 'CL8x4 MIMO', only support no port selection (PdschPrecodingOption4x4=0)

 for PDSCH transmissions for C-RNTIs with valid CSI reports, depends on i13:

 i13=0, rank shall be limited to rank 1.

 I13!=0, rank shall be limited to up to rank 1.

 Otherwise: rank shall be limited to rank 1.

Note: During above rank downgrade, the codebookIndex, the PMI value i11, i12, i13, i2 should not be changed.

For other energySavingState, L2-PS shall remove above rank restriction.

[CB015174-A]

If MIMO muting with hopping indicator due to RF thermal management is received, L2-PS shall restrict the number of layers for use. That is,

If dlMimoMode is 'OL 2x2 MIMO' or 'CL 2x2 MIMO',

\- L2-PS shall use rank 1 for scheduling independent reported value.

If dlMimoMode is 'OL 4x4/4x2 MIMO' or 'CL 4x4/4x2 MIMO',

\- and if the reported RI in the CSI report<=2, the rank shall be scheduled based on reported value.

\- else if the reported RI in the CSI report>2, L2-PS shall use rank 2 for scheduling independent reported value.

[End CB015174-A]

For 1-layer SU-MIMO, the PDSCH antenna port is {1000}.

For 2-layer SU-MIMO,

**-For DL DMRS configuration type 1,** if the number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data is 1, the PDSCH antenna ports are {1000, 1001}. Otherwise, the PDSCH antenna ports are are {1000, 1001} or {1000, 1002} according to rdDlAntennaPortFlagForTwoLayers (cf. 5G_L2_1080_replaced([11186547](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276jsvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).****

**\- For DL DMRS configuration type 2,** the PDSCH antenna ports are {1000, 1001}.****

For 3-layer SU-MIMO, the PDSCH antenna ports are {1000, 1001, 1002}.

For 4-layer SU-MIMO, the PDSCH antenna ports are {1000, 1001, 1002, 1003}.

In TDD FR1, if the PRB is scheduled for PDSCH in SSB slot without CSI-RS for tracking and the RI indicator is larger than 2, then two layers SU-MIMO shall be used, precoding with rank adaption refers to .

~~(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3180_replaced([11139272](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for 4Tx, and 5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for 8Tx)**.** ~~

Generally, closed loop/open loop shall be indicated according to dlMimoMode.

---

### 3.9.1.2 Precoder settings and CSI handling for allowed transmission schemes

#### 3.9.1.2.0-1 Precoder settings and CSI handling for allowed transmission schemes PDSCH precoding and spatial mode settings for different transmission schemes (ID: 11139234)

**3.9.1.2.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `12789540`)

Precoder settings and CSI handling for allowed transmission schemes This requirement defines PDSCH precoding and spatial mode settings for different transmission schemes. The scenarios for Comformence test are not defined hereafter.

If the cell has dlMimoMode as CL 8x4 MIMO **[CB008577-B] or CL 32x4 MIMO**[End CB008577-B]:****

one UE can be configured with 4 port or 8 port **[CB008577-B] or 32 port**[End CB008577-B] CSI-RS for channel acquisition:****

 If L2 receives configuration of **[Before CB008577-B] 4 port or 8 port**[CB008577-B] x port **[End CB008577-B] of CSI-RS for the 1st time, then it shall be used for DL scheduling immediately ;** ****

 If L2 receives changed number of ports of CSI-RS via User modify, **[Before CB008577-B] i.e. from 4 to 8, or from 8 to 4,**[End CB008577-B] **L2 shall adopt the old number of ports for DL scheduling until new valid CSI report based on newly configured CSI-RS is received at L2 ;** ****

 If no CSI-RS **configuration is received for the UE, or the UE dedicated configuration is not activated including the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration, or for common channels(PDSCH for P-RNTI/SI-RNTI/RA-RNTI/Temporary C-RNTI), the default precoding mode defined by dlMimoMode [Before CB008577-B] CL 8x4 MIMO [End CB008577-B] shall be used for DL scheduling ;**

 High important note: even the UE does not have valid CSI **report of x CSI-RS port L2 may still see this UE as x port, for example, when CQI is out of date, or for the 1st time CSI-RS/report is configured to the UE;**

else if the cell has dlMimoMode as CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO or OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO:

one UE can only be configured with 4 port CSI-RS for channel acquisition:

 L2 shall handle the PDSCH for C-RNTIs with valid CSI report and beam reports as 4 port ;

 L2 shall handle the PDSCH for P-RNTI/SI-RNTI/RA-RNTI/Temporary C-RNTI or PDSCH for C-RNTIs (w/o valid CSI report and beam reports, or without UE dedicated configuration actived **including the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration) as the default precoding mode defined by dlMimoMode CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO or OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO shall be used for DL scheduling ;**

else if the cell has dlMimoMode as 1x1 Single antenna transmission:

one UE can only be configured with 1 port CSI-RS for channel acquisition:

 L2 shall handle the PDSCH for C-RNTIs with numStreamIndex = 1 and 1 port without using existing precoding and regardless CSI-RS report or beam reports ;

 L2 shall handle the PDSCH for P-RNTI/SI-RNTI/RA-RNTI/Temporary C-RNTI with 1 port ;

else:

one UE can only be configured with 2 port CSI-RS for channel acquisition:

 L2 shall handle the PDSCH for C-RNTIs with valid CSI report and beam reports as 2 port. ;

 L2 shall handle the PDSCH for P-RNTI/SI-RNTI/RA-RNTI/Temporary C-RNTI or PDSCH for C-RNTIs (w/o valid CSI report and beam reports, or without UE dedicated configuration activated including the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration) as the default precoding mode defined by dlMimoMode CL 2x2 MIMO or OL 2x2 MIMO shall be used for DL scheduling ;

Note When **the cell has dlMimoMode as CL 8x4 MIMO and actDlSrsBm is True, UEs with 8 port CSI-RS configured always adopt port selection for rank2 as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_7278_replaced([11112223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

---

**3.9.1.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12805302`)

Precoder settings and CSI handling for allowed transmission schemes The requirement applies when NRCELL\actDlMuMimo is false. When NRCELL\actDlMuMimo is true, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4364_replaced([11141957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note that with and without port selection NumStreamIndex is 4 cf. also additional L1 references in the first table**.**

**Wcsirs = Identity** (5G_UP_ALG_625_replaced([11100259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knMEmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | No port selection (NumStreamIndex=4) | - | 2 beams | 2 beams | 2 beams | 5G_UP_ALG_416_replaced([11097863](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km6Xw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  
Port selection (NumStreamIndex=2) | 1 beam | 1 beam | - | - | ~~5G_UP_ALG_429_replaced([11097968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km6-1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))~~ 5G_UP_ALG_393_replaced([11097539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km5JoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |   
  
For SU MIMO, Rank2 is sent on 2 beams (i.e. 4 streams) in regular slots (no SSB /TRS slot) where there is 1C4+BF in CPRI or eCPRI.

Notes :

For SU MIMO, Rank2 is sent on 1 beam (i.e. 2 streams) if PDSCH is scheduled on SSB/TRS slots and there is only 1C4+BF (cf. 5G_UP_2530_replaced([11390617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufUiI_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in CPRI or eCPRI without FD beamforming.

For SU MIMO, Rank2 is sent on 2 beams (i.e. 4 streams) if PDSCH is scheduled on SSB/TRS slots and there is 1C4+BF (cf. 5G_UP_2530_replaced([11390617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufUiI_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in eCPRI with FD beamforming.

For SU MIMO, Rank2 is sent on 2 beams (i.e. 4 streams) when PDSCH is scheduled on SSB/TRS slots for CPRI and 2C4+BF (cf. 5G_UP_2536_replaced([11390702](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufVJMvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). But this configuration is more likely to be supported for MU MIMO only due to a PDL rule at OAM side.

(-) means this case does not occur i.e. 5G-L2-PS does not configure this to 5G-L1-DL.

In supercell mode the users associated SSB beam, utilizes C2 and C4 L1 subcell type. the precoder uses the dlMimoMode as configured. Port selection and switching precodingOption is not applied.

---

#### 3.9.1.2.1 UCI and Precoder settings

##### 3.9.1.2.1-1 Precoding options

###### 3.9.1.2.1-1.0-2 Precoding options If subcell type is C4, two users (ranks &lt;= 2) can be scheduled separately using different AxC/eAxC indexes with one subcell, the AxC\eAxC related parameters shall be set as below: · numStreamIndex = 2 · streamIndex = {0, 1} or {2, 3} The detail about AxC and eAxC can be found in 5G_UP_ALG_14007_replaced( 11098058 ). If subcell type is not C4 (A4 for example), values of numStreamIndex and streamIndex are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_14007_replaced( 11098058 ). If subcell type is A1, the stream configuration for 1x1 Single antenna transmission with statically rank=1 shall be as numStreamIndex = 1 and streamIndex = {0} If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True, the algorithm to select stream configuration for PDSCH is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_7433_replaced( 11145188 ). Note: 5G_UP_ALG_6591_replaced( 11139260 ) shall be followed when and NRCELL\actDlMuMimo is false. [CB013440-A] For non-beamforming mode (5G_UP_908_replaced( 11353388 )), if NIDD parameters configuration NRCELL.actEnhCtrlChannelTrans = True and (NRCELL.enhCtrlChannelTransMode = 1  [Before CB013440-A-UPD002] [CB013440-B]or 3[End CB013440-B] [CB013440-A-UPD002] 4 or 6 [End CB013440-A-UPD002]) , gNB-DU shall decide number of streams according to precodings in 5G_UP_ALG_3183_replaced( 11139297 ).[End CB013440-A] [CB013440-D] Note supercell mode (5G_UP_5548_replaced( 11353423 )) follows non-beamforming mode (5G_UP_908_replaced( 11353388 )). [End CB013440-D] (ID: 11139595)

##### 3.9.1.2.1-2 Precoding options

###### 3.9.1.2.1-2.0-2 Precoding options This conversion assumes the PMI is based on type I single-panel codebook and codebookMode is 1. About codebooks using 2/4/8 CSI-RS antenna ports, please refer to the table 6.3.1.1.2-1 in 3GPP 38.212 and the table 5.2.2.2.1-1 in 3GPP 38.214. For closed loop transmissions of 1) 4xN MIMO, if UE's rank is 1 and port selection is enabled, 2) CL 8x4 MIMO and for UE has 8 port configured and rank is 1, [CB008577-B] 3)CL 32x4 MIMO and for UE has 8/32 port configured and rank is 1: [End CB008577-B]**** the codebooks of more than 2 ports can be equivalently converted to 2 ports codebooks according to the below mapping table: i2 Codebook index 0 0 1 1 2 2 3 3 For closed loop transmissions of 1) 4xN MIMO, 2) CL 8x4 MIMO and for UE has 8 port configured, [CB008577-B] 3)CL 32x4 MIMO and for UE has 8/32 port configured: [End CB008577-B]: if UE's rank is 2 and port selection is enabled, the codebooks of more than 2 ports can be equivalently converted to 2 ports codebooks according to the below mapping table:**** i2 Codebook index 0 0 1 1 (ID: 12827579)

##### 3.9.1.2.1.1 Default precoder settings

###### 3.9.1.2.1.1.0-1 Default precoder settings Default precoder settings CL/OL (2x2 transmissions) (ID: 11139281)

**3.9.1.2.1.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11139291`)

Default precoder settings The default precoder settings apply to below scenarios:

 PDSCH scheduled for P-RNTI/SI-RNTI/RA-RNTI/Temporary C-RNTI

 PDSCH scheduled for C-RNTIs w/o valid CSI and beam reports [CNI-81991] or without UE dedicated configuration actived [End CNI-81991]

 Beam Failure Recovery, refer to 5G_L2_666_replaced([11164473](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25s9PPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Timer rdDlCsiFallBackTimer (cf. 5G_L2_1101_replaced([11186535](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276jsPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires.

The number of PDSCH layers is 1.

For closed loop:

 The spatial mode is closed loop spatial multiplexing.

 The codebook index is 0 (see table 5.2.2.2.1-1 in 38.214).

For open loop:

 The spatial mode is open loop spatial multiplexing.

 The 3GPP defined codebook is not used.

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.1.0-2 Default precoder settings Default precoder settings CL/OL (4Tx transmissions) (ID: 11139297)

**3.9.1.2.1.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11139317`)

Default precoder settings The default precoder settings apply to below scenarios:

 PDSCH scheduled for P-RNTI/SI-RNTI/RA-RNTI/Temporary C-RNTI

 PDSCH scheduled for C-RNTIs w/o valid CSI and beam reports or without UE dedicated configuration actived including the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration

 Beam Failure Recovery, refer to 5G_L2_666_replaced([11164473](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25s9PPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Timer rdDlCsiFallBackTimer (cf. 5G_L2_1101_replaced([11186535](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276jsPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires.

The number of PDSCH layers is 1.

For closed loop:

 The spatial mode is closed loop spatial multiplexing.

 The codebook is selected as i1,1 = 0, i1,2 = 0, i2 = 0 (see table 5.2.2.2.1-5 in 38.214).

For open loop:

 The spatial mode is open loop spatial multiplexing.

 The 3GPP defined codebook is not used.

For case of digital beamforming mode (see 5G_UP_912_replaced([11353600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucAve_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), pdschPrecodingOption4x4 is set to 2 (port selection up to rank4).

For cases of sub-sectorization mode (5G_UP_910_replaced([11353407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hU_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[Before CB013440-A] and non-beamforming mode (5G_UP_908_replaced([11353388](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hUPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End CB013440-A], pdschPrecodingOption4x4 is set to 0 (no port selection).****

**[CB013440-A] For non-beamforming mode (5G_UP_908_replaced([11353388](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hUPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if NIDD parameters configuration _NRCELL.actEnhCtrlChannelTrans = True and_**

  * if _NRCELL.enhCtrlChannelTransMode =__[Before CB013440-A-UPD002] 1_ _[CB013440-A-UPD002] 4_ _[End CB013440-A-UPD002] , (5G_UP_13733_replaced([11353784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucB9oPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,_***** *



\-- gNB-DU shall select precoding as a pair of antennas that belong to a cross polarizations. If dlMimoMode equals 4x4 or 4x2 CL SU MIMO, refers to 5G_UP_ALG_407_replaced([11097619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km5wsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If dlMimoMode equals 4x4 or 4x2 OL SU MIMO, refers to 5G_UP_ALG_344_replaced([11097224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km2GXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CB013440-B]- else if _NRCELL.enhCtrlChannelTransMode =**[Before CB013440-A-UPD002] 3**[CB013440-A-UPD002] 6 **[End CB013440-A-UPD002]:_******* *

\-- gNB-DU shall select precoding as a pair of antennas that belong to a cross polarizations. If dlMimoMode equals 4x4 or 4x2 CL SU MIMO, refers to 5G_UP_ALG_407_replaced([11097619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km5wsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **[End CB013440-B],**

  * else



\-- pdschPrecodingOption4x4 is set to 0 (no port selection).**[End CB013440-A]**

**[CB013440-A-UPD002] Note: For non-beamforming mode (5G_UP_908_replaced([11353388](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hUPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if NIDD parameters configuration _NRCELL.actEnhCtrlChannelTrans = True and _NRCELL.enhCtrlChannelTransMode is not 0 (5G_UP_13733_replaced([11353784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucB9oPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the __precoding for a given UE on a HARQ retransmission shall be the same as the initial transmission for the current HARQ process._ *[End CB013440-A-UPD002]_*******

Note supercell mode (5G_UP_5548_replaced([11353423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hVvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) follows non-beamforming mode (5G_UP_908_replaced([11353388](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hUPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[CB013440-A] gNB-DU shall support online change of _NRCELL.actEnhCtrlChannelTrans**and NRCELL.enhCtrlChannelTransMode. Note this is general for all subfeatures.**[End CB013440-A]_******

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.1.0-3 Default precoder settings Default precoder settings CL (8Tx transmissions) (ID: 11139322)

**3.9.1.2.1.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11139327`)

Default precoder settings **Default layer, precoding, beam setting**

Default setting are used when cell has dlMimoMode as CL 8x4 and:

For UE specific PDSCH:

  * Before valid CSI report, including msg2/msg4, or



\- outdated CSI, i.e. timer rdDlCsiFallBackTimer (cf. 5G_L2_1101_replaced([11186535](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276jsPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is expired, or

\- Beam Failure Recovery, refer to 5G_L2_666_replaced([11164473](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25s9PPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For Cell specific PDSCH for common channels:

  * Paging, SIB, OSI.



The default number of layers is 1.

The default precoding matrix is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3171_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The beam PatternID is chosen by the best SSB/CSI-RS (for beam management) beam for this UE. For common channel paging and SIB, the beam PatternID is set according to SSB beam sweeping manner as before.

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.1.0-4 Default precoder settings Default precoder settings CL (32Tx transmissions) (ID: 12780250)

**3.9.1.2.1.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12780251`)

Default precoder settings **Default layer, precoding, beam setting**

Default setting are used when cell has dlMimoMode as CL 32x4 and:

For UE specific PDSCH:

  * Before valid CSI report, including msg2/msg4, or



\- outdated CSI, i.e. timer rdDlCsiFallBackTimer (cf. 5G_L2_1101_replaced([11186535](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276jsPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is expired, or

For Cell specific PDSCH for common channels:

  * Paging, SIB, OSI.



If dlMimoMode is CL32x4, gNB-DU shall set precoding and spatial mode for all kind of PDSCH, either RA-Msg2, RA-Msg4, SRB0, or any transmission until the UE dedicated configuration is activated (5G_UP_ALG_18227_replaced([11153313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) including the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration, paging/SI or normal PDSCH according to 5G_UP_ALG_3171_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The default number of layers is 1. 

gNB-DU shall assume UE reports all UCI bits as 0 for the rank if there no valid CSI report. This shall be applied for UEs that have 8 ports or 32 ports CSI-RS configured. Default precoding matrix is decided accordingly. Common channels shall also apply the same default precoding.

The beam of UE specific PDSCH is refers to [12777257: FDD: Maximum Two beams from CSI feedback](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ldAtcI1KEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). The beam of common channel PDSCH is shall be the full sector beam.

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.2 UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI

###### 3.9.1.2.1.2.0-1 UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI (1x1 transmissions) (ID: 11139337)

**3.9.1.2.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11139346`)

UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI The number of layers for a given UE on a HARQ retransmission shall be fixed as 1.

[CB010767-A]

For 1Rx RedCap check 5G_UP_10923_replaced([11354642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucJ5ZPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For other UEs,

[End CB010767-A]

In the decoded UE CSI report received in UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs for a 1x1 transmission (UCI bits):

  * 1 bit (optional) can be received for SR

  * bit number for the RI report is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_9657_replaced([11139366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which has a table to define number of RI bits under all possible scenarios.

  * 4 bits are expected for CQI report (used for link adaptation)

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.2.0-2 UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI (2x2 transmissions) (ID: 11139352)

**3.9.1.2.1.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11139361`)

UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI [CB010767-A]

For 1Rx RedCap check 5G_UP_10923_replaced([11354642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucJ5ZPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For other UEs,

[End CB010767-A]

The number of layers for a given UE transmission shall be selected as the latest RI decoded at 5G-L1-UL from CSI report.

The number of layers for a given UE on a HARQ retransmission shall be selected as the number of layers of the first transmission for the current HARQ process.

In the decoded UE CSI report received in UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs for a 2x2 transmission (UCI bits):

  * 1 bit (optional) can be received for SR

  * For the RI report, the expected bits number is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_9657_replaced([11139366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which has a table to define number of RI bits under all possible scenarios.

  * 4 bits are expected for CQI report (used for link adaptation)

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.2.0-3 UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI (4Tx transmissions) (ID: 11139366)

**3.9.1.2.1.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11139385`)

UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI [CB010767-A]For 1Rx RedCap check 5G_UP_10923_replaced([11354642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucJ5ZPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and they should be treated based on row "any" from the below table [PR770392] except if reporting is configured without PMI reporting, then fixed number of RI bits are used (according to table below) [End PR770392]. For other UEs,[End CB010767-A]

The number of layers for a given UE transmission shall be selected as the latest RI decoded at 5G-L1-UL from CSI report. In the decoded UE CSI report for a 4 antenna ports transmission (UCI bits):

  * 1 bit (optional) can be received for SR

  * For the RI report, the expected number of bits shall be decided based on NIDD NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode and maxNumOfDlLayers except when the non-PMI reporting is used then the numbers of antenna ports shall be used if it differs form the vealue of maxNumOfDlLayers. See the detail in below table.


|  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---  
DL MIMO Mode(input) | maxNumOfDlLayers(input) | Number of antenna ports of CSI (input) | Number of allowed rank values (output) | Bit width of RI (output) | Notes  
1x1 transmission | 1 | 1 | 1 | 0 | CB008983  
2x2 MIMO (CL or OL) | [Before PR770392] 2 [PR770392] <=2 [End PR770392] | 2 | 2 | 1 |   
2x2 MIMO (CL or OL) | >= 4 | 2 | 2 | 1 |   
4x4 or 4x2 MIMO with PMI reporting | 2 | 4 | 2 | 1 | CB009086-B  
4x4 or 4x2 MIMO without PMI reporting | NA | 4 | NA | 2 | CB009086-B  
4x4 or 4x2 MIMO with PMI reporting | >= 4 | 4 | 4 | 2 | CB009086-B  
any | 1 | any | 1 | 0 | 5GC001248-M, CB010767-A  
  
  * 4 bits are expected for CQI report (used for link adaptation)



The number of layers for a given UE on a HARQ retransmission shall be selected as the number of layers of the initial transmission for the current HARQ process.

[CB010767-A]

Note:

maxNumOfDlLayers is a value which is recevied from the UE Capability (maxNumberMIMO-LayersPDSCH)

[End CB010767-A]

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.2.0-4 UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI (8Tx [CB008577-B] /32Tx [End CB008577-B] transmissions) (ID: 11139392)

**3.9.1.2.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11139398`)

UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI **Periodic Report on PUCCH**

When the cell has dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO and for UEs with 8 port CSI-RS configured.

In the decoded UE CSI report received in UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs for a 8 CSI-RS antenna ports transmission:

Refer to 5G_L2_952_replaced([11180418](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MK__vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), overall numOfBitsOfUciInformation shall be set to the sum of nANPucch and the size of the expected CSI report, if any;

The UCI bits of CSI report part shall be calculated as 5G_UP_ALG_3626_replaced([11160044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktN0EfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.2.0-5 UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI Coexistence of CL (8Tx transmissions) and CL (4Tx transmissions) (ID: 11139405)

**3.9.1.2.1.2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11139414`)

UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI If actDlSrsBm is true and dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO, both 4 and 8 ports CSI-RS/precoding coexist in the cell.

If {actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true and [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001] is greater than 4}, both 4 and 8 ports CSI-RS/precoding coexist in the cell.

For UEs with 4 ports CSI-RS the UCI bit and precoder shall follow 5G_UP_ALG_9657_replaced([11139366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), Note n1-n2 can only be 2-1 for this case;

For UEs with 8 ports CSI-RS the UCI bit and precoder shall follow 5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), Note n1-n2 can be diffierent value based on configuration from Cplane.

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.2.0-6 UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI Coexistence of CL (32Tx transmissions) and CL (8Tx transmissions) (ID: 12788230)

**3.9.1.2.1.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12788231`)

UCI bits for SR/Rank/CQI If the cell has dlMimoMode is CL 32x4 MIMO, gNB-DU shall support 32 and 8 ports CSI-RS/precoding coexist in the cell. 

Common channel without UE info shall shall follow: [12780250: Default precoder settings CL (32Tx transmissions)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bc6RcI1MEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For UEs with 8 ports CSI-RS configured, precoder shall follow: [11139457: Precoder settings (8Tx transmissions)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krnRmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11139322: Default precoder settings CL (8Tx transmissions)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For UEs with 32 ports CSI-RS configured, precoder shall follow: [11139487: Precoder settings (32Tx transmissions)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krnRnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [12780250: Default precoder settings CL (32Tx transmissions)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bc6RcI1MEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

For UE modification with changed number of ports, refers to [11139234: PDSCH precoding and spatial mode settings for different transmission schemes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

---

##### 3.9.1.2.1.3 Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank

###### 3.9.1.2.1.3.0-1 Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank Precoder settings (2x2 transmissions) (ID: 11139427)

**3.9.1.2.1.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11139430`)

Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank The NIDD NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode informs whether OL (Open Loop) or CL (Closed Loop) is selected. This impacts the precoding matrix choice.

For closed loop transmissions:

The precoding matrix is selected as the latest PMI decoded at 5G-L1-UL from CSI report. The precoding matrix is selected as the latest decoded PMI indicating the same number of layers as the first transmission for the current HARQ process.

The decoded UE CSI report received in UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs for a 2x2 transmission (UCI bits):

  * For CL, 2 or 1 bits are expected for the PMI report when the ranks is 1 or 2, respectively. (It refers to the codebook indices defined in Table 5.2.2.2.1-1 in 38.214 V15.0.0 with an extension, see 5G_UP_IF_2078_replaced([11517023](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tUcauPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



For open loop transmissions:

  * 0 bit is expected for PMI report



The reportQuantity is either cri-RI-PMI-CQI or cri-RI-CQI according to UE capabilities. When reportQuantity = cri-RI-PMI-CQI, PMI report from the UE shall be ignored by 5G-L2-PS. The precoding matrix corresponding to the reported rank is determined by the Open Loop scheme at 5G-L1-DL.Thus it is not indicated by 5G-L2-PS in DlData_PdschSendReq.

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.3.0-2 Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank Precoding settings (4Tx transmissions) (ID: 11139437)

**3.9.1.2.1.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11139452`)

Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank The NIDD NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode informs whether OL (Open Loop) or CL (Closed Loop) is selected. This impacts the precoding matrix choice.

For closed loop transmissions:

The precoding matrix is selected as the latest PMI decoded at 5G-L1-UL from CSI report. The decoded UE CSI report for a 4 antenna ports transmission (UCI bits) shall support the following number of bits :

  * For reportQuantity = cri-RI-PMI-CQI, PMI report is expected with below information:



\-- if rank1, PMI has 5 bits (i1.1 has 3 bits, i1.2 has 0 bit, i2 has 2 bits)

\-- if rank2, PMI has 5 bits (i1.1 has 3 bits, i1.2 has 0 bit, i1.3 has 1 bit, i2 has 1 bit)

\-- if rank3 or rank4, PMI has 4 bits (i1.1 has 3 bits, i1.2 has 0 bit, i1.3 has 0 bit, i2 has 1 bit)

The PMI selected shall be sent by 5G-L2-PS to 5G-L1-DL via DlData_PdschSendReq through the following parameters:

  * i1Codebook4AntPorts[0] = i1,1

  * i1Codebook4AntPorts[1] = 0

  * i1Codebook4AntPorts[2] = i1,3 when the rank >1 otherwise i1Codebook4AntPorts[2] shall be set 0

  * i2Codebook4AntPorts = i2




If subcell type is C4, two users (ranks <= 2) can be scheduled separately using different AxC/eAxC indexes with one subcell. Codebooks for 4xN MIMO shall be converted to codebooks for 2x2 MIMO by mapping i1.1, i1.2, i1.3 and i2 to codebook indexes with rules which are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3190_replaced([11139602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krofs_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR758319] Note: For transmission and retransmission via subband beams, the precoding matrix is not needed as 5G_UP_ALG_13751_replaced([11156407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0Le_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Reported rank is used with some latency as 5G_UP_ALG_21414_replaced([11156886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If initial transmission is via subband beams and retransmission is via not subband beams: The precoding matrix is selected as the latest decoded PMI indicating the same number of layers as the initial transmission for the current HARQ process. 5G-L2-PS shall assume UE reports all UCI bits as 0 for the rank if there no valid CSI report. [End PR758319]

For open loop transmissions:

The reportQuantity is either cri-RI-PMI-CQI or cri-RI-CQI according to UE capabilities. When reportQuantity = cri-RI-PMI-CQI, PMI report from the UE shall be ignored by 5G-L2-PS. The precoding matrix corresponding to the reported rank is determined by the selected Open Loop scheme at 5G-L1-DL.

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.3.0-3 Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank Precoder settings (8Tx transmissions) (ID: 11139457)

**3.9.1.2.1.3.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `12789391`)

Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank When the cell has dlMimoMode is ( CL 8x4 MIMO [CB008577-B] or CL 32x4 MIMO [End CB008577-B] ) and for UEs with 8 port CSI-RS configured:

If there no valid CSI report, refers to [11139277: Default precoder settings](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

For initial Tx: The number of layers for a given UE transmission shall be selected as the latest RI decoded at 5G-L1-UL from CSI report.

Note: For transmission and retransmission via subband beams, the precoding matrix is not needed as 5G_UP_ALG_13751_replaced([11156407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0Le_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Reported rank is used with some latency as 5G_UP_ALG_21414_replaced([11156886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

If force rank 1 is used in forced dci format scenario, which means the reported CSI for this UE is not out of date but scheduler need to use rank 1 which is different from CSI report (5G_UP_ALG_8181_replaced([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_16216_replaced([11178050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuzvjPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the precoding matrix is set the same as default precoding for rank1 [CB008577-B] if dlMimoMode is CL8x4. If dlMimoMode is CL32x4, refer to general handling in [11139510: Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krn4ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB008577-B], and the patternID is selected as the best beam from the latest PMI decoded from CSI report. NOTE: the latest PMI from report only limits to the new report with has same rank as the old report when initial transmission happens, this is for software convenience.

[CB008577-B] If dlMimoMode is CL8x4: [End CB008577-B] port selection of rank 2 enabling or not refers to: 

  * If NIDD:actDlMuMimo is true ([11112211: TDD: Two beams from CSI feedback](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) or.

  * If NIDD:dlSrsBm is true ([11112223: Two beams from SRS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).




[CB008577-B]else if dlMimoMode is CL32x4:

\- If rdPortSelectionCL32x4 ([12805307: rdPortSelectionCL32x4](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XSTs8J9LEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is true, then Port selection for rank 2 shall be applied.

end

[End CB008577-B]

The precoding matrix and patternID are selected as the latest PMI decoded at 5G-L1-UL from CSI report.

For ReTx

The number of layers for a given UE on a HARQ retransmission shall be selected as the number of layers of the first transmission for the current HARQ process.

The precoding matrix and patternID is selected as the latest decoded PMI indicating the same number of layers as the first transmission for the current HARQ process. Note reTx will try to beams of the same type as initial Tx first for implementation convenience. [CB008577-B] If there is no valid CSI report for reTx scheduling, the same precoding matrix and patternID as initial Tx shall be used. [End CB008577-B]

If actDlSrsBm is true and dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO, both 4 and 8 ports CSI-RS/precoding coexist in the cell.

L2 shall set precoding and spatial mode for all kind of PDSCH, either RA-Msg2, RA-Msg4, SRB0, or any transmission until the UE dedicated configuration is activated (5G_UP_ALG_18227_replaced([11153313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) including the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration, paging/SI or normal PDSCH according to 5G_UP_ALG_3171_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.9.1.2.1.3.0-4 Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank Precoder settings (32Tx transmissions) (ID: 11139487)

**3.9.1.2.1.3.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12789389`)

Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank The requirement applies for UEs with 32 ports-CSI-RS configured. Transient phase between User modification of number of ports refers to [11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

If there no valid CSI report for initial Tx, refers to [11139277: Default precoder settings](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

If rdPortSelectionCL32x4 ([12805307: rdPortSelectionCL32x4](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XSTs8J9LEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is true, then Port selection for rank 2 shall be applied.

The number of layers for a given UE's PDSCH shall be selected as the latest RI decoded at 5G-L1-UL from CSI report.

If force rank 1 is used in forced dci format scenario, which means the reported CSI for this UE is not out of date but scheduler needs to use rank 1 which is different from CSI report (5G_UP_ALG_8181_replaced([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_16216_replaced([11178050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuzvjPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the precoding matrix refer to general handling in [11139510: Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krn4ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), and the patternID is selected as the best beam from the latest PMI decoded from CSI report. NOTE: the latest PMI from report only limits to the new report with has same rank as the old report when initial transmission happens, this is for software convenience.

The precoding matrix and patternID are selected as the latest PMI decoded at 5G-L1-UL from CSI report. i2 from CSI feedback shall be used to decide precoding matrix.

For ReTx:

The number of layers for a given UE on a HARQ retransmission shall be selected as the number of layers of the first transmission for the current HARQ process.

The precoding matrix and patternID is selected as the latest decoded PMI indicating the same number of layers as the initial transmission for the current HARQ process. Note reTx will try to beams of the same type as initial Tx first for implementation convenience. If there is no valid CSI report for reTx scheduling, same precoding matrix and patternID as initial Tx shall be used.

---

##### 3.9.1.2.1.4 Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank

###### 3.9.1.2.1.4.0-1 Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank (ID: 11139510)

**3.9.1.2.1.4.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `12789609`)

Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank If NIDD NRCELL/actDlRankAdpAndSRB1McsLimDurHO is set to TRUE, upon reception of the LoCtrl_DlBufferStatusInd with rrcAction set as "RRCReconfigHo" or PsUser_UserSuspendSchedulingReq message with ueSuspendCause set as "_HO_intra_du" or "_ HO_others" or "_HO_with_ExtScell_ _", in order to increase the reliability of SRB1 transmission to the UE, the rank degradation below shall be performed for the initial SRB1 transmission. In case PsUser_UserResumeSchedulingReq is received, the rank degradation below shall not be performed for the initial SRB1 transmission. Detailed precoding refers to general handling below._ ****

  * For FDD or TDD FR1, L2-PS shall degrade the initial SRB1 transmission at rank 2 to rank 1.
  * For FDD or TDD FR1, L2-PS shall degrade the initial SRB1 transmission at rank 3 or rank 4 to rank 2.



A transmission with, [SRB1/SRB2 (if actDlForceRankDowng is set to dlSrbOnly/dlVoNRSrbVoNRCtrl **/dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrNonGbrBr) or** 5QI5/69 (if actDlForceRankDowng is set to dlVoNRCtrlOnly/ dlVoNRSrbVoNRCtrl /dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrNonGbrBr)****

data, shall be rank downgraded and PMI is calculated as

  * For FDD or TDD FR1, L2-PS shall downgrade the SRB1/SRB2/5QI5/5QI69 transmission at rank 2 to rank 1.
  * For FDD or TDD FR1, L2-PS shall downgrade the SRB1/SRB2/5QI5/5QI69 transmission at rank 3 or rank 4 to rank 2.



with detailed precoding refers to general handling below.

If actDlForceRankDowng is set to dlNonGbrBrOnly(applicable for FDD only) or dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrNonGbrBr, and configured with only non-GBR bearer with basic reliability (IMS for 5QI-5 is included), L2PS will initiate a rank downgrade for downlink transmission **with non-GBR data**(and without SRB1/SRB2/5QI5/5QI1 data) **at rank X (where X can be 1, 2, 3, or 4) if the following criteria are met:** ****

 The corrected CQI is below rdLowCqiThresholdRankX.

 The BLER exceeds shortTermBlerThreshold1.

The rank downgrade will continue until the following exit conditions are satisfied:

 The corrected CQI exceeds rdHighCqiThresholdRankX.

 The BLER falls below shortTermBlerThreshold2.

The BLER check shall be skipped if shortTermBlerThreshold1 or shortTermBlerThreshold2 is set to 0. L2PS shall perform rank downgrade as follows:

 rank 2 to rank 1: refers to general handling below.

 rank 3 or rank 4 to rank 2:

  * In case of UE transmission at closed loop precoding based on 8 ports [CB008577-B] or 32 ports [End CB008577-B], the PMI value i11,i12,i13,i2 shall not be changed. port selection (5G_UP_ALG_12747_replaced([11139457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krnRmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for PDSCH rank 2 shall be adopted [CB008577-B] without impact by rdPortSelectionCL32x4 ([12805307: rdPortSelectionCL32x4](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XSTs8J9LEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).[End CB008577-B]..

  * In case of UE transmission at closed loop 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO, the PMI value i1,1 and i2 shall not be changed. i1,3 shall be set as follows:




If rdI13SelectForRankDown, referring to 5G_UP_ALG_31818_replaced([11141851](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), is true:

i1,3(rank2) = i1,3 (rank4 or rank3) +1

Rationale: This approach preserves the mapping of i1,3 reported by the UE to the values of k1, k2 as per comparison of 38.214 tables 5.2.2.2.1-3 and 5.2.2.2.1-4

else:

i1,3 = 0

Note: 1) i11,i12,i13,i2 here mean precoding info in UCI bit, exact indication to L1 refer to EFS. 2) For ReTx, if reported rank changes after initial Tx, latest PMI info may not be used in reTx for simplicity. For ReTx, if report rank does not change after initial Tx, latest PMI info is used.

General handling for above cases:

  * For FDD or TDD FR1, when downgrade from rank 2 to rank 1.



**\- In case of UE transmission** at closed loop precoding based on 8 ports [CB008577-B] or 32 ports [End CB008577-B], the PMI value i11,i12,i13,i2 shall not be changed.****

  * In case of UE transmission **at closed loop precoding based on 4 ports, the PMI value i1,1 and i2 shall not be changed.**

  * In case of closed loop 2x2 MIMO, codebookIndex shall not be changed.

  * For FDD or TDD FR1, when downgrade from rank 3 or rank 4 to rank 2.




**\- In case of UE transmission** at closed loop precoding based on 8 ports [CB008577-B] or 32 ports [End CB008577-B], the PMI value i11,i12,i13,i2 shall not be changed. port selection (5G_UP_ALG_12747_replaced([11139457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krnRmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for PDSCH rank 2 shall be adopted [CB008577-B] without impact by rdPortSelectionCL32x4 (**[12805307: rdPortSelectionCL32x4](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XSTs8J9LEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).[End CB008577-B].**

  * In case of UE transmission **at closed loop 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO, the PMI value i1,1 and i2 shall not be changed, i1,3 shall be set to 0.**



If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True and rank adaption is enabled, for UEs which are applied with rank downgrade, the precoding codebook index for PDSCH (rank 2) shall be selected from the mapping table between codebook index and i2 bits in PMI report. For more information, please refer to in 5G_UP_ALG_7563_replaced([11142677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5ldPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

R&D parameter definitions:

rdLowCqiThresholdRank1 [5G_UP_ALG_31518_replaced([11139047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krkOQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

rdLowCqiThresholdRank2 [5G_UP_ALG_31522_replaced([11139057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krkORPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

rdLowCqiThresholdRank3 [5G_UP_ALG_31525_replaced([11139066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krkORvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

rdLowCqiThresholdRank4 [5G_UP_ALG_31527_replaced([11139078](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krkOSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

rdHighCqiThresholdRank1 [5G_UP_ALG_31529_replaced([11139089](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krkOSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

rdHighCqiThresholdRank2 [5G_UP_ALG_31531_replaced([11139101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krkOTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

rdHighCqiThresholdRank3 [5G_UP_ALG_31533_replaced([11139110](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krkOTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

rdHighCqiThresholdRank4 [5G_UP_ALG_31535_replaced([11139119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krk1UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

###### 3.9.1.2.1.4.0-2 Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank Precoding matrix selection with Forced Rank 1 and Max MCS (ID: 11139539)

**3.9.1.2.1.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12827510`)

Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank If (actDlVoNRLimMaxMcsAndLayer is set to TRUE) OR (actDlForceRankDowng is set to dlVoNROnly)

 a transmission with 5QI1/65/66 traffic shall use a forced rank 1 transmission whose PMI is calculated as below;

OR

If (actDlForceRankDowng is set to dlVoNRSrbVoNRCtrl /dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrNonGbrBr)

 a transmission with 5QI1/65/66 traffic (and without SRB1/SRB2/5QI5/5QI69) shall use a forced rank 1 transmission whose PMI is calculated as below; 

rank 1

  * The PMI shall remain unchanged.



rank 2 to rank 1

[Before CB008577-B] 

  * In case of closed loop 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO, the PMI value i1,1 and i2 shall not be changed.

  * In case of closed loop 2x2 MIMO, codebook index shall not be changed.

  * In case of closed loop 8x4 MIMO, the PMI value i11, i12, i13, i2 shall not be changed. Existing conversion rules from i2 to codebook index applies.




[CB008577-B] refer to general handling in [11139510: Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krn4ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[End CB008577-B]

rank 3 or rank 4 to rank 1

[Before CB008577-B]- In case of closed loop 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO, the PMI value i1,1 and i2 shall not be changed, i1,3 shall be set to 0.

  * In case of closed loop 8x4 MIMO, the PMI value i11, i12, i13, i2 shall not be changed. Existing conversion rules from i2 to codebook index applies.



[CB008577-B] refer to general handling in [11139510: Precoding matrix selection with adaptive rank](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krn4ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[End CB008577-B]

Notes:

  * VoNR rank and MCS restriction algorithm activation flag value is derived from NRCELL.tmpActFeat1.bit13 in 22R2 through 22R3 and NRBTS/NRCELL.actDlVoNrLimMaxMcsAndLayer in 22R4 and onwards.

##### 3.9.1.2.1.5 Precoding options

###### 3.9.1.2.1.5.0-1 Precoding options (ID: 11139560)

**3.9.1.2.1.5.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11139578`)

Precoding options When (NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode is 2x2 or CL 8x4 [CB008577-B] or CL 32x4 [End CB008577-B] MIMO) or (actBeamforming is False) or (numOfSubSectors == 2 or 4), the pdschPrecodingOption4X4, which is sent to L1, shall be set to 0 (not used).

**When NRBTS/dlMimoMode is 4x4 or 4x2 (open loop or closed loop), how to set value of pdschPrecodingOption4X4, which is sent to L1, is defined by below requirements:**

When NIDD NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode indicates Closed Loop. the parameter rdPdschPrecodingOption4X4 (cf. RG 5G_L2_6956_replaced([11186551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276js_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **indicates whether original Type I precoding matrix is used or not:**

  * if 0, it means original Type I precoding matrix from 3GPP is used for rank1, rank2, rank3, rank4.

  * if 1, it means Type I with Port Selection up to rank2. Port selection precoding matrix is used for rank1, rank2. Original type I precoding matrix is used for rank3, rank4.

  * if 2, it means Type I with Port Selection up to rank4. Port selection precoding matrix is chosen for rank1, rank2, rank3, rank4.




The proposed precoding matrices are described in [https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:b:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC0400-5GC0599/5GC000531_5GC000605%20-%20DL%202x2_4x4%20SU%20MIMO/Beamforming_and_codeBookTypes/CodeBookTypeI_PortSelection-v0.7.pdf?csf=1&e=UzOPZJ](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:b:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC0400-5GC0599/5GC000531_5GC000605%20-%20DL%202x2_4x4%20SU%20MIMO/Beamforming_and_codeBookTypes/CodeBookTypeI_PortSelection-v0.7.pdf?csf=1&e=UzOPZJ)

When NIDD NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode indicates Open Loop, the parameter rdPdschPrecodingOption4X4 is also used to **indicate whether original Open Loop precoding matrix is used or not.**

  * if 0, it means original Open Loop precoding matrix is used for rank1, rank2, rank3, rank4. According to the selected Open Loop scheme at 5G-L1-DL please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_358_replaced([11097353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km3UePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))， 5G_UP_ALG_372_replaced([11097420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km37h_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_344_replaced([11097224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km2GXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * if 1, it means Open Loop Port Selection up to rank2. Port selection precoding matrix is used for rank1, rank2 (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_427_replaced([11097960](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km6-0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Original Open Loop precoding matrix is used for rank3, rank4.

  * if 2, it means Open Loop with Port Selection up to rank4. Port selection precoding matrix is chosen for rank1, rank2, rank3, rank4 (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_427_replaced([11097960](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km6-0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))




For both closed loop and open loop, pdschPrecodingOption4X4, which is sent to L1, shall be calculated as below:

  * pdschPrecodingOption4X4 = (rdPdschPrecodingOption4X4 + 4 x rdCSIRSprecoding4X4).



If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True, pdschPrecodingOption4X4 = 2.

**[CB013442-D]**

  * If rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), pdschPrecodingOption4X4 **= 0.**



**[End CB013442-D]**

**[Before CB008577-B]**[CB008577-A] If the cell has FDD beamforming enabled ([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): pdschPrecodingOption4X4 **= 0. Note WA as asked by EFS. [End CB008577-A]**[End CB008577-B]**_*_** *

When dlMimoMode equals 4x4 or 4x2 CL/OL SU MIMO, for non-beamforming mode (5G_UP_908_replaced([11353388](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hUPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and supercell mode (5G_UP_5548_replaced([11353423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hVvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), refers to 5G_UP_ALG_3183_replaced([11139297](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.9.1.2.2 Open loop scheme selection

##### 3.9.1.2.2.0-1 Open loop scheme selection Precoding scheme for Open Loop (ID: 11139618)

**3.9.1.2.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11139629`)

Open loop scheme selection The precoding scheme for Open Loop is chosen at 5G-L2-PS and indicated to 5G-L1-DL through the PDSCHSendRequest message (5G_UP_ALG_3200_replaced([11139612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kroftfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Except for artificial PDSCH load (5G_UP_ALG_3193_replaced([11183902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_O_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_1816_replaced([11212192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-joCvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and conformance tests (5G_L2_1749_replaced([11210085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-aeGfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the precoding shall depend on :

  * PDSCHSendRequest parameter SpatialMode (5G_UP_ALG_14007_replaced([11098058](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km7l5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * NIDD parameters NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme

  * NIDD parameters NRBTS/NRCELL.dlMimoMode

  * beamforming mode or no beamforming mode or subsectorization mode or [CB009543-A] TDD [End CB009543-A] supercell mode, see 5G_UP_ALG_2183_replaced([11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_907_replaced([11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))




If SpatialMode is set to "open loop spatial multiplexing"

If NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "No Precoding" or "SCDD" or "LCDD"

The precoding is cell-specific.

PDSCHSendRequest.openLoopScheme = NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme

else if NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "Automatic"

The precoding is cell-specific.

cf. 5G_UP_ALG_3203_replaced([11139635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krofufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

else if NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "Dynamic"

The precoding is UE-specific.

cf. 5G_UP_ALG_3204_replaced([11139648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krofu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

else ( i.e. value DISABLED)

PDSCHSendRequest.openLoopScheme = "No Precoding" . (cell-specific : cf. Note)

else

PDSCHSendRequest.openLoopScheme = INVALID

Note: Corresponds to dlMimoMode= closed loop and spatialMode = open loop. Currently does not happen. Relation between SpatialMode and NRBTS/NRCELL.dlMimoMode is given in 5G_UP_ALG_3171_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.9.1.2.2.0-2 Open loop scheme selection NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "Automatic" (ID: 11139635)

**3.9.1.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11139642`)

Open loop scheme selection This requirement is related to 5G_UP_ALG_3202_replaced([11139618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kroftvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "Automatic"

If NRBTS/NRCELL.dlMimoMode = "2x2 Open Loop Spatial Multiplexing"

PDSCHSendRequest.openLoopScheme = LCDD

If NRBTS/NRCELL.dlMimoMode = "4x4 or 4x2 Open Loop Spatial Multiplexing"

PDSCHSendRequest.openLoopScheme = SCDD

When NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "Automatic", PDSCHSendRequest.openLoopScheme is the same for all UEs, all slots of a given subcell.

---

##### 3.9.1.2.2.0-3 Open loop scheme selection NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "Dynamic" (ID: 11139648)

**3.9.1.2.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12730171`)

Open loop scheme selection This requirement is related to 5G_UP_ALG_3202_replaced([11139618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kroftvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "Dynamic" (L1 HW allowed is handled through PDL rules).

If NRBTS/NRCELL.dlMimoMode = "2x2 Open Loop Spatial Multiplexing"

PDSCHSendRequest.openLoopScheme = LCDD

If NRBTS/NRCELL.dlMimoMode = "4x4 or 4x2 Open Loop Spatial Multiplexing"

|  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
| No beamforming mode or subsectorization mode **or supercell mode,** see 5G_UP_ALG_2183_replaced([11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_907_replaced([11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |  |  | Beamforming mode, see 5G_UP_ALG_2183_replaced([11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_907_replaced([11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |  |   
Rank and MCS | Rank 1,2 | Rank3,4 MCS < threshold | Rank3,4 MCS>=threshold | Rank 1,2 | Rank3,4 MCS < threshold | Rank3,4 MCS>=threshold  
Open Loop Precoding | SCDD | SCDD | No Precoding | SCDD | SCDD | SCDD  
  
When NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme= "Dynamic", 

PDSCHSendRequest.openLoopScheme is different accross UEs, and accross slots for a given UE.

MCS thresholds are determined via r&d parameters:

  * rdStartMcsNoPrecodingTable64QAM is defined in 5G_L2_1317_replaced([11184244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27peAfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * rdStartMcsNoPrecodingTable256QAM is defined in 5G_L2_1318_replaced([11184247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27peA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




[CB008949-A]

  * rdStartMcsNoPrecodingTable1024QAM is defined in [12730161: rdStartMcsNoprecodingTable1024Qam](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Uc6JA3KcEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw).



[End CB008949-A]

Appropriate power backoff value is specified in [Before CB008949-A] 5G_UP_ALG_2563_replaced([11118462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB008949-A][11118372: Overview of power setting for PDSCH](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_U5RwUPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) [End CB008949-A].
