### 3.9.1.3 Low PAPR optimized precoding

#### 3.9.1.3.0-1 Low PAPR optimized precoding How to enable low PAPR optimized precoding (ID: 11139664)

**3.9.1.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11139668`)

Low PAPR optimized precoding 5G-L2-PS shall indicate to 5G-L1-DL that Low PAPR optimized precoding is enabled on DL transmission basis. Therefore, it will be possible to disable the functionality for specific DL transmissions (or UEs) whenever needed.

Until any issue is reported for some configuration (e.g. rel16 DMRS sequence generation in DMRS-DownlinkConfig), the functionality shall be enabled for all UEs based on NIDD parameter actDlLowPAPRoptimizedPrecoding and rdDlLowPAPRoptimizedPrecodingWithPdschRateMatching (5G_L2_1458_replaced([11186448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2758oPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When actDlLowPAPRoptimizedPrecoding is true:

  * the value 1 of rdDlLowPAPRoptimizedPrecodingWithPdschRateMatching, the functionality shall be enabled without PDSCH rate matching check.

  * the value 0 of rdDlLowPAPRoptimizedPrecodingWithPdschRateMatching, the functionnality is disabled on the slots with PDSCH rate matching with LTE CRS or TRS.




Until performance issue is seen with PDSCH rate matching (e.g. with LTE CRS), defaut value of rdDlLowPAPRoptimizedPrecodingWithPdschRateMatching is 1. In case performance issue is observed, default value of rdDlLowPAPRoptimizedPrecodingWithPdschRateMatching shall be changed to 0.

Note: Rel16 DMRS sequence generation in DMRS-DownlinkConfig is not expected before 24R4.

---

#### 3.9.1.3.0-2 Low PAPR optimized precoding Bundling size information (ID: 11139675)

**3.9.1.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11139681`)

Low PAPR optimized precoding When Low PAPR optimized precoding fucntionality is enabled, PRB bundling size used by gNB is explained in 5G_UP_1078_replaced([11354876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucMVoPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR673677] Note: PRB bundling size follows exact same rules with or without Artificial load. [End PR673677]

---

### 3.9.1.4 Rank Adaptation

##### 3.9.1.4.1 Rank Adaptation for rank3/4

###### 3.9.1.4.1.0-1 Rank Adaptation for rank3/4 Overall concept (ID: 11139697)

**3.9.1.4.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11139707`)

Rank Adaptation for rank3/4 [Before CNI-110468] In order to improve DL performance on the field, in real radio conditions, gNB should be able to perform a rank adaptation in case of 4x4 or 4x2 Open Loop dlMimoMode. When rank adaptation is enabled (rd4x4MimoRAEnabled is True), DL scheduler should follow the RI received from the UE in the CSI report in case of rank 1,2 and 4, while in case of rank 3 DL scheduler should follow the rank computed by the rank adaptation algorithm. [End CNI-110468]

---

###### 3.9.1.4.1.0-2 Rank Adaptation for rank3/4 Algorithm (ID: 11139713)

**3.9.1.4.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11139723`)

Rank Adaptation for rank3/4 [Before CNI-110468] The purpose of rank adaptation is to force rank 4 used by the DL scheduler in case the UE reports RI 3 and several conditions are accomplished when receiving a new CSI report for channel measurements, as described bellow:

-CQI reported by the UE is higher or equal than rdLayer4CqiThreshold;

-if previous rank used by the DL scheduler for this UE was 4, current rrmDeltaCQI computed by DL OLLA is higher or equal than rdLayer4DeltaCqiThreshold;

-if previous rank used by the DL scheduler for this UE was 3, current rrmDeltaCQI computed by DL OLLA is higher or equal than rdLayer3DeltaCqiThreshold;

-current rrmDeltaCQI computed by DL OLLA is not too old (rrmDeltaCQI should have been updated during last CSI report period);

When rank adaptation detects a rank force from 3 layers to 4 layers, the CQI value used by DL ILLA should be reduced with an offset equal to rdRank3CqiOffset to follow the channel's spectral efficiency computed by the UE.

When conditions are not accomplished and rank adaptation decides to use the same rank as the one received from the UE, CQI value reported by the UE should be used by DL ILLA.

As radio conditions can change dramatically between two CSI reports for channel measurements, in case of rank force the rank adaptation algorithm should check before each scheduling that rrmDeltaCQI has not decreased beyond the threshold that is checked in the initial condition; in case if did, rank adaptation should switch from rank 4 to rank 3, following the RI requested by the UE. [End CNI-110468]

---

#### 3.9.1.4.2 Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch

##### 3.9.1.4.2.0-1 Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch Overview for switch block (ID: 11139737)

**3.9.1.4.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11139741`)

Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch For TDD FR1 with beamforming and basic reliable DRB(not including URLLC), in case of **NRCELL/actInterRankSwitchBlock is TRUE, the following shall be followed.**

When the number of layers which reported by the UE is changed, the UE will filter the channel estimation result, but that maybe cause the BLER increased. During the rank decreasing, the higher MCS is used, and if the code rate > 0.8 it will seriously impact the LDPC coding. So it is necessary to improve the accuracy of reduction of rank in DL based on UE's Rank Indication at a high MCS, and the switch blocking mechanism is introduced which is based on observed deltaCQI and BLER when a reduction of rank is reported.

[PR830179] Upon exiting rank switch blocking, the gNB will use the restored RI related CQI to update the average CQI. [END PR830179]

During the rank increasing, when gNB-DU receives the report from UE side, just perform the propose MCS switch based on the MCS mapping table.

If the new rank report is two steps lower, just perform the new reported rank and the proposed MCS directly.

---

##### 3.9.1.4.2.0-2 Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch Rank decreasing scenarios (ID: 11139747)

**3.9.1.4.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11139752`)

Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch The gNB shall block the RANK switch in case of the following conditions are met:

  1. The BLER is valid (the samples of new HARQ initial TX > rdInterRankSwitchBlockMinInitTx (5G_UP_ALG_23910_replaced([11141708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) and lower than the threshold (5G_UP_ALG_23891_replaced([11139800](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpt2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), AND

  2. The Observing DeltaCQI is higher than the threshold (5G_UP_ALG_23889_replaced([11139778](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpt1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND

  3. the hysteresis timer (5G_UP_ALG_23887_replaced([11139769](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpt1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not expired




gNB shall replace the reported rank from UE with the rank gNB proposed. The other functionality assumes gNB received proposed rank from UE.

---

##### 3.9.1.4.2.0-3 Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch MCS threshold for the Rank decreasing (ID: 11139757)

**3.9.1.4.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11139762`)

Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch The MCS threshold for rank4 is as the following table:

|  |   
---|---|---  
Rank | MCS threshold for block Rank low risk | MCS threshold for block Rank High risk  
4 | NRCELL/interRankSwitchBlockThresholds/rankSwitchBlockMcsThres1 | NRCELL/interRankSwitchBlockThresholds/rankSwitchBlockMcsThres2  
  
The above MCS thresholds are:

 If the propose MCS >= MCS threshold for block Rank low risk, it means the rank decreasing possibility reported from UE is highly wrong, and the risk of blocking the rank decreasing is low, so need to observe a long period BLER to decide the rank decreasing or not.

 If the propose MCS range is between MCS threshold for block rank low risk and high risk, it means the rank decreasing reported from UE is possibly wrong, and the risk of blocking the rank decreasing is high, so need to observe a short period BLER to decide the rank decreasing or not to prevent even worse BLER.

Note: If the rank reported from UE is wrong, then we have no risk to ignore the new rank since we use the right rank. But if the new decreased rank is right, then it's high risk if we ignore it and use the old higher rank, It will cause NACK storm.

---

##### 3.9.1.4.2.0-4 Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch Hysteresis timer for the Rank decreasing (ID: 11139769)

**3.9.1.4.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13371922`)

Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch Hysteresis timer is introduced to avoid the absence of OLLA feedback or BLER due to there is not enough initial HARQ TX during the observing duration, and wrongly perform the block of the rank decreasing via CSI report from UE.

In case of there is few initial DL HARQ, before the timer expired, then the lower rank is directly used.

The timer is started in the case of:

 When new rank report has one step down and current propose MCS for the old rank >= MCS threshold for block Rank Low risk, then timer started with interval set to rdInterRankSwitchBlockLowRiskTimerDuration (5G_UP_ALG_23906_replaced([11141678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 When new rank report have one step down. And current propose MCS for the old ranks is between MCS threshold for block Rank Low risk and high risk, then timer started with interval set to rdInterRankSwitchBlockHighRiskTimerDuration (5G_UP_ALG_23908_replaced([11141693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The Timer is stopped in the case of:

  * When the timer is running, if current new HARQ initial TX number > rdInterRankSwitchBlockMinInitTx(5G_UP_ALG_23910_replaced([11141708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  * The deltaCQI dropped below rankSwitchCqiThreshold - rrmAvgCqi and then perform the rank switch.
  * [PR868166]For subband BF, a rank of RANK3 computed by L1 overrides RANK4.[End PR868166]



When the timer is expired, gNB-DU shall perform the rank decreasing but not blocking the new CQI report.

---

##### 3.9.1.4.2.0-5 Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch Delta CQI Observing (ID: 11139778)

**3.9.1.4.2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11139795`)

Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch 11139795: Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch The delta CQI observing is used to protect NACK storming due to the block of rank switch during the rank blocking period (still use the previous rank). The condition is as following: [image-0][image_desc]The image contains the following text: rnnAvgCqj + rnnDeltaCqj <= rankSwitchCqjThreshold[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_8591.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] where rankSwitchCqiThreshold is required CQI with previous rank based on rankSwitchBlockMcsThres2 which are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_23885_replaced([11139757](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpt0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CNI-110468, CB012783] If NIDD: actDlRankProbing is true and Rank switch is blocked, rdCqiJitterDl (defined in 5G_UP_ALG_17571_replaced([11138437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kreuvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), used in 5G_UP_ALG_7557_replaced([11125689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall use 0 for this UE's LA. [End CNI-110468, CB012783]

---

##### 3.9.1.4.2.0-6 Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch Short term BLER Computation (ID: 11139800)

**3.9.1.4.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11139805`)

Block of Unnecessary Inter Rank Switch BLER shall to be introduced here to prevent the delta CQI not updated in case of there is not enough data in DL but the MCS decreasing performed. It’s to evaluate whether the block of rank switch is right or not.

When the initial TX number > rdInterRankSwitchBlockMinInitTx(5G_UP_ALG_23910_replaced([11141708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), start to evaluate the short term BLER of RANK4 TX.

When the BLER is higher than the threshold as the following table then perform the rank decreasing directly.

The BLER threshold, which depends on the proposed MCS range within MCS threshold of block rank High risk or Low risk, are defined as following:

|  |   
---|---|---  
Rank | Block risk | BLER threshold  
Rank 4 | Low risk | NRCELL/interRankSwitchBlockThresholds/rankSwitchBlockBlerHighThres  
Rank 4 | High risk | NRCELL/interRankSwitchBlockThresholds/rankSwitchBlockBlerLowThres

---

#### 3.9.1.4.3 Rank 4 probing

##### 3.9.1.4.3.0-1 Rank 4 probing Candidate UE for rank4 probing (ID: 11139816)

**3.9.1.4.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12506853`)

Rank 4 probing If NRBTS/NRCELL.actDlRankProbing is true and for UEs that meets the following criteria shall be seen as rank4 probe candidates.

  1. have periodical SRS configured for DL BF, either wideband (5G_UP_ALG_6962_replaced([11155660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) oDFT beam or real time subband BF (5G_UP_ALG_13751_replaced([11156407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0Le_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

  2. not have High Reliability RB configured (5G_UP_5835_replaced([11353136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub9FEPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

  3. not have VoNR [Before CB008118-CB] 5QI1 [CB008118-CB] 5QI1/65/66 [End CB008118-CB] configured for VoNR if NRBTS/NRCELL. actDlVoNrLimMaxMcsAndLayer is true;




Note: The CNI is released to customer via CB012783 with the scope not changed.

---

##### 3.9.1.4.3.0-2 Rank 4 probing Monitoring for rank4 probing (ID: 11139827)

**3.9.1.4.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11139832`)

Rank 4 probing [Before 04050418] If the candidate UE (5G_UP_ALG_25330_replaced([11139816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpt3PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has initial HARQ transimission for PDSCH been scheduled with 1) SRS beam, 2) Rank3, 3) MCS is higher or equal than rdRank4ProbeMcsThreshold (5G_UP_ALG_23132_replaced([11141721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and 4) ack received for this PDSCH,

5G-L2-PS shall increase the contiguous ack counter for this UE,

Else

5G-L2-PS shall reset the contiguous ack counter as 0.

[04050418]

For each candidate UE (5G_UP_ALG_25330_replaced([11139816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpt3PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall track the number and ratio of PDSCH using Rank3 and high MCS (rank3HighMcsScheduling) to the number of PDSCH of this UE over monitoring window.  
1) rank3HighMcsScheduling is defined as PDSCH scheduling with Rank3 and MCS is higher or equal than rdRank4ProbeMcsThreshold (5G_UP_ALG_23132_replaced([11141721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  
2) The length of each monitoring window equals to max{160slot, CQI report periodicity}. It is known the window length may varies due to variable latency for gNB-DU handling the CSI report.  
3) PDSCH that fit either one of following conditions are skipped from the monitor here:  
a) PDSCH not via SRS beam  
b) re-transmission  
c) MCS is downgrade according to 5G_UP_ALG_3060_replaced([11129299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq78IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) point 5 or low buffer according to 5G_UP_ALG_4630_replaced([11192270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvjWafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  
d) The average corrected CQI is adapted (see 5G_UP_ALG_3012_replaced([11126056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqwV9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for slots with high BLER according to 5G_UP_ALG_3060_replaced([11129299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq78IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) point 10

e) Fake DAI scheduling 5G_UP_ALG_3060_replaced([11129299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq78IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) point 11

Note: The above counters/ratios are reset when UE reported rank is not rank3.

Note: periodic CSI report and aperiodic CSI report is handled in the same way.

[End 04050418]

Where SRS beam is oDFT beam or real time subband (RT) beam and RT beam fallback to oDFT beam will not reset the counter.

---

##### 3.9.1.4.3.0-3 Rank 4 probing Rank4 Change (ID: 11139837)

**3.9.1.4.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11139842`)

Rank 4 probing [Before 04050418]

If the candidate UE (5G_UP_ALG_23132_replaced([11141721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has valid CSI report with rank3 for channel acquisition received and the contiguous ack counter is larger than rdNumOfContiguousAckThreshold (5G_UP_ALG_25332_replaced([11141736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and last PDSCH scheduling has valid SRS beam indicated and SRS beam is still valid (5G_UP_ALG_22213_replaced([11139827](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpt3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,

[04050418]

If the candidate UE (5G_UP_ALG_23132_replaced([11141721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has all the following criteria met,

1) number of rank3HighMcsScheduling is higher than rdNumOfSchedulingThreshold(5G_UP_ALG_25332_replaced([11141736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and ratio of rank3HighMcsScheduling is higher than 90%.

2) The HARQ ACK ratio of rank3HighMcsScheduling scheduling is larger than 99%

3) The UE has valid CSI report and latest reported CQI is larger than 10

4) The latest PDSCH scheduling has valid SRS beam indicated and SRS beam is still valid (5G_UP_ALG_22213_replaced([11139827](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpt3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  
5) The MCS used by the latest PDSCH scheduling(excluding skipping slot and MU scheduling) is higher or equal than rdRank4ProbeMcsThreshold.

[End 04050418]

gNB-DU shall:

1) replace the reported rank3 as rank4.

2) Closed loop precoding matrix: Either for UEs with 4 or 8 ports CSI-RS configured, precoding matrix shall be decided for rank4 as the same i1,1 and i2 as UE reported one for rank3. 8 ports CSI-RS only needs i2.

Open loop precoding matrix: precoding matrix for rank 4 is decided as legacy scheme(5G_UP_ALG_3200_replaced([11139612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kroftfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))..

3) CQI shall be replaced with one value that has mapped MCS near to MCS:NRCELL/interRankSwitchBlockThresholds rankSwitchBlockMcsThres1.

4) If the UE has 8 ports CSI-RS being configured, the PMI beam shall be updated according to UE reported rank3. In this case when SRS beam changes to invalid, PMI beam with rank3 is still there.

5) rdCqiJitterDl (defined in 5G_UP_ALG_17571_replaced([11138437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kreuvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), used in 5G_UP_ALG_7557_replaced([11125689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall use 0 for this UE's LA.

---

## 3.9.2 UL SU-MIMO

#### 3.9.2.1 Transmission scheme on PUSCH w/ SRS configured

##### 3.9.2.1.0-1 Transmission scheme on PUSCH w/ SRS configured PUSCH scheduled with DCI scrambled with C-RNTI or CS-RNTI (ID: 11139858)

**3.9.2.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11139870`)

Transmission scheme on PUSCH w/ SRS configured PUSCH scheduled with DCI scrambled with C-RNTI shall be scheduled with spatial multiplexing over 2 antenna ports.

[CB008124-B] PUSCH scheduled with DCI scrambled with CS-RNTI for configured grant type2 activation shall be scheduled with spatial multiplexing over 2 antenna ports [End CB008124-B]

The rank and PMI to use is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3223_replaced([11139902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When the number of layers is 1 , the DMRS antenna port is 0. When the number of layers is 2, if the number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data is 1, the UL DMRS antenna ports are (0,1), otherwise, the used UL DMRS antenna ports (0,1) or (0,2) are determined following rdUlAntennaPortFlagForTwoLayersDynamicRIPMI [5G_L2_1082_replaced([11186568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276jtvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]. Please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_975_replaced([11103235](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kntpAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_977_replaced([11103246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kntpBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_979_replaced([11103258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kntpFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for illustration about UL antenna ports before and after precoding.

Three cases have to be distinguished depending on nrofSrsPorts (see 5G_CP_IF_RRC_5360_replaced([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the SRS resource with srsResourceId 0:

  * If nrofSrsPorts is 1, then PUSCH shall be scheduled with DCI format 0_1 over one antenna port with antenna port 1000. The DCI field "Precoding information and number of layers" has 0-bit length because higher layer parameter "ulTxConfig" set to "Codebook" (see chapter 7.3.1.1.2 in TS 38.212). The DCI field “PTRS-DMRS association” has 0-bit length because the “maxRank” = 1.

  * If nrofSrsPorts is 2, and maxNumOfUlLayers (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2371_replaced([11285102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpvgevvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 1 then PUSCH shall be scheduled with DCI format 0_1 using spatial multiplexing over 2 antenna ports (after precoding) with fixed rank 1. The rank and PMI of UL transmission is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3223_replaced([11139902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The maxNumOfUlLayers is taken into account for all PUSCH C-RNTI [CB008124-B] or CS-RNTI [End CB008124-B] Transmission (for any UL grant following msg3). The DCI field “PTRS-DMRS association” has 0-bit length because the “maxRank” = 1.

  * If nrofSrsPorts is 2, and maxNumOfUlLayers (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2371_replaced([11285102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpvgevvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 2, then PUSCH shall be scheduled with DCI format 0_1 using spatial multiplexing over 2 antenna ports (after precoding) with adaptive rank. The rank and PMI of UL transmission is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3223_replaced([11139902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The maxNumOfUlLayers is taken into account for all PUSCH C-RNTI [CB008124-B] or CS-RNTI [End CB008124-B] Transmission (for any UL grant following msg3).




For a UE having an adaptive number of SRS ports state (see 5G_UP_ALG_6925_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), nrofSrsPorts value depends on this state as expressed in 5G_L2_656_replaced([11164313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25sWIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_12934_replaced([11164357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25sWPPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

A UE having an "adaptive number of SRS ports" state (see 5G_UP_ALG_6925_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and whose state is either "Reconfiguration 1-to-2" or "Reconfiguration 2-to-1" (see 5G_L2_656_replaced([11164313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25sWIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall have PUSCH scheduled with DCI scrambled with C-RNTI and by format 0_0 (see 5G_UP_ALG_3935_replaced([11168314](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktvYg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Then according to TS38.214 section 6.1.1 the PUSCH transmission is based on single antenna port.

And the DM-RS configuration is the one used for DCI 0_0 (see 5G_UP_ALG_235_replaced([11096217](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmtjevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

To make the requirement clear. The table as below defines the bit width of the field 'Precoding information and number of layers' in DCI 0_1 under different cases:

|  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
Bit width | nrofSrsPorts | maxNumOfUlLayers | ul-FullPowerTransmission | Coherent mode | txConfig | Notes  
0 | any | any | Not configured | any | nonCodeBook |   
0 | 1 | any | Not configured | any | codebook |   
2 | 2 | 2 | Not configured or fullpower or fullpowerMode2 | nonCoherent | codebook | See Table 7.3.1.1.2.4;  
2 | 2 | 2 | fullpowerMode1 | nonCoherent | codebook | See table 7.3.1.1.2.4A; MaxRank in PUSCH-Config = 2  
4 | 2 | 2 | Not configured | fullyAndPartialAndNonCoherent | codebook | See Table 7.3.1.1.2.4; MaxRank in PUSCH-Config = 2  
1 | 2 | 1 | Not configured or fullpower or fullpowerMode2 | nonCoherent | codebook | See Table 7.3.1.1.2.5; MaxRank in PUSCH-Config = 1  
2 | 2 | 1 | fullpowerMode1 | nonCoherent | codebook | See table 7.3.1.1.2.5A; MaxRank in PUSCH-Config = 1  
3 | 2 | 1 | Not configured | fullyAndPartialAndNonCoherent | codebook | See Table 7.3.1.1.2.5; MaxRank in PUSCH-Config = 1  
  
In absence of srsResourceId0, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3221_replaced([11139889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.9.2.1.0-2 Transmission scheme on PUSCH w/ SRS configured Precoding information and numbers of layers DCI 0_1 field for Transform Precoding Enabled and SRS Configured (ID: 11139877)

**3.9.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11139882`)

Transmission scheme on PUSCH w/ SRS configured The bit widths supported for DCI 0_1 field Precoding information and numbers of layers shall be per table below when UE is configured for PUSCH Transform Precoding.

|  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
Bit Width | nrofSrsPorts | maxNumOfUlLayers | ul-FullPowerTransmission | Coherent Mode | txConfig | Notes  
0 | any | Any | Not configured | Any | nonCodebook |   
0 | 1 | any | Not configured | any | codebook |   
1 | 2 | 1 | Not configured or fullpower or fullpowerMode2 | nonCoherent | codebook | See 38.212 Table 7.3.1.1.2-5  
2 | 2 | 1 | fullpowerMode1 | nonCoherent | codebook | See 38.212 Table 7.3.1.1.2-5A  
3 | 2 | 1 | Not configured | fullyAndPartialAndNonCoherent | codebook | See 38.212 Table 7.3.1.1.2-5  
  
Notes:

\- Transform Precoding only supports Rank 1

\- In absence of srsResourceId0, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3221_replaced([11139889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- Table above is a subset of table in 5G_UP_ALG_10493_replaced([11139858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), restricted to entries in that table which apply to Transform Precoding

---

#### 3.9.2.2 Transmission scheme on PUSCH w/o SRS configured

##### 3.9.2.2.0-1 Transmission scheme on PUSCH w/o SRS configured In absence of SRS resource with srsResourceId 0 : nrofSrsPorts shall be considered as 1, then PUSCH shall be scheduled with DCI format 0_1 over one antenna port with antenna port 1000. The DCI field "Precoding information and number of layers" has 0-bit length because this case corresponds to higher layer parameter "ulTxConfig" set to "Codebook" (see chapter 7.3.1.1.2 in TS 38.212). The DCI field “PTRS-DMRS association” has 0-bit length because the “maxRank” shall be considered as 1. Notes: Therefore in absence of srsResourceId0 : 5G_UP_ALG_3223_replaced( 11139902 ) does not apply as the UE is always single Tx (no Rank computation), 5G_L2_656_replaced( 11164313 ) does not apply as the UE only 1 SRS port capable is not eligible to SRS port reconfigurations (ID: 11139896)

### 3.9.2.3 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH

#### 3.9.2.3.0-1 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Overview : UL rank compution and resulting PMI rules (ID: 11139906)

**3.9.2.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11139912`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH UL rank compution and resulting PMI rules.

Long Term UL Rank computation

A long term rank for any given UE, rrmUlRiLongTerm, shall be derived as described in 5G_UP_ALG_19663_replaced([11139919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq78PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

rrmUlRiLongTerm computation is amended for UE who has an "adaptive number of SRS ports" state.

Rank selection

How to use rrmUlRiLongTerm to derive rank is described in 5G_UP_ALG_3226_replaced([11139957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq79_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If nrofSrsPorts in the SRS resource with srsResourceId 0 (see 5G_CP_IF_RRC_5360_replaced([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 2, and maxNumOfUlLayers (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2371_replaced([11285102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpvgevvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 1, rrmUlRiLongTerm is forced to 1.

PMI selection and default precoder

PMI selection and default precoder is described in 5G_UP_ALG_3231_replaced([11139991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq7_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The rules are updated when UE capability of pusch-TransCoherence is nonCoherent.

Long period with PUSCH rank1 scheduling and without SRS measurements

These rules are described in 5G_UP_ALG_3232_replaced([11140029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Rules are extended to UE with "adaptive number of SRS ports" state "single Tx" (5G_L2_656_replaced([11164313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25sWIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Update of the rules regarding the timer, thresholds between SINRs and resulting PMIs.

Update of the rules for UEs with pusch-TransCoherence = noncoherent.

---

#### 3.9.2.3.0-2 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Long Term UL Rank computation (ID: 11139919)

**3.9.2.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11139928`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH This requirement applies to 5G_UP_ALG_3224_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

A long term rank for any given UE shall be derived from :

**[CB009849-A]**

If (NRCELL.actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to FALSE**, OR (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND**[Before CB008118-C]5QI1 **[CB008118-C] 5QI1/65/66**[End CB008118-C]DRB is not configured for the UE)**[End CB009849-A]****_*_** *

rrmUlRiLongTerm = rrmUlRiLongTerm * (1 - rdUlRiBeta) + rrmUlRiShortTerm * rdUlRiBeta

**[CB009849-A]**

Else,

If User [Before PR829683] setup/[End PR829683] modification complete **[Before CB008118-C] (to add the first 5QI1 DRB)**[CB008118-C] (to add the first 5QI1/65/66 DRB) **[End CB008118-C] is received (user below defined mechanism to identify the usser modification complete), and current scheduled number of layers is 2, and rrmUlRiLongTerm is not less then ulRank2to1Thresh(defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3226_replaced([11139957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq79_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then reset rrmUlRiLongTerm to ulRank2to1Thresh - rdUlRiBeta. ****[End CB009849-A]****_*_** *

[CB009849-A][PR829683]

User modification complete can be identifed in below 2 ways;

  * When the DL-DCCH is triggered and monitored by the RRC layer, then RRC reconfiguration complete indication from the higher layer. 

  * When DL-DCCH procedure is monitored by the MAC layer, then at the end of the Mac layer monitoring (Refer [11153671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksn-NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), [11153868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) )




[End PR829683] [End CB009849-A]

Where

  * rrmUlRiShortTerm is determined as follows :



**[CB009849-A]If (NRCELL.actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE** ,****

Set rrmUlRiShortTerm as per 5G_UP_ALG_30679_replaced([11139943](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq79fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**[End CB009849-A]**

Else,

**[CB013202-B] If NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.** enhRankSelectSe is true [PR829702-25R3] and UE is not in Transform Precoder Enabled State ( [11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))[End PR829702-25R3],****

Set rrmUlRiShortTerm as per 5G_UP_ALG_30873_replaced([11139935](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq78_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Else,

**[End CB013202-B]**

Set rrmUlRiShortTerm from _UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs and_ UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs **Rank indication** **

  * rdUlRiBeta is defined in 5G_L2_1086_replaced([11186509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2758q_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * Initial value of rrmUlRiLongTerm shall be equal to rdInitialUlRi defined in 5G_L2_3731_replaced([11182981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




Long term averaged value is only updated based on VALID rank indication coming from L1 **[CB013202-B] or from SE check function (5G_UP_ALG_30873_replaced([11139935](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq78_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End CB013202-B]. Update of long term averaged value shall only be done when nonDTX has been received from _UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs or_ UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs **.******* *

For a UE who has an "adaptive number of SRS ports" state (see 5G_UP_ALG_6925_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) rrmUlRiLongTerm keeps the same value as long as the UE "adaptive number of SRS ports" state is either "Reconfiguration 1-to-2" or "Reconfiguration 2-to-1".

For a UE who has an "adaptive number of SRS ports" state, rrmUlRiLongTerm initial value is 1 if initial state is “single Tx” and 2 if initial state is “ulRank 2” (see 5G_UP_ALG_30477_replaced([11157753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks98cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for initial state decision).

-The rank used for the first initial transmission in spatial multiplexing (after initial access in singleTx) shall be 1. Therefore the initial value of rrmUlRiShortTerm shall be 1.

For a UE who has an "adaptive number of SRS ports" state, the rank used for the first initial transmission in spatial multiplexing is 2 and rrmUlRiShortTerm shall be 2 if initial state is “ulRank 2” (see 5G_UP_ALG_30477_replaced([11157753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks98cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for initial state decision).

#### 3.9.2.3.0-3 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Short Term UL Rank Computation (ID: 11139935)

**3.9.2.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11139940`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH If NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectSe is set to True [PR829702-25R3] and UE is not in Transform Precoder Enabled State ( [11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))[End PR829702-25R3], gNB-DU shall determine the Short Term (ST) rank rrmUlRiShortTerm to be used in the long term average (5G_UP_ALG_19663_replaced([11139919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq78PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for 2Tx capable UEs as defined in this requirement.

A) For UEs without adaptive number of SRS ports configuration:

[PR832038] sinr inputs for rank2 are called generically Rank2Sinr_0 and Rank2Sinr_1 in this requirement. [End PR832038]

During rrmUlRiShortTerm determination, input (cf. Note1) depends on scheduled number of layers:

rrmInstSinrRank2= average(Rank2Sinr_0, Rank2Sinr_1), see Note2.

 When PUSCH scheduled number of layers is 1

o rrmInstSinrRank1 is from ulPmiRank1Sinr from UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs

o Rank2Sinr_0 and Rank2Sinr_1 are respectively from ulPmiRank2Sinr[0], ulPmiRank2Sinr[1] from UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs

o ulRank from UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs (or Min over rdNumSrsFreqHops last ulRank measurements from UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs if applicable, cf. Note5).

 When PUSCH scheduled number of layers is 2

o rrmInstSinrRank1 is from ulPmiRank1Sinr from _UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs_

o Rank2Sinr_0 and Rank2Sinr_1 are [Before PR832038] respectively from ulPmiRank2Sinr[0], ulPmiRank2Sinr[1] [PR832038] as per [12631297: Input Rank2 Sinr for PUSCH SE check](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kCNeEDviEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [End PR832038] from UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs

o ulRank are computed from ulRank from _UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs_

The SE check is performed only if all of the following conditions are met (cf. Note1):

 VALID ulRank indication AND nonDTX have been received

 ulPmiRank1Sinr and Rank2Sinr_0 and Rank2Sinr_1 are VALID

 Short term ulPmiRank1Sinr is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 min(Rank2Sinr_0 and Rank2Sinr_1) is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and max(Rank2Sinr_0 and Rank2Sinr_1) is inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 Absolute value of the SINR difference between Rank2Sinr_0 and Rank2Sinr_1 of the 2 layers is strictly inferior to rdUlMaxSinrDiffLayers**(5G_UP_ALG_24307_replaced([11141409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

The SE check algorithm to determine the rrmUlRiShortTerm is as following.

**[CB013202-B-UPD001]**

If ulRank == 2 **[End CB013202-B-UPD001] AND { rrmInstSinrRank2 < rdUlSinrThresForSeCheck) OR (abs(Rank2Sinr_0 - Rank2Sinr_1) > rdSinrGapBetweenLayersThresh [PR832038] AND (rrmInstSinrRank2 < rdUlSinrKeepRank2ThreshForSeCheck) [End PR832038] ) }(see Note3)**

Calculate the predicted MCS as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_30887_replaced([11132172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krFGGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where

predicted_mcs_rank1 uses rrmInstSinrRank1 and predicted_mcs_rank2 uses rrmInstSinrRank2 

**If (SE_3GPP_Table(predicted_mcs_rank1)) > ((1+ rdThrPredictedGainRatio (5G_UP_ALG_30885_replaced([11141824](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) x SE_3GPP_Table(predicted_mcs_rank2) **[CB013202-B-UPD001] x 2**[End CB013202-B-UPD001]), see Note4** ****

rrmUlRiShortTerm=1

**Else**

rrmUlRiShortTerm= [Before PR83884-25R3] scheduled number of layers [PR83884-25R3] ulRank [End PR83884-25R3]

**End If**

**[CB013202-B-UPD001]**

Else If ulRank == 1 AND { rrmInstSinrRank2 >= rdUlSinrThresForSeCheck) AND (abs(Rank2Sinr_0 - Rank2Sinr_1) <= rdSinrGapBetweenLayersThresh) }(see Note3)

Calculate the predicted MCS as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_30887_replaced([11132172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krFGGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where

predicted_mcs_rank1 uses rrmInstSinrRank1 = ulPmiRank1Sinr[0], and

predicted_mcs_rank2 uses rrmInstSinrRank2 = average(ulPmiRank2Sinr[0], ulPmiRank2Sinr[1]), see Note2.

**If (SE_3GPP_Table(predicted_mcs_rank2)****x 2**) > ((1+ rdThrPredictedGainRatio (5G_UP_ALG_30885_replaced([11141824](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) x SE_3GPP_Table(predicted_mcs_rank1)), see Note4** _*_** *

rrmUlRiShortTerm=2

**Else**

rrmUlRiShortTerm=[Before PR83884-25R3] scheduled number of layers [PR83884-25R3] ulRank [End PR83884-25R3]

**End If**

**[End CB013202-B-UPD001]**

Else

rrmUlRiShortTerm**=ulrank**

**End If**

B) For UEs configured with adaptive number of SRS ports (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_6925_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If scheduled number of layers == 2

Same algorithm presented above in (A) applies.

Else If scheduled number of layers == 1

Legacy behavior applies as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3232_replaced([11140029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note0: SE_3GPP_Table(predicted_mcs_rankX) is outcome of **5G_UP_ALG_30887_replaced([11132172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krFGGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

Note1: If one of the conditions of the list is not satisfied (e.g., INVALID measurement in inputs (5G_UP_ALG_1742_replaced([11109711](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7J9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), then rrmUlRiShortTerm shall be set equal to ulRank.

Note2: Average calculation shall be according to rdAverageBetween2LayersFromPusch (see 5G_L2_1455_replaced([11186237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_274HevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Note3: rdUlSinrThresForSeCheck is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_31074_replaced([11141838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UDPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and rdSinrGapBetweenLayersThresh is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_30883_replaced([11141811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note4: In "(SE_3GPP_Table(predicted_mcs_rank2) **x 2" , 2 is the number of layers in rank2.**

Note5: if applicable as per PR629197, [CB013202-B-UPD002] when number of measurements is lower than rdNumSrsFreqHops then ulRank=1 is input of SE check function.[End CB013202-B-UPD002]

---

#### 3.9.2.3.0-4 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Input Rank2 Sinr for PUSCH SE check (ID: 12631297)

**3.9.2.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12631302`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Depending on the R&D parameter[12631289: rdUlRank2SinrSourceForPuschSeCheck](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gxnM1DveEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) the Rank2Sinr_0 and Rank2Sinr_1 are used :

· either by the SINR parameter ulPmiRank2Sinr[0][1] of the ulData_PuschReceiveRespPs message if rdUlRank2SinrSourceForPuschSeCheck is set to 0 or rdUlRank2SinrSourceForPuschSeCheck is set to 2 and the UE is a coherent UE

· or the post SINR after equalization (5G_UP_ALG_25392_replaced([11131411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCp5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if rdUlRank2SinrSourceForPuschSeCheck is set to 1 or rdUlRank2SinrSourceForPuschSeCheck is set to 2 and the UE is a non-coherent UE.

---

#### 3.9.2.3.0-5 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Short Term Rank Adaptation- Due to forced DFT-s-OFDM of VoNR UE (ID: 11139943)

**3.9.2.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11139950`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE,

  * From the point when user setup/modification is received for UE to add first [Before CB008118-C]5QI1 [CB008118-C] 5QI1/65/66 [End CB008118-C] DRB, upon PUSCH/SRS reception, force rrmUlRiShortTerm to be 1, instead of using UL Rank measured for updating rrmUlRiShortTerm.
  * If user setup/modification to add first[Before CB008118-C]5QI1 [CB008118-C] 5QI1/65/66 [End CB008118-C] DRB fails or when last [Before CB008118-C]5QI1 [CB008118-C] 5QI1/65/66 [End CB008118-C] DRB is released, stop forcing of rrmUlRiShortTerm to be 1, so that UL Rank measured is used to update rrmUlRiShortTerm upon PUSCH/SRS reception.

---

#### 3.9.2.3.0-6 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Rank selection (ID: 11139957)

**3.9.2.3.0-6.0-5**  (ID: `11139985`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH This requirement applies to 5G_UP_ALG_3224_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If DFT-S-OFDM for PUSCH is deactivated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = false):

 For next initial transmission, rank change from 1 to 2 shall occur when rrmUlRiLongTerm >1.5 + rdRiThresholdOffsetSwitchToRank2 (5G_L2_1096_replaced([11186646](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_277KxfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 For next initial transmission, rank change from 2 to 1 shall occur when rrmUlRiLongTerm <1.5 - rdRiThresholdOffsetSwitchToRank1 (5G_L2_1095_replaced([11186642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_277KxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If DFT-S-OFDM for PUSCH is activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = true):

 For next initial transmission, rank change from 1 to 2 shall occur when rrmUlRiLongTerm > ulRank1to2Thresh + rrmUlRank1to2ThreshOffset.

 For next initial transmission, rank change from 2 to 1 shall occur when rrmUlRiLongTerm < ulRank2to1Thresh + rrmUlRank2to1ThreshOffset.

ulRank1to2Thresh and ulRank2to1Thresh are provided at cell setup/reconfiguration through teh NIDD parameters:

 NRBTS/NRCELL/ulRank1to2Thresh.

 NRBTS/NRCELL/ulRank2to1Thresh.

rrmUlRank1to2ThreshOffset and rrmUlRank2to1ThreshOffset are set to rdUlRank1to2ThreshR16DmrsOffset (see 5G_UP_ALG_22796_replaced([11141624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0F7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdUlRank2to1ThreshR16DmrsOffset (see 5G_UP_ALG_22798_replaced([11141636](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0F7vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if UE is configured as R16 DMRS for transform precoding (dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding-r16 is present in RRC setup/reconfiguration), both set to 0 otherwise. Note: 5G-CP-RT would already configure transform precoding parameters (e.g. R15 or R16 DMRS) to UE and 5G-L2-PS, even before transform precoding is activated (which is signalled seperately via RRC reconfiguration).

For re-transmissions using spatial multiplexing, the rank shall not be changed.

L2-PS shall use the selected rank to fill the numOfLayers field in the UlData_PuschReceiveReq message.

If the UE capability is “single antenna” (see 5G_UP_ALG_3216_replaced([11139853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), i.e., singleTx, then the rank for the next initial transmission shall be always 1.

For UL transmissions performed in “UCI only” mode, UL rank is enforced to value 1, irrespective of the UE’s computed UL rank.

For a UE configured for Transform Precoder Enabled, UL rank is enforced to value 1 (per 3GPP), irrespective of the UE’s computed UL rank.

For users which are configured with periodic SRS in active BWP, the rrmUlRiLongTerm shall be fixed at 1 when the SU-MIMO state machine is at the state of **SU_MIMO_AGED. See 5G_UP_ALG_3236_replaced([11155554](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

NB : Initial access in singleTx is applicable from 5GC000425-S onwards.

**[CB013388-C]If NRCELL.actUlCgType2= TRUE,**[End CB013388-C] for a UE with configured grant (CG) type2 in CG-Configured state, an update of UE rank from 1 to 2 shall trigger the ‘SINR update event’ event that shall evaluate the opportunity of further triggering the CG activation (see 5G_UP_ALG_15121_replaced([11173004](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuPu2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).****

Any reconfiguration triggerd by the RRC layer, shoud not modify directly the rank selection, which should based only on the DCI Format used, the expected data on PUSCH (UCI only mode or not), the rrmUlRiLongTerm the thresholds defined above.

**Notes:**

 ulRank1to2Thresh is used when UE is in Transform Precoder disabled state (for example back to CP OFDM returning from DFT-S-OFDM).

 ulRank2to1Thresh is used before UE is configured for Transform Precoder enabled.

---

#### 3.9.2.3.0-7 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH PMI selection and default precoder (ID: 11139991)

**3.9.2.3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11140008`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH 11140008: L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH This requirement applies to 5G_UP_ALG_3224_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The TPMI used for the first rank1 initial transmission (after initial access in singleTx) shall be [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. It shows a fraction with 1 in the numerator and the square root of 2 in the denominator. This fraction is multiplied by a column vector containing the numbers 1 and 0. The expression is enclosed in a black border.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_8627.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] , if the UE capability of pusch-TransCoherence is nonCoherent. Otherwise, it shall be [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. It shows a fraction with 1 in the numerator and the square root of 2 in the denominator. This fraction is multiplied by a column vector containing two 1s. The expression is: $$ \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \begin{pmatrix} 1 \ 1 \end{pmatrix} $$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_8627.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] .

The PMI used if a first rank2 initial transmission (after initial access in singleTx) occurs before measurements from L1 is [image-2][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_8627.003.png[/image_path][/image-2] .

5G-L2-PS shall assign PUSCH power scaling ratio (see 5G_UP_ALG_6818_replaced([11103724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knzvrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to UE's full power mode, see 5G_UP_ALG_6881_replaced([11140012](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and deliver the assigned PUSCH scaling ratio to 5G-L1-UL.

For the next transmissions (including retransmissions) using spatial multiplexing:

The PMI shall be selected from last received VALID PMI in UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs and UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs corresponding to selected rank.

Update of rank1 and rank2 PMIs value shall only be done when nonDTX has to be received from UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs or UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs. In such case, latest received rank1 and rank2 PMIs are updated based on latest VALID PMIs from these messages.

---

#### 3.9.2.3.0-8 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH PUSCH power scaling ratio assignment (ID: 11140012)

**3.9.2.3.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11140022`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH This requirement applies to 5G_UP_ALG_3231_replaced([11139991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq7_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * If UE is not configured with RRC IE: ul-FullPowerTransmission-r16 then



\- 5G-L2-PS shall assign 5G-L1-UL the PUSCH power scaling ratio (5G_UP_ALG_6818_replaced([11103724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knzvrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) per 1 layer TPMI (TPMI 0,1,2) when PUSCH or SRS receiving is requested.

|  |  |   
---|---|---|---  
Full Power Mode Type (see 5G_UP_3769_replaced([11355420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucQnHvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | 1Layer TPMI 0 | 1Layer TPMI 1 | 1Layer TPMI 2  
Non-full power mode | INVALID | INVALID | INVALID  
  
  * If RRC IE: ul-FullPowerTransmission-r16 is fullpower then



\- 5G-L2-PS shall assign 5G-L1-UL the PUSCH power scaling ratio per 1 layer TPMI (TPMI 0,1,2) when PUSCH or SRS receiving is requested.

|  |  |   
---|---|---|---  
Full Power Mode Type (see 5G_UP_3769_replaced([11355420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucQnHvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | 1Layer TPMI 0 | 1Layer TPMI 1 | 1Layer TPMI 2  
fullpower | 2 | 2 | INVALID  
  
  * If RRC IE: ul-FullPowerTransmission-r16 is fullpowerMode1 then



\- 5G-L2-PS shall check UE’s Power limit status determined by 5G_UP_ALG_9755_replaced([11130171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_ffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- 5G-L2-PS shall assign 5G-L1-UL the PUSCH power scaling ratio per 1 layer TPMI (TPMI 0,1,2) when PUSCH or SRS receiving is requested.

|  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---  
Full Power Mode Type (see 5G_UP_3769_replaced([11355420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucQnHvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | 1Layer TPMI 0 | 1Layer TPMI 1 | 1Layer TPMI 2 | UE power limit status  
fullpowerMode1 | INVALID | INVALID | 1 | In power limit  
fullpowerMode1 | 1 | 1 | INVALID | Not in power limit  
  
  * If RRC IE: ul-FullPowerTransmission-r16 is fullpowerMode2 then



\- Based on UE's capability ul-FullPwrMode2-TPMIGroup-r16 >>twoPorts-r16, 5G-L2-PS shall get UE's full power TPMI.

\- 5G-L2-PS shall assign 5G-L1-UL the PUSCH power scaling ratio per 1 layer TPMI (TPMI 0,1,2) depend on UE's full power TPMI indication when PUSCH or SRS receiving is requested.

|  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---  
Full Power Mode Type (see 5G_UP_3769_replaced([11355420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucQnHvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | 1Layer TPMI 0 | 1Layer TPMI 1 | 1Layer TPMI 2 | Full power TPMI indicated by UE's capability  
fullpowerMode2 | 2 | 1 | INVALID | 0 (TPMI 0)  
fullpowerMode2 | 1 | 2 | INVALID | 1 (TPMI 1)  
  
[Note]

For Rel 16's UE, if UE capability of pusch-TransCoherence is not nonCoherent, then RRC IE: ul-FullPowerTransmission-r16 is not configured.

#### 3.9.2.3.0-9 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Long period without SRS measurements (ID: 11140029)

**3.9.2.3.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11140046`)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH 11140046: L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH This requirement applies to 5G_UP_ALG_3224_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For the case of periodic SRS in active BWP : For users which are configured with periodic SRS, to handle long period without SRS measurements, see algorithms defined in state machine for BM (5G_UP_ALG_2136_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and state machine for SU-MIMO (5G_UP_ALG_3236_replaced([11155554](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) . For the case of aperiodic SRS: **Long period with PUSCH rank1 scheduling and without SRS measurements** or UE has "adaptive number of SRS ports" state "single Tx" (5G_L2_656_replaced([11164313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25sWIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**_* The Long Term Rank Measurments timer (rrmLtrPollTimer) (_ timer defined in 5G_UP_ALG_8305_replaced([11140053](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be reinitialized to zero and (re-)started:_\- if the first initial transmission is rank 1. i.e. the timer is not running and an UL grant is sent to UE and indicates rank1, \- or each time the rank of next initial transmission changes from 2 to 1, \- or each time a valid PMI is measured from SrsReceiveResponse. i.e. the timer was running and the SRS response is not DTX, \- or each time, rrmLtrPollTimer expires and the rank of next initial transmission is 1. i.e. rrmUlRiLongTerm is 1 at timer expiration. For each UE, the SRS report aged flag shall be maintained (its initial value is 0). On each time a valid PMI is measured from SrsReceiveResponse, the SRS report aged flag shall be set to 0 When the timer expires and the rank of next initial transmission is 1: \- the SRS report aged flag of UE shall be set to 1. \- If adaptive numbers of SRS ports are configured (defined in 5G_UP_ALG_6925_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) the sinr from latest UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs in 5G_UP_ALG_1701_replaced([11108899](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kowx7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_2640_replaced([11119228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) corresponding to the latest PUSCH scheduled with rank 1 is compared to rdUlSinrThreForRiAdaptSrsPorts defined in 5G_L2_1094_replaced([11186486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2758p_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If sinr is below rdUlSinrThreForRiAdaptSrsPorts, rrmUlRiLongTerm is updated with rrmUlRiShortTerm=1, else with rrmUlRiShortTerm=2. else the sinr from latest UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs in 5G_UP_ALG_1701_replaced([11108899](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kowx7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_2640_replaced([11119228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) corresponding to the latest PUSCH scheduled with rank 1 is compared to rdUlSinrThresholdForRi defined in 5G_L2_1093_replaced([11186513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2758rPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If sinr is below rdUlSinrThresholdForRi, rrmUlRiLongTerm is updated with rrmUlRiShortTerm=1, else with rrmUlRiShortTerm=2. For both cases the SINR from latest _UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs only contributes once to rrmUlRiLongTerm computation: if the timer expires more than once before a new *UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs is available, rrmUlRiLongTerm is not updated.** \- According to the long-term average rule, if the updated rank of next initial transmission is 1, the PMI is set based on the following rule: **If RRC IE:_ul-FullPowerTransmission-r16 is not configured | is configured to fullpower Then_** **If sinr[0] (corresponding to the last PUSCH) >= rdUlSinrThresholdForRi & _timer defined in 5G_UP_ALG_8305_replaced([11140053](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) expires [High SINR]_** Then, the PMI is not toggled (last PMI is used) **Elseif sinr[0] (corresponding to the last PUSCH) < rdUlSinrThresholdForRi & _timer defined in 5G_UP_ALG_8305_replaced([11140053](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) expires [Low SINR]_** Then, the PMI shall be set to the last valid PMI received for rank 1. [approach proposed in PR457399 with new condition] note: the last used PMI might lead to failure. So instead the "last valid PMI" shall be used (the last PMI that yield to a successful transmission) **[Before PR721391]** If UE is configured for skippable grants (5G_UP_ALG_4839_replaced([11195286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7J1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), a PUSCH DTX indication is ignored in determination of " last valid PMI" if DTX is associated with any of the following. #### 3.9.2.3.0-10 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Timer Selection for Long period without SRS measurements (ID: 11140053)

L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH This requirement applies to 5G_UP_ALG_3232_replaced([11140029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 3.9.2.3.0-11 L2 Rank and PMI selection on PUSCH Reinitialization of the UL precoder settings and number of layers after a beamforming recovery procedure (ID: 11140062)

### 3.9.2.4 L2 inputs for L1 Rank and PMI selection

#### 3.9.2.4.1 Threshold for L1 SVD RI algorithm

##### 3.9.2.4.1.0-1 Threshold for L1 SVD RI algorithm Overview (ID: 11140083)

**3.9.2.4.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11140102`)

Threshold for L1 SVD RI algorithm The gNB-DU shall select as follows an appropriate threshold for use by the L1 Single Value Decomposition (SVD) Rank Indicator (RI) algorithm.

  * Usage: When PUSCH or SRS reception is requested, L2 sends value to L1 in decode request:
  * Value selection:
  * If PUSCH DFT-s-OFDM is enabled (NRCELL.actUlDftSOfdm = True),
  * For PUSCH,SRS received with 8 streams cf. 5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) : rdUlRiSelectionThresh8RxTp (5G_UP_ALG_25790_replaced([11141577](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0F5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * [CB010708-D] For PUSCH,SRS received with 16 streams cf. 5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) : rdUlRiSelectionThresh16RxTp (5G_UP_ALG_27495_replaced([11141592](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0F5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB010708-D]
  * Otherwise: rdUlRiSelectionThreshCommonTp (5G_UP_ALG_25792_replaced([11141612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0F6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Else:
  * For PUSCH,SRS received with 8 streams cf. 5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) : rdUlRiSelectionThresh8Rx (5G_UP_ALG_19769_replaced([11141521](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * [CB010708-D] For PUSCH,SRS received with 16 streams cf. 5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) : rdUlRiSelectionThresh16Rx (5G_UP_ALG_27493_replaced([11141542](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0F4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB010708-D]
  * Otherwise: rdUlRiSelectionThreshCommon (5G_UP_ALG_25951_replaced([11141562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0F4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



Simulation results are available here : [CB009363_SU_MIMO_RI_PMI_IRCgain_folder](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB009000%20-%20CB009499/CFAM/CB009363%208Rx%20IRC%20receiver%20ABIP%20FR1%20TDD/References-Simulations/SU_MIMO_RI_PMI_IRCgain?csf=1&web=1&e=7elSYW)

Notes:

  * See 5G_UP_ALG_6449_replaced([11103673](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knzIlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for references to L1 HW.
  * The change to have L2 send valid thresholds to L1 for both C8 and non-C8 scenarios was introduced by CNI-108786 but is applicable even if CNI-108786 is disabled (NRCELL/ulTransPreEnhRankIwk = false).
  * MU receiver use same RI threshold as SU receiver size , [CB010708-D] please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_27913_replaced([11140110](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB010708-D]

---

##### 3.9.2.4.1.0-2 Threshold for L1 SVD RI algorithm Overview : MU receiver (ID: 11140110)

**3.9.2.4.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11140115`)

Threshold for L1 SVD RI algorithm The gNB-DU shall select as follows an appropriate threshold for use by the L1 Single Value Decomposition (SVD) Rank Indicator (RI) algorithm.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
NO. | numOfRxPusch | rdSuUeReceiverSize | one SSB | Mu status | streams number for single UE | receiver size | UlRiSelectionThreshold  
1 | 16 | 8 | / | SU | 8 | 8 | riThresh8Rx  
2 | 16 | 16 | YES | SU | 8 | 8 | riThresh8Rx  
3 | 16 | 16 | NO | SU | 16 | 16 | riThresh16Rx  
4 | 16 | 8 | / | 2 UE MU | 8 | 16 | riThresh8Rx  
5 | 16 | 8 | / | 4 UE MU | 4 | 16 | riThresh8Rx  
6 | 16 | 16 | / | 2 UE MU | 8 | 16 | riThresh16Rx  
7 | 16 | 16 | / | 4 UE MU | 4 | 16 | riThresh16Rx

---

#### 3.9.2.4.2 L2 IRC gain estimation

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-1 L2 IRC gain estimation IRC gain overview (ID: 11140125)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11140130`)

L2 IRC gain estimation This requirement provides a summary to have a quick view of requirements of interest depending on NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod. Main differences are highlighted in bold.

|  |   
---|---|---  
**Requirements per IRC gain estimation Method** | **NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh. enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = longTermDiff** | **NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh. enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = shortTermDiff**  
PUSCH IRC Gain overview | 5G_UP_ALG_19665_replaced([11140137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | 5G_UP_ALG_19665_replaced([11140137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  
**PUSCH IRC gain computation** | **5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** | **5G_UP_ALG_30791_replaced([11140190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**  
SRS IRC Gain overview | 5G_UP_ALG_19742_replaced([11140202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | 5G_UP_ALG_19742_replaced([11140202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  
Long term average for rank1/rank2 PUSCH post Equalized SINR | 5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | 5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  
**Long term average for uncompensated rank1/rank2 PUSCH PMI SINR** | **5G_UP_ALG_19677_replaced([11140280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))****5G_UP_ALG_19679_replaced([11140353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))****** | **Not used**  
Long term average for uncompensated rank1/rank2 SRS PMI SINR | 5G_UP_ALG_19678_replaced([11140301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G_UP_ALG_19680_replaced([11140371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | 5G_UP_ALG_19678_replaced([11140301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G_UP_ALG_19680_replaced([11140371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  
**Longterm Averaging coefficient for SINR** | **5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** | **5G_UP_ALG_30793_replaced([11141291](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**  
**Long term Averaging coefficient for IRC gain** | **Not used** | **5G_UP_ALG_30795_replaced([11141306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**  
Timers for long term averaging for SINR PUSCH rank1, PUSCH rank2, SRS | 5G_UP_ALG_19684_replaced([11141342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19694_replaced([11141353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19686_replaced([11141368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3w_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | 5G_UP_ALG_19684_replaced([11141342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19694_replaced([11141353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19686_replaced([11141368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3w_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  
  
When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGain is false, NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod is ignored.
