##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-2 L2 IRC gain estimation PUSCH IRC Gain overview (ID: 11140137)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11140159`)

L2 IRC gain estimation For PUSCH received with [CB013202-A] 4, [End CB013202-A] 8 or 16 streams cf. 5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and when [Before CB013202-A] rdCompensateIrcGain = true (5G_UP_ALG_19667_replaced([11141270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB013202-A] NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGain =true [End CB013202-A] and for UEs which are not fake UEs (5G_UP_ALG_17489_replaced([11215719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxU4CvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), DU shall estimate IRC gain in order to improve RI and PMI estimation in presence of interference,

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = longTermDiff, [End CB013202-C]

Before PUSCH reception DU shall perform PUSCH IRC gain computation

At each PUSCH reception request (whatever the rank), at slot N+x:

  * DU shall compute PUSCH IRC Gain (5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on long term values from slots M and N (see. long term averaging below)



\- DU shall convey PUSCH IRC Gain (computed in slot N+x) in PUSCH reception request (slot N+x) to preparePUSCH PMI/RI selection (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * DU shall keep PUSCH IRC Gain in memory until the PUSCH response of slot (N+x) is processed (including impact of capping in 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



where:

  * x is the delay since the latest PUSCH reception in slot N

  * M is latest PUSCH rank1 reception

  * N is the latest PUSCH rank2 reception




Upon PUSCH reception DU shall perform following long term averaging

At each Pusch rank1 reception (slot M):

  * DU shall perform long term average of PUSCH rank 1 post-equ SINR (cf.5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



At each Pusch rank2 reception (slot N>M):

  * DU shall perform long term average of PUSCH rank 2 post-equ SINR after averaging both layers (5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



\- DU shall perform long term average of Rank1 and rank2 PUSCH PMI SINR separately after removing PUSCH IRC gain used in the receive request of slot N (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_19677_replaced([11140280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19679_replaced([11140353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = shortTermDiff ,

Before PUSCH reception

At each PUSCH reception request (whatever the rank), at slot N+x:

\- DU shall convey PUSCH IRC Gain (using last long term average in slot N, 5G_UP_ALG_30791_replaced([11140190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in PUSCH reception request (slot N+x) to prepare PUSCH PMI/RI selection (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * DU shall keep PUSCH IRC Gain in memory until the PUSCH response of slot (N+x) is processed (including impact of capping in 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



where:

  * x is the delay since the latest PUSCH reception in slot N

  * M is latest PUSCH rank1 reception

  * N is the latest PUSCH rank2 reception




Upon PUSCH reception DU shall perform following long term averaging

At each Pusch rank1 reception (slot M):

  * DU shall perform long term average of PUSCH rank 1 post-equ SINR (cf.5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



At each Pusch rank2 reception (slot N>M):

  * DU shall perform long term average of PUSCH rank 2 post-equ SINR after averaging both layers (5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * DU shall perform long term average rrmIrcGainLT (5G_UP_ALG_30791_replaced([11140190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after computation of short term IRC gain (5G_UP_ALG_30787_replaced([11140179](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * In order to compute short term IRC gain DU shall use PUSCH IRC Gain in memory to uncompensate the short term rank2 PUSCH PMI SINR (5G_UP_ALG_30787_replaced([11140179](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))




Whatever NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod, [End CB013202-C] when IRC gain functionality is not active for [CB013202-A] 4, [End CB013202-A] 8 and 16 streams reception, PUSCH IRC Gain is equal to 0dB.

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-3 L2 IRC gain estimation PUSCH IRC gain computation (longTermDiff) (ID: 11140163)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12784375`)

L2 IRC gain estimation When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = longTermDiff **,**

DU shall compute rrmPuschIrcGain (as per 5G_UP_ALG_19665_replaced([11140137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) overview). Initial value of rrmIrcGainPusch is 0dB.

1) rrmRank1IrcGainPusch = max(0, rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT - rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT)

when :

  * rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT (5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not INVALID

  * **and rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT (5G_UP_ALG_19677_replaced([11140280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not INVALID**




otherwise

rrmRank1IrcGainPusch is INVALID

2) If NRCELL.actUlMuMimo=true and NRCELL.actPmiSinrUlMuMimo=true,

rrmRank2IrcGainPusch = rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT – rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT

else 

rrmRank2IrcGainPusch = max(0, rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT – rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT)

when :

  * rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT (5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not INVALID

  * **and rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT(5G_UP_ALG_19679_replaced([11140353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not INVALID**




otherwise

rrmRank2IrcGainPusch is INVALID

3) [PR845031] When NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainPerRank=false, [End PR845031] If neither rrmRank1IrcGainPusch nor rrmRank2IrcGainPusch are INVALID,

rrmPuschIrcGain = average (rrmRank1IrcGainPusch , rrmRank2IrcGainPusch) depending on rdUlIrcGainRank1Rank2Average (5G_UP_ALG_19939_replaced([11141380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3xfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If only either rrmRank1IrcGainPusch or rrmRank2IrcGainPusch is INVALID

rrmPuschIrcGain = rrmRank1IrcGainPusch or rrmRank2IrcGainPusch (avoiding INVALID measure)

If both rrmRank1IrcGainPusch and rrmRank2IrcGainPusch is INVALID

rrmPuschIrcGain =0dB

[PR845031] When NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainPerRank=true, 

If rrmRank2IrcGainPusch is VALID

rrmPuschIrcGain = rrmRank2IrcGainPusch, else rrmPuschIrcGain =0dB

[End PR845031] 

rrmPuschIrcGain is used in 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note : For NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = shortTermDiff , please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_30787_replaced([11140179](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-4 L2 IRC gain estimation PUSCH IRC gain computation (shortTermDiff) (ID: 11140179)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11140185`)

L2 IRC gain estimation When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = shortTermDiff ,

DU shall compute rrmIrcGainST from PUSCH rank2 reception on slot N+x ( N,x as per 5G_UP_ALG_19665_replaced([11140137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) overview):

If one condition below is not met, rrmIrcGainST (i,j,t) is not computed (e.g. set to negative value)

\- VALID rank indication AND nonDTX have been received

\- sinr[0] and sinr[1] and ulPmiRank2Sinr[0] and ulPmiRank2Sinr[1] are VALID

\- lowest layer ulPmiRank2Sinr is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and highest layer ulPmiRank2Sinr is inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Same rule applies to post SU-SINR[0] and post SU-SINR[1] when available otherwise same rule applies to sinr[0] and sinr[1].

\- absolute value of the SINR difference between ulPmiRank2Sinr of the 2 layers is strictly inferior to rdUlMaxSinrDiffLayers (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24307_replaced([11141409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Same rule applies to post SU-SINR[0] and post SU-SINR[1] when available. otherwise same rule applies to sinr[0] and sinr[1].

Else

\- DU shall compute sinr average between layers of Rank2 transmissions (result is in dB scale) from PUSCH on slot N depending on R&D parameter rdAverageBetween2LayersFromPusch (see 5G_L2_1455_replaced([11186237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_274HevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3084_replaced([11131461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

\- i.e. DU shall shall compute rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers of the SINR parameter UlPmiRank2Sinr[0] and UlPmiRank2Sinr[1] of the current PUSCH reception,

\- i.e. DU shall compute sinrAv2layers of post SU-SINR[0] and post SU-SINR[1] when available in the last PUSCH reception otherwise L2-PS shall compute sinrAv2layers of the SINR parameter sinr[0] and sinr[1] of the current PUSCH reception,

\- then DU shall :

if NRCELL.actPmiSinrMuMimo=true,

compute rrmIrcGainST (i,j,t) = sinrAv2layers(i,j,t) – (rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers (i,j,t)- rrmPuschIrcGain (from the PUSCH receive request of slot N , cf. Note2))

else

compute rrmIrcGainST (i,j,t) = max (0, sinrAv2layers(i,j,t) – (rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers (i,j,t)- rrmPuschIrcGain (from the PUSCH receive request of slot N , cf. Note2))

\- next, DU shall restart rdIrcGainValidityTimer (5G_UP_ALG_30795_replaced([11141306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

\- DU shall use rrmIrcGainST in 5G_UP_ALG_30791_replaced([11140190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- With:

\- i: Index of the UE

\- j: Index of the carrier

\- t: Time (UL slot) for that the SINR is predicted

When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = longTermDiff, rrmIrcGainST is not computed.

Note : For NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = longTermDiff , please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Important Note2:

When rrmPuschIrcGain is capped to compute Pboost for a given PUSCH request (see 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the capped value (rdUlPuschIrcGainMax see 5G_UP_ALG_24309_replaced([11141429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3zPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) should be used here to uncompensate rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers from the corresponding PUSCH response

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-5 L2 IRC gain estimation PUSCH IRC gain computation (long term average in shortTermDiff Method) (ID: 11140190)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11140196`)

L2 IRC gain estimation When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = shortTermDiff ,

When rrmIrcGainST is computed, DU shall start rdIrcGainValidityTimer and compute rrmIrcGainLT as follows :

rrmIrcGainLT = rrmIrcGainLT * (1 – rdUlIrcGainBetaMethod2) + rrmIrcGainST * rdUlIrcGainBetaMethod2

Where :

  * rrmIrcGainST (i,j,t) is output from 5G_UP_ALG_30787_replaced([11140179](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * rdUlIrcGainBetaMethod2 is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_30793_replaced([11141291](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * Initial value of rrmIrcGainLT shall be equal to 0dB.




Update of long-term averaged value shall only be done when nonDTX has been received from UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs.

If rdIrcGainValidityTimer (5G_UP_ALG_30795_replaced([11141306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires then rrmIrcGainLT is reset to 0dB.

DU shall use rrmPuschIrcGain=rrmIrcGainLT in 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = longTermDiff,

rrmIrcGainLT is not computed.

Note : For NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = longTermDiff , please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-6 L2 IRC gain estimation SRS IRC gain overview (ID: 11140202)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `11140226`)

L2 IRC gain estimation For SRS received with [CB013202-A] 4, [End CB013202-A] 8 or 16 streams cf. 5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and when [Before CB013202-A] rdCompensateIrcGain = true (5G_UP_ALG_19667_replaced([11141270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB013202-A] NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGain =true [End CB013202-A] and for UEs which are not fake UEs (5G_UP_ALG_17489_replaced([11215719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxU4CvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), IRC gain is estimated at L2 and sent to L1 in order to improve RI and PMI estimation in presence of interference,

Before SRS reception DU shall perform SRS IRC gain computation

At each SRS reception request (slot Q= O+x or slot Q=P+x):

\- SRS IRC Gain (5G_UP_ALG_19671_replaced([11140233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is computed based on long term values from slots N, O and P (see long term averaging below)

\- SRS IRC Gain (computed in slot Q) shall be sent to L1 in the SRS reception request (slot Q) for PUSCH PMI/RI selection (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_2656_replaced([11119429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

\- SRS IRC Gain shall be kept in memory until the SRS response of slot Q is processed at DU (including impact of SRS power offset capping in 5G_UP_ALG_10497_replaced([11119432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

where :

  * x is delay since the latest PUSCH reception in slot O for Q=O+x, ie SRS reception follows a pusch rank1

  * or x is the delay since the latest SRS reception in slot P for Q=P+x ie two SRS reception without intermediate pusch rank1 reception

  * N is the latest PUSCH rank2 reception

  * O is latest PUSCH rank1 reception

  * P is the latest SRS reception




Upon PUSCH or SRS reception DU shall perform following long term averaging

At each Pusch rank2 reception (slot N):

\- PUSCH rank 2 post-equ SINR is long term averaged after averaging both layers (5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

At each Pusch rank1 reception (slot O>N):

\- PUSCH rank 1 post-equ SINR is long term averaged (cf.5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

At each SRS reception (slot P):

Rank1 and rank2 SRS PMI SINR are long term averaged after averaging both layers and after removing respective SRS IRC gain used in the receive request of slot P (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_19678_replaced([11140301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19680_replaced([11140371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When IRC gain functionality is not active for [CB013202-A] 4, [End CB013202-A] 8 and 16 streams reception, SRS IRC Gain is equal to 0dB.

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=shortTermDiff, SRS IRC gain is impacted in longterm averaging cf. 5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),5G_UP_ALG_19678_replaced([11140301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19680_replaced([11140371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB013202-C]

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-7 L2 IRC gain estimation SRS IRC gain computation (ID: 11140233)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `12784462`)

L2 IRC gain estimation 5G-L2-PS shall compute rrmSrsIrcGain (as per 5G_UP_ALG_19742_replaced([11140202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) overview). Initial value of rrmIrcGainSrs is 0dB.

1) If rdUlIrcGainNegativeValues (5G_UP_ALG_19941_replaced([11141393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3x_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true

rrmRank1IrcGainSrs = rrmUlpostEqRank1SinrPuschLT - rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT

else

rrmRank1IrcGainSrs =max (0, rrmUlpostEqRank1SinrPuschLT - rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT)

for :

  * rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT (5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not INVALID

  * **and rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT (5G_UP_ALG_19678_replaced([11140301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not INVALID**




otherwise

rrmRank1IrcGainSrs is INVALID

2) If rdUlIrcGainNegativeValues (5G_UP_ALG_19941_replaced([11141393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3x_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true

rrmRank2IrcGainSrs = rrmUlpostEqRank2SinrPuschLT - rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT

else

rrmRank2IrcGainSrs =max (0, rrmUlpostEqRank2SinrPuschLT - rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT)

when :

  * rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT (5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not INVALID

  * **and rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT(5G_UP_ALG_19680_replaced([11140371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not INVALID**




otherwise

rrmRank2IrcGainSrs is INVALID

3) [PR845031] When NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainPerRank=false,[End PR845031] If neither rrmRank1IrcGainSrs nor rrmRank2IrcGainSrs are INVALID,

rrmSrsIrcGain = average(rrmRank1IrcGainSrs , rrmRank2IrcGainSrs) depending on rdUlIrcGainRank1Rank2Average (5G_UP_ALG_19939_replaced([11141380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3xfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If only either rrmRank1IrcGainSrs or rrmRank2IrcGainSrs is INVALID

rrmSrsIrcGain = rrmRank1IrcGainSrs or rrmRank2IrcGainSrs (avoiding INVALID measure)

If both rrmRank1IrcGainSrs and rrmRank2IrcGainSrs is INVALID

rrmSrsIrcGain =0dB

[PR845031] When NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainPerRank=true, 

If rrmRank1IrcGainSrs is VALID

rrmSrsIrcGain = rrmRank1IrcGainSrs, else rrmSrsIrcGain =0dB

[End PR845031] 

rrmSrsIrcGain is used in 5G_UP_ALG_2656_replaced([11119429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Important Note : Negative IRC gain corresponds to correction of SRS optimistic measures e.g. SRS has less interferences than PUSCH.

Note : NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod has impact on SRS IRC gain because of longterm averaging cf. 5G_UP_ALG_19676_replaced([11140325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19674_replaced([11140254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),5G_UP_ALG_19678_replaced([11140301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_19680_replaced([11140371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-8 L2 IRC gain estimation Long term average for rank1 post equalized SINR (ID: 11140254)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `11140273`)

L2 IRC gain estimation For any given UE, a long term rank1 sinr average shall be derived from PUSCH post SU-SINR (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_21980_replaced([11108940](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when available otherwise post-equalizer SINR (cf.5G_UP_ALG_7163_replaced([11108902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Both possible inputs to long term rank1 sinr average are called sinr as follows :

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=longTermDiff, [End CB013202-C] 

if rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT is reset to Invalid value,

rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT = sinr +UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection

else

rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT = rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT * (1 - rdUlIrcGainBeta) + (sinr+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection) * rdUlIrcGainBeta

Where

  * rdUlIrcGainBetais defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))



Update of long-term averaged value shall only be done when :

· nonDTX has been received

· and short term first layer sinr from same message is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If all conditions above are satisfied, rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank1 is restarted once for a given PUSCH reception.

UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_22294_replaced([11140393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank1 (5G_UP_ALG_19694_replaced([11141353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires then rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT is reset to Invalid value (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_1746_replaced([11109764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7xC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmUlPostEqRank1SinrPuschLT is used for PUSCH IRC gain [CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=longTermDiff, [End CB013202-C] (5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and SRS IRC gain (5G_UP_ALG_19671_replaced([11140233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=shortTermDiff,

Only change in this requirement compared to longTermDiff is that DU shall use rdUlIrcGainBetaMethod2( 5G_UP_ALG_30793_replaced([11141291](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in long term averaging instead of rdUlIrcGainBeta (5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB013202-C]

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-9 L2 IRC gain estimation Long term average for uncompensated rank1 PUSCH PMI SINR (ID: 11140280)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11140295`)

L2 IRC gain estimation [CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=longTermDiff, [End CB013202-C]

For any given UE, a long term uncompensated PUSCH rank1 PMI SINR average shall be derived from PUSCH (UlPmiRank1Sinr) on slot N as follows :

if rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT is reset to Invalid value,

rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT= (UlPmiRank1Sinr+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection) -rrmPuschIrcGain (from the PUSCH receive request of slot N cf. Note2 )

else

rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT= rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT* (1 - rdUlIrcGainBeta) + (UlPmiRank1Sinr+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection-rrmPuschIrcGain from the PUSCH receive request of slot N cf. Note2) * rdUlIrcGainBeta

Where

  * rdUlIrcGainBeta is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * rrmPuschIrcGain is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))




Update of long-term averaged value shall only be done when :

· VALID rank indication AND nonDTX have been received

· and short term UlPmiRank1Sinr from same message is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If all conditions above are satisfied, rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank2 is restarted once for a given PUSCH reception.

UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_22294_replaced([11140393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank2 (5G_UP_ALG_19684_replaced([11141342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires then rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT is reset to Invalid value (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_1746_replaced([11109764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7xC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT is used for PUSCH IRC gain (5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Note: rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank2 is used because UlPmiRank1Sinr,UlPmiRank2Sinr are only measured when PUSCH rank2 is received.

Important Note2:

When rrmPuschIrcGain is capped to compute Pboost for a given PUSCH request (see 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the capped value (rdUlPuschIrcGainMax see 5G_UP_ALG_24309_replaced([11141429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3zPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) should be used here to uncompensate UlPmiRank1Sinr from the corresponding PUSCH response.

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=shortTermDiff,

rrmUlPmiRank1SinrPuschLT is not computed. [End CB013202-C]

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-10 L2 IRC gain estimation Long term average for uncompensated rank1 SRS PMI SINR (ID: 11140301)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `11140317`)

L2 IRC gain estimation For any given UE, a long term uncompensated SRS rank1 PMI SINR average shall be derived from ndication (UlPmiRank1Sinr) on slot O as follows :

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=longTermDiff, [End CB013202-C]

if rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT is reset to Invalid value:

rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT = UlPmiRank1Sinr+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection -rrmSrsIrcGain (from the SRS receive request of slot O, cf. note2 )

else

rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT = rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT* (1 - rdUlIrcGainBeta) + (UlPmiRank1Sinr+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection-rrmSrsIrcGain from the SRS receive request of slot O, cf. note2) * rdUlIrcGainBeta

Where

  * rdUlIrcGainBeta is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * rrmSrsIrcGain is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19671_replaced([11140233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))




UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_22294_replaced([11140393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If rdIrcGainValidityTimerSRS (5G_UP_ALG_19686_replaced([11141368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3w_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires then rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLTis reset to Invalid value.

Update of long-term averaged value shall only be done when :

· nonDTX has been received

· and short term UlPmiRank1Sinr from same message is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If all conditions above are satisfied, rdIrcGainValidityTimerSrs is restarted once for a given SRS reception. [End

If rdIrcGainValidityTimerSrs (5G_UP_ALG_19684_replaced([11141342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires then rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT is reset to Invalid value (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_1746_replaced([11109764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7xC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmUlPmiRank1SinrSrsLT is used for SRS IRC gain (5G_UP_ALG_19671_replaced([11140233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Important Note2 :

When powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe is capped to minimum or maximum value for a given SRS request, then rrmSrsIrcGainAfterCapping as per 5G_UP_ALG_10497_replaced([11119432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) should be used here to uncompensate the UlPmiRank1Sinr from the corresponding SRS response.

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=shortTermDiff,

Only change in this requirement compared to longTermDiff is that DU shall use rdUlIrcGainBetaMethod2( 5G_UP_ALG_30793_replaced([11141291](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in long term averaging instead of rdUlIrcGainBeta (5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB013202-C]

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-11 L2 IRC gain estimation Long term average for rank2 post equalized SINR (ID: 11140325)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-11.0-3**  (ID: `11140346`)

L2 IRC gain estimation [CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=longTermDiff, [End CB013202-C]

For any given UE,

1) depending on R&D parameter rdAverageBetween2LayersFromPusch (see 5G_L2_1455_replaced([11186237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_274HevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3084_replaced([11131461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall compute sinr average between layers of Rank2 transmissions (result is in dB scale) from PUSCH :

· sinrAv2layers of [Before CB010708-K-UPD001] post SU-SINR[0] and post SU-SINR[1] [CB010708-K-UPD001] max (post SU-SINR[0], sinr[0]) and max (post SU-SINR[1], sinr[1]) [End CB010708-K-UPD001]

when available in the last PUSCH reception otherwise

· [Before CB010708-K-UPD001] sinrAv2layers of post SU-SINR[0] and post SU-SINR[1] [CB010708-K-UPD001] max (sinrAv2layers, PostsinrAv2layers) where sinrAv2layers is average of of the SINR parameter sinr[0] and sinr[1] and PostsinrAv2layers is average of post SU-SINR[0], post SU-SINR[1] [End CB010708-K-UPD001] when available in the last PUSCH reception otherwise

· sinrAv2layers of the SINR parameter sinr[0] and sinr[1] of the last PUSCH reception

2) A long-term rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT average shall be derived from sinrAv2layers as follows:

if rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT is reset to Invalid value:

rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT = sinrAv2layers+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection 

else

rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT = rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT * (1 - rdUlIrcGainBeta) + (sinrAv2layers+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection) * rdUlIrcGainBeta

Where

  * rdUlIrcGainBeta is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))



Long term averaged value is only updated when:

· VALID rank indication AND nonDTX have been received

· and lowest layer sinr is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and highest layer sinr is inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

· and absolute value of the SINR difference between the 2 layers is strictly inferior to rdUlMaxSinrDiffLayers (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24307_replaced([11141409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If all conditions above are satisfied, rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank2 is restarted once for a given PUSCH reception.

UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_22294_replaced([11140393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank2 (5G_UP_ALG_19684_replaced([11141342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires then rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT is reset to Invalid value (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_1746_replaced([11109764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7xC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmUlPostEqRank2SinrPuschLT is used for PUSCH IRC gain [CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=longTermDiff, [End CB013202-C] (5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and SRS IRC gain (5G_UP_ALG_19671_replaced([11140233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=shortTermDiff,

Additional change in this requirement compared to longTermDiff is that DU shall use rdUlIrcGainBetaMethod2( 5G_UP_ALG_30793_replaced([11141291](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in long term averaging instead of rdUlIrcGainBeta (5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB013202-C]

---

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-12 L2 IRC gain estimation Long term average for uncompensated rank2 PUSCH PMI SINR (ID: 11140353)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-12.0-3**  (ID: `12539532`)

L2 IRC gain estimation **[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=longTermDiff,**[End CB013202-C]****

For any given UE,

1) depending on R&D parameter rdAverageBetween2LayersFromPusch (see 5G_L2_1455_replaced([11186237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_274HevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3084_replaced([11131461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall compute sinr average between layers of Rank2 transmissions (result is in dB scale) from PUSCH on slot N:

· rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers of the SINR parameter UlPmiRank2Sinr[0] and UlPmiRank2Sinr[1] of the last PUSCH

2) a long-term uncompensated PUSCH rank2 PMI SINR average shall be derived from rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers as follows:

if rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT is reset to Invalid value:

rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT = rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers**+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection -rrmPuschIrcGain (from the PUSCH receive request of slot N, cf. note2 )**

else

rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT = rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT * (1 - rdUlIrcGainBeta) + (rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers**+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection -rrmPuschIrcGain from the PUSCH receive request of slot N,** cf. Note2) * rdUlIrcGainBeta****

where

  * rdUlIrcGainBeta is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * rrmPuschIrcGain is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))




Long term averaged value is only updated when:

· VALID rank indication AND nonDTX have been received

· and lowest layer sinr of UlPmiRank2Sinr is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and highest layer sinr of UlPmiRank2Sinr is inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

· and absolute value of the SINR difference between the 2 layers of UlPmiRank2Sinr is strictly inferior to rdUlMaxSinrDiffLayers **(cf.** 5G_UP_ALG_24307_replaced([11141409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**.** ****

If all conditions above are satisfied, rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank2 is restarted once for a given PUSCH reception.

UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_22294_replaced([11140393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank2 (5G_UP_ALG_19684_replaced([11141342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires then rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT is reset to Invalid value (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_1746_replaced([11109764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7xC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT is used for PUSCH IRC gain (5G_UP_ALG_19670_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Note: rdIrcGainValidityTimerPuschRank2 is used because UlPmiRank1Sinr,UlPmiRank2Sinr are only measured when PUSCH rank2 is received.

Important Note2**:**

When rrmPuschIrcGain is capped to compute Pboost for a given PUSCH request (see 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the capped value (rdUlPuschIrcGainMax see 5G_UP_ALG_24309_replaced([11141429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3zPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) should be used here to uncompensate rank2PmiSinrPuschAv2layers from the corresponding PUSCH response.

**[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=shortTermDiff,**

rrmUlPmiRank2SinrPuschLT is not computed. **[End CB013202-C]**

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-13 L2 IRC gain estimation Long term average for uncompensated rank2 SRS PMI SINR (ID: 11140371)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-13.0-2**  (ID: `11140385`)

L2 IRC gain estimation [CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=longTermDiff, [End CB013202-C]

For any given UE,

1) depending on R&D parameter rdAverageBetween2LayersFromPusch (see 5G_L2_1455_replaced([11186237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_274HevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3084_replaced([11131461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall compute sinr average between layers of Rank2 transmissions (result is in dB scale) from SRS on slot P:

· rank2PmiSinrSrsAv2layers of the SINR parameter ‘UlPmiRank2Sinr[0][1]’ of the last SRS reception

2) a long-term uncompensated SRS rank2 PMI SINR shall be derived from rank2PmiSinrSrsAv2layers as follows:

if rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT is reset to Invalid value:

rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT = rank2PmiSinrSrsAv2layers+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection -rrmSrsIrcGain (from the SRS receive request of slot P, cf. note2)

else

rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT = rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT * (1 - rdUlIrcGainBeta) + (rank2PmiSinrSrsAv2layers+UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection -rrmSrsIrcGain from the SRS receive request of slot P, cf. note2 )* rdUlIrcGainBeta

where

  * rdUlIrcGainBeta is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * rrmSrsIrcGain is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19671_replaced([11140233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))




Long term averaged value is only updated when:

· nonDTX has been received

· and lowest layer sinr of UlPmiRank2Sinr is superior or equal to rdInstSinrMinForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24316_replaced([11141501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and highest layer sinr of UlPmiRank2Sinr is inferior or equal to rdInstSinrMaxForIrcGain (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24315_replaced([11141482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

· and absolute value of the SINR difference between the 2 layers of UlPmiRank2Sinr is strictly inferior to rdUlMaxSinrDiffLayers (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_24307_replaced([11141409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If all conditions above are satisfied, rdIrcGainValidityTimerSrs is restarted once for a given SRS reception.

UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_22294_replaced([11140393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If rdIrcGainValidityTimerSrs (5G_UP_ALG_19684_replaced([11141342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires then rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT is reset to Invalid value (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_1746_replaced([11109764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7xC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmUlPmiRank2SinrSrsLT is used for SRS IRC gain (5G_UP_ALG_19671_replaced([11140233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Important ,:

When powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe is capped to minimum or maximum value for a given SRS request, then rrmSrsIrcGainAfterCapping as per 5G_UP_ALG_10497_replaced([11119432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) should be used here to uncompensate the rank2PmiSinrSrsAv2layers from the corresponding SRS response.

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod=shortTermDiff,

Only change in this requirement compared to longTermDiff is that DU shall use rdUlIrcGainBetaMethod2( 5G_UP_ALG_30793_replaced([11141291](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in long term averaging instead of rdUlIrcGainBeta (5G_UP_ALG_19682_replaced([11141320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB013202-C]

##### 3.9.2.4.2.0-14 L2 IRC gain estimation UnlimitedPowerSinrCorrection (ID: 11140393)

**3.9.2.4.2.0-14.0-4**  (ID: `12697984`)

L2 IRC gain estimation Each short term sinr shall be corrected with the term below before long term average :

1) UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection = -1 * min(0, (rrmPathlossFactor - 10log10(numPrb)))

where **numPrb**

o For PUSCH, numPrb is the size of the PUSCH allocation ;

o For aperiodic SRS, numPrb is the number of PRBs used for the SRS ;

o For periodic SRS, numPrb is the number of PRBs of the previous PUSCH allocation, as the SRS measurements are already compensated to match that allocation (cf. 5G_UP_ALG_10497_replaced([11119432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This means that the same num of PRBs PUSCH which was used to compute SRS power offset in a given SRS receive request, must be used for UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection applied on ulPmiSinrs of the corresponding SRS receive response.

**and rrmPathlossFactor = min (rrmPhr + 10log10(numPuschPrbPhr) + mprPhr, 10 * log10(rrmMaxNumPrb))**

with

 **rrmPhr**

o is the latest PHR report,

 **numPuschPrbPhr**

o is the corresponding PRB number of the latest PHR report

 **rrmMaxNumPrb**

o Maximum number of PRBs available for PUSCH, wideband SRS in the particular bandwidth system (e.g. taking into account long PUCCH)

2) if (UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection **> 0) i.e. UE is power limited**

UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection = UnlimitedPwrSinrCorrection + MPR + DeltaMPR256QAM

where

 **DeltaMPR256QAM**

o if the R&D parameter rdMprQam256ActiveFddTdd (see 5G_L2_3347_replaced([11184869](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27uWcvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled for current technology and sinr or UlpmiRank1Sinr or UlpmiRank2Sinr comes from PUSCH and mcs>=20 (table 256QAM)

If UE is not configured with FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA

DeltaMPR256QAM = 3dB

else if UE is configured with FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA

if SCell with intra-band contiguous UL CA is deactivated or transmission buffer in UL is not split between PCell and SCell (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_10377_replaced([11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[Before PR840715]

DeltaMPR256QAM = 3dB for inner RB allocation for contiguous RB allocation and CA bandwidth class B.

DeltaMPR256QAM = 2dB for outer RB allocation for contiguous RB allocation and CA bandwidth class B.

DeltaMPR256QAM = 2dB for inner RB allocation for contiguous RB allocation and CA bandwidth class C.

DeltaMPR256QAM = 0 in all other cases.

note: see 3GPP TS38.101-1 section 6.2A.2 for the calculation rule to determine it's inner RB allocation or outer RB allocation for contiguous RB allocation and 3GPP TS38.101-1 section 5.3A.5 for CA bandwidth class.

[PR840715]

DeltaMPR256QAM = 3dB

[End PR840715]

else

DeltaMPR256QAM = 0

endif

endif

else

DeltaMPR256QAM = 0

endif

 **MPR or** mprPhr (depending on curent allocation i.e. PUSCH or SRS is received )****

If UE is not configured with FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA

If the R&D parameter rdMprActive (see 5G_L2_1371_replaced([11185224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27wysPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 1 or to 2 and for the deployment defined by rdMprActiveFddTdd

 MPR = rdMprFdd (see 5G_L2_1375_replaced([11185245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27wytPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if the allocation is greater than the bandwidth specific inner RB allocation in FDD deployment

 MPR = rdMprTddFr1 (see 5G_L2_1376_replaced([11185252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27wytfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if the allocation is greater than the bandwidth specific inner RB allocation in TDD FR1 deployment

 MPR = 0 in all other cases

else

MPR is always 0

endif

else if UE is configured with FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA

if (SCell with intra-band contiguous UL CA is deactivated or transmission buffer in UL is not split between PCell and SCell (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_10377_replaced([11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))))

MPR = rdMprFr1CCAConRbB (see 5G_UP_ALG_28222_replaced([11138943](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krjAKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for CA bandwidth class B, if the PUSCH allocation is outer RB allocation for contiguous RB allocation.

MPR = rdMprFr1CCAConRbC (see 5G_UP_ALG_28224_replaced([11138954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krjALPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for CA bandwidth class C, if the PUSCH allocation is outer RB allocation for contiguous RB allocation.

MPR = 0 in all other cases

else

MPR = 0

endif

endif

### 3.9.2.5 Rank computation on 1 layer transmissions

#### 3.9.2.5.0-1 Rank computation on 1 layer transmissions Aperiodic SRS transmission shall be requested by L2-PS for any transmission with rank 1. Triggering of the SRS transmission is not guaranteed. Aperiodic SRS transmission shall not be requested by L2-PS for single antenna transmission (singleTx). Aperiodic SRS transmission shall not be requested by L2-PS for PUSCH signal which will be scheduled in UL slots with PRACH configuration. (ID: 11140429)

### 3.9.2.6 PUSCH Transform Precoder

#### 3.9.2.6.0-1 PUSCH Transform Precoder Transform Precoder Specification Concept (ID: 12977638)

**3.9.2.6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12977637`)

PUSCH Transform Precoder 12977637: PUSCH Transform Precoder This artifact is an informative requirement in a cumulative module. It is not an official requirement.

This section covers how the gNB-DU supports PUSCH DFT-s-OFDM in the following ways:

DFT-s-OFDM usage for DCI 0_1 and DCI 0_0/Msg3

  * [CB008148-A] DFT-s-OFMD application to Msg3 and DCI 0_0, for ABIN and later baseband boards [End CB008148-A]
  * Semi-static transitions between DFT-s-OFDM and CP OFDM for data symbols of DCI 0_1 transmissions
  * [CB008148-B] With option for a TP On initial state [End CB008148-B]
  * Requirements for applying DFT-s-OFDM
  * Requirements for DMRS symbols with DFT-s-OFDM



For semi-static DFT-s-OFDM vs CP OFDM selection with DCI 0_1, the gNB-DU manages the PUSCH waveform state for a UE as summarized by the State Machine view below (note that this state machine view is a representation for ease of understanding and it is not a requirement for implementation).

Illustrative State Machine for Semi-Static PUSCH Transform Precoder Usage with DCI 0_1

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a state diagram illustrating different states and transitions related to TP (Transport Path) configurations and VoNR (Voice over NR) status. The diagram is divided into two main regions: "TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On" and "TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off". **States:** * **(1) Start:** The initial state of the system. * **(2) TP Off/On; Off:** Represents a state where TP is off/on and VoNR is off. * **(3) TP Off/On; On 64QAM:** Represents a state where TP is off/on, VoNR is on, and 64QAM is used. * **(4) TP Off/On; Off VoNR:** Represents a state where TP is off/on, VoNR is off. * **(5) TP Off/On; On 64QAM VoNR:** Represents a state where TP is off/on, VoNR is on, and 64QAM is used. **Transitions:** Transitions are indicated by arrows and labeled with event triggers or conditions. * **From (1) Start:** * `[0.1] PUSCH-Config sent to UE` leads to an unspecified state (represented by a dark blue circle). * `[1.3] Access mode (2)` leads to state (3). * `[1.5] Access mode (3)` leads to an unspecified state (represented by a dark blue circle). * `[1.2] Access Mode (1)` leads to state (2). * `[1.4] VoNR HO, SAg Off` leads to state (4). * **From (2) TP Off/On; Off:** * `[2.4] VoNR Add` leads to state (3). * `[2.5] VoNR Add CB9849-A` leads to state (4). * **From (3) TP Off/On; On 64QAM:** * `[3.5] VoNR Add` leads to state (5). * `[3.2] DU_trig_RRC_ReConfig [Good SINR, TP Off]. Only for non VoNR` leads to state (2). This transition is shown as a dashed line, indicating it might be conditional or a fallback. * **From (4) TP Off/On; Off VoNR:** * `[4.2] VoNR Release` leads to state (2). * `[4.5] DU_trig_RRC_ReConfig [Bad SINR, TP On]` leads to state (3). This transition is shown as a dashed line. * **From (5) TP Off/On; On 64QAM VoNR:** * `[5.3] VoNR Release` leads to state (3). * `[5.4] DU_trig_RRC_ReConfig [Good SINR, TP Off] + nonVonr If CB9849-A` leads to state (4). This transition is shown as a dashed line. **Regions:** * **TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On:** This region encloses states (3) and (5). * **TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off:** This region encloses states (2) and (4). The diagram uses different line styles (solid and dashed) and colors (green for states 3 and 5, pink for states 2 and 4, blue for the start state and other unspecified states) to differentiate elements. The dashed lines likely represent conditional or less direct transitions.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-12042129.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Diagram notes:

  * Access Mode (1): Init Access, HO, RRE
  * Access Mode (2): CNI-108979, CB008148 Init Access, HO, RRE
  * Access Mode (3): VoNR HO: CB009849-A, CNI-108979 TP On at Source & SAg disabled at target & CB009849-A disabled



The states define the following:

  * TP state for DCI 0_0: It is static (either On or Off per OAM configuration), managed separately from DCI 0_1
  * TP state for DCI 0_1: semi-static based on a L2-PS specific SINR metric
  * VoNR or no VoNR DRB: impacts TP state selection
  * MCS table for TP On: default TP-specific 64QAM



The main, higher level, states are TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On and TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off. Each of these states have substates with arbitrary numbers assigned to them for ease of reference. All transitions shown are between substates.

State references to TP 0_0 On/Off and sub state references to TP On/Off; indicate that TP state for DCI 0_0 is selected in a static manner at OAM, independently of state/sub state for DCI _01.

The following table tracks all the substate transitions, with additional details added. The table also identifies which transitions are covered by requirements in this section.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
Out Transition | From State | From Sub-State | To State | To Sub-State | Trigger | RRC Procedure within Transition | NIDD Activation  
1.2 | UE_Setup | UE Setup | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off No VoNR | Init Access,HO,RRE | RRC Setup + ReConfiguration, HO Exec | actUlDftSOfdm, actUlTransPreUsageEnh = 'Disabled'  
1.3 | UE_Setup | UE Setup | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM No VoNR | CB8148.1.2.A Init Access/RRE/HO, CB9849-A HO | RRC Setup + ReConfiguration, HO Exec | [CB008148-B]actUlTransPreUsageEnh = 'DCI01_TpOnOff_StartTpOn'[End CB008148-B]; actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl=true  
1.4 | UE_Setup | UE Setup | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off VoNR | VoNR HO | HO Exec | actEnhancedVoNR=true  
1.5 | UE_Setup | UE Setup | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM VoNR | CB9849-A: VoNR HO/RRE, CNI-108979 HO | HO Exec | actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl=true; actUlTransPreEnhHo=true  
2.3 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off No VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM No VoNR | TP Off to TP On for DCI 0_1 | gNB-DU triggered RRC ReConfig | actUlDftSOfdm = true  
2.4 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off No VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off VoNR | VoNR Add | RRC ReConfigs for DRB Add and DRx Profile change | actEnhancedVoNR=true  
2.5 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off No VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM VoNR | VoNR Add | RRC ReConfigs for DRB Add and DRx Profile change | actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl=true; actUlTransPreEnhHo=true  
3.2 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM No VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off No VoNR | TP On to TP Off for DCI 0_1 | gNB-DU triggered RRC ReConfig | actUlDftSOfdm = true  
3.5 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM No VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM VoNR | VoNR Add | RRC ReConfigs for DRB Add and DRX Profile change | actUlDftSOfdm=true, actEnhancedVoNR=true  
4.2 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off No VoNR | VoNR Release | RRC ReConfigs for DRB Release and DRx Profile change | actEnhancedVoNR=true  
4.5 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM VoNR | TP Off to TP On for DCI 0_1 | gNB-DU triggered RRC ReConfig | actUlDftSOfdm = true  
5.3 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM No VoNR | VoNR Release | RRC ReConfigs for DRB Add and DRX Profile change | actUlDftSOfdm=true, actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl=true  
5.4 | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On | TP On 64QAM VoNR | TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off | TP Off VoNR | TP On to TP Off for DCI 0_1 | gNB-DU triggered RRC ReConfig | actUlDftSOfdm = true  
  
There are other requirements throughout the L2-RT outside of this section addressing PUSCH DFT-s-OFDM when associated to a requirement’s particular function. Examples of L2-PS requirement areas with DFT-s-OFDM content (not meant as an exhaustive list):

  * PUSCH Slot Aggregation for VoNR (SAg)
  * CG Type 2
  * Basic vs High Reliability UL LA
  * SINR-to-MCS tables for UL ILLA
  * UL SU MIMO
  * UCI on PUSCH
  * Adaptive Re-transmissions
  * UL throughput pooling
  * UL TBS calculation



Notes:

  * Aspects of TP On for Msg3 and DCI 0_0, plus always starting at TP On state are only applicable for L2-PS NewFR1
  * Equivalent terminology within L2-RT SFS when relative to PUSCH waveform:
  * DFT-s-OFDM = Transform Precoder enabled = TP On
  * CP OFDM = Transform Precoder disabled = TP Off
  * Note: Other parts of L2-RT SFS may use the TP acronym to mean something else when content is not related to PUSCH waveform
  * Terminology throughout 5G UP Algorithms module:
  * If PUSCH DFT-s-OFDM is "enabled" or Transform Precoder is enabled means the following unless explicitly stated otherwise:
    1. ​​​​​​​NRCELL. actUlDftSOfdm = true as a prerequisite, with other related activation flags adding to that if not disabled (such as NRCELL.actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl and NRCELLactUlTransPreUsageEnh)
  * ​​​​​​​[Before CB008148-A-UPD006]If UE has Transform Precoder (or words to that effect): UE has been configured for PUSCH Transform Precoder at RRC layer because Transform Precoder is enabled and UE meets applicable criteria (such as SINR condition, Slot Aggregation condition, TP On always for VoNR, etc.)
    1. If NRCELLactUlTransPreUsageEnh is set to 'Disabled', this applies only for PUSCH transmissions associated with DCI 0_1. [CB008148-A] Else it may apply to Msg3 and DCI 0_0 transmissions depending on NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh (this parameter is a multi-valued enumerated parameter)[CB008148-A-UPD006] actMsg3TP [End CB008148-A]



[End CB008148-A-UPD006]

  * In the event of a conflict between this informative artifact and a Requirement artifact, the Requirement artifact shall govern
  * VoNR is this context means a UE configured with a 5QI-1,-65, or -66 DRB
  * The diagram above does not show a complete system level view as it excludes Slot Aggregation aspects
  * The diagram can be found at SPOL link:



File: aTpUsageModeDiagrams_v0.pptx

#### 3.9.2.6.0-2 PUSCH Transform Precoder UE Eligibility for Transform Precoder (ID: 11140454)

**3.9.2.6.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13133995`)

PUSCH Transform Precoder [CB008148-B]The gNB-DU shall consider a UE eligible for PUSCH Transform Precoder based on indication from L3 at UE setup when NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh is not set to 'disabled'[End CB008148-B]

Notes:

  * [CB008148-B] TP On for DCI 0_1
  * If NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains ‘DCI01_TpOnOff_StartTpOn' the initial state for TP On/Off state switching is per ( [11140543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZEp5sPvLEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) ) [End CB008148-B]
  * [CB008148-A]TP On for Msg3
  * CP-RT indicates that this TP usage mode is activated at cell setup [Before CB008148-A-UPD006]/ reconfiguration (NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains ‘Msg3_TPOn’ )[CB008148-A-UPD006] based on NRCELL.actMsg3TP [End CB008148-A-UPD006]
    * Note: Assumption is that all UEs support it. There are older commercial UEs which do not support PUSCH Transform Precoder at all. Operators are strongly encouraged not to enable this TP usage mode if such UEs are present in their network
  * TP On for DCI 0_0
  * CP-RT indicates that this TP usage mode is activated for new UEs at cell setup [Before CB008148-A-UPD006]/ reconfiguration (NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains ‘DCI00_TPOn’ )[CB008148-A-UPD006] based on NRCELL.actMsg3TP [End CB008148-A-UPD006]
    * CP-RT indicates that specific UE supports Transform Precoding at user setup as CP has to configure UE for it at RRC layer in a static manner[End CB008148-A]

#### 3.9.2.6.1 Transform Precoder for Msg3 and DCI 0_0

##### 3.9.2.6.1.0-1 Transform Precoder for Msg3 and DCI 0_0 Transform Precoder for RA-Msg3 (ID: 11140441)

**3.9.2.6.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12977639`)

Transform Precoder for Msg3 and DCI 0_0 The gNB-DU shall request L1 to decode Msg3 transmissions with a PUSCH waveform as defined below:

  * [CB008148-A] If [Before CB008148-A-UPD006] NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains enumerated value 'Msg3_TPOn' [CB008148-A-UPD006] NRCELL.actMsg3TP = TRUE [End CB008148-A-UPD006] 
  * TP ON (DFT-s-OFDM) 
    * pi/2-BPSK is not supported.
    * For SA or SA + NSA modes: UEs are informed of TP On for Msg3 in SIB1. [Before CB008148-A-UPD006] OAM parameter actUlTransPreUsageEnh is online modifiable. Therefore, gNB-DU must wait to apply change like any other SIB1 related change (wait until 3rd SIB1 Modification Period)[End CB008148-A-UPD006]
    * Note: [Before CB008148-A-UPD006] actUlTransPreUsageEnh can only contain value 'Msg3_TPOn' for base band boards ABIN or later[End CB008148-A-UPD006]



[End CB008148-A]

  * Else 
  * TP Off (CP OFDM)



Above applies for both initial and HARQ re-transmissions of Msg3 and for both CBRA and CFRA.

Default 64QAM table (TP-specific in case of TP On) is used in all cases 

Notes:

  * There is no guarantee that all UEs support DFT-S-OFDM (although vast majority do), and no way for L2-PS to know which UEs do or don’t before Msg3. If gNB guesses incorrectly then UE cannot connect. Operator is warned in CuDo not to set [Before CB008148-A-UPD006]actUlTransPreUsageEnh to contain 'Msg3_TPOn' CB008148-A-UPD006] NRCELL.actMsg3TP = TRUE [End CB008148-A-UPD006] when aware that their network has older devices which do not support PUSCH DFT-s-OFDM.
  * [Before CB008148-A-UPD006]A UE can be configured with TP On for Msg3 independently of TP for DCI 0_0 and DCI 0_1[End CB008148-A-UPD006]
