##### 3.9.2.6.1.0-2 Transform Precoder for Msg3 and DCI 0_0 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_0 (ID: 12977641)

**3.9.2.6.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12977644`)

Transform Precoder for Msg3 and DCI 0_0 The gNB-DU shall request L1 to decode DCI 0_0 related PUSCH transmissions with a PUSCH waveform as defined below. [Before CB008148-A-UPD001] Coordination between L2-PS and L3 is required to make sure of alignment between L1 and UE on PUSCH waveform.

  * If NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains enumerated value ' Dci00_TPOn' but not 'Msg3_TPOn'
  * TP On (DFT-s-OFDM)
    * This is applicable only for DCI 0_0 transmissions after RRC Setup message is sent to UE.
    * After dedicated BWP configuration, If the UE has been configured for pi/2-BPSK (indication from L3 at UE setup) then decode request to L1 must identify pi/2-BPSK for used UL MCS 0 or 1.
  * ElseIf NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains enumerated values ' Dci00_TPOn' and 'Msg3_TPOn'
  * TP On (DFT-s-OFDM) 
    * Due to msg3-transformPrecoder = enabled present in SIB1, TP On applies to all DCI 0_0 transmissions for all UEs, starting with first DCI 0_0 (until L3 tells a specific UE otherwise in a subsequent RRC message). 
    * It cannot have pi/2-BPSK until UE is configured with a dedicated BWP (no way in 3GPP to tell UE to use pi/2-BPSK until then)
    * After dedicated BWP configuration, If the UE has been configured for pi/2-BPSK (indication from L3 at UE setup) then decode request to L1 must identify pi/2-BPSK for used UL MCS 0 or 1.
  * Else 
  * TP Off (CP OFDM)



Above applies for both initial and HARQ re-transmissions of DCI 0_0.

Default 64QAM MCS table (TP-specific in case of TP On) is used in all cases

Notes: 

  * actUlTransPreUsageEnh can only contain value ' Dci00_TPOn' for base band boards ABIN or later
  * A UE can be configured with TP On for DCI 0_0 independently of TP for DCI 0_1
  * UEs are informed of TP On for DCI 0_0 by the msg3-transformPrecoder field set to enabled within RRC IE RACH-CommonConfig. This IE can appear in RRC DL messages to a dedicated UE. It can also appear in SIB1 for all UEs but msg3-transformPrecoder = enabled will occur only when actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains 'Msg3_TPOn'
  * Once UE has dedicated BWP, it will honor the tp-pi2-bpsk field in PUSCH-Config IE for both DCI 0_1 and DCI 0_0 (only if both configured for TP On). L3 will include this field only if NRCELL.ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodePi2Bpsk=true and UE Capabilities indicate support (L3 sends indication to L2-PS at UE setup).
  * If NRBTS.actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom=TRUE, there is no transient phase with forced DCI 0_0 scheduling for a User ReConfiguration procedure



[CB008148-A-UPD001]

  * TP On indicator from L3 at User Setup
  * Set to TRUE:
    * TP On (DFT-s-OFDM)
  * Set to FALSE
    * TP Off (CP OFDM)
  * Not present:
    * Follow TP setting for Msg3:
  * TP On indicator from L3 at 1st User Modify:
  * Set to TRUE:
    * TP On (DFT-s-OFDM)
  * Set to FALSE:
    * TP Off (CP OFDM)



[PR877949]

Related settings for TP On:

  * Target BLER: 10% regardless of UL LA mode, for all DCI 0_0 related transmissions including in reconfiguration transient phase (note that UL LA mode for UE is not changed)



[End PR877949]

Notes:

  * [PR880889] Scheduling constraint for FORCED_DCI_00 with TP On AND Pi-2BPSK is specified by {[13481602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_NtuEwD5eEfG0jPRAdLhzvA) }[End PR880889]
  * This requirement applies to all configured UL dedicated BWPs. It applies to Initial Access, HO, and RRE.
  * Above applies for both initial and HARQ re-transmissions of DCI 0_0.
  * Default 64QAM MCS table (TP-specific in case of TP On) is used in all cases
  * L3 configures TP state for UE at RRC layer based on content of [Before CB008148-A-UPD006] NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh [CB008148-A-UPD006] NRCELL.actMsg3TP [End CB008148-A-UPD006]
  * [Before CB008148-A-UPD006] Contains ' Dci00_TPOn'[CB008148-A-UPD006] set to TRUE[End CB008148-A-UPD006] : 
    * [Before CB008148-A-UPD006] L3 will set TP On at 1st DL SRB message of a RRC access procedure, if it can. Else, it will wait for next DL SRB message to do so. L3 indicates how UE was configured to L2-PS with three possible values: Present Indication = TRUE (TP On), Present Indication = FALSE (TP Off), Indication not present (follow TP setting for Msg3, which depends on whether NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains ' Msg3_TPOn')[End CB008148-A-UPD006] :
  * L3 can only configure a UE with pi/2-BPSK within an UL dedicated BWP configuration. Whether this applies to DCI 0_0 depends on whether DCI 0_0 is sent on a dedicated BWP (not on whether PUSCH Tx is sent in initial or dedicated BWP PRB region but whether it is transmitted on a dedicated BWP. L2-PS follows the pi/2-BPSK indication sent at User Setup for any subsequent use of TP On on a dedicated BWP (DCI 0_0 or DCI 0_1)
  * [Before CB008148-A-UPD006] actUlTransPreUsageEnh can only contain value ' Dci00_TPOn' for base band boards ABIN or later[End CB008148-A-UPD006]
  * A UE can be configured with TP On for [CB008148-A-UPD006] Msg3 and [End CB008148-A-UPD006] DCI 0_0 independently of TP for DCI 0_1
  * When NRCELL.actSmallestRRCSetup = true, L3 can not configure TP state for a UE in a RRC Setup message
  * NRBTS.actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom=true, there is no transient phase with forced DCI 0_0 scheduling for a User ReConfiguration procedure. Only DCI 0_1 is used while waiting for a RRC ReConfigurationComplete indication.
  * DCI for Msg5 may vary. If actCbraContResDCI00 = true, DCI 0_0 is used (else DCI 0_1 is used)
  * [Before CB008148-A-UPD006] An online change of NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh only applies to new UEs.[CB008148-A-UPD006]NRCELL.actMsg3TP has a cell reset modification mode to avoid TP state ambiguity between new and existing UEs for an online change[End CB008148-A-UPD006]



[End CB008148-A-UPD001]

---

#### 3.9.2.6.2 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1

##### 3.9.2.6.2.0-1 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 Transform Precoder Selection (ID: 11140467)

**3.9.2.6.2.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `13133998`)

Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 The gNB-DU shall semi-statically switch a UE’s PUSCH waveform between TP On and TP Off for DCI 0_1 transmissions as described below.

  * UE Eligibility: UE is eligible for dynamic UL waveform switching per 5G_UP_ALG_3265_replaced([11140454](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * Applicability: All of UE's PUSCH transmissions associated with DCI 0_1
  * Exceptions:
  * If UE has a VoNR (5QI-1 or 5QI65/66) DRB and UE is PUSCH slot aggregation eligible, then 5G-L2-PS shall select the UL waveform per ([11204759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * For a UE with Configured grant type 2, execution of a Transform Precoder (TP) transition is evaluated (i.e. it's checked if it's allowed) in accordance to ([11173226](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuSLEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl set to TRUE:
    * If UE has a 5QI1 or 5QI65/66 DRB configured (i.e after User setup/modification complete to add a 5QI1 or 5QI65/66 DRB is received), UL waveform is set as DFT-s-OFDM (Transform precoder enabled). After the last 5QI1 or 5QI65/66 DRB is released, the gNB-DU shall dynamically switch a UE’s PUSCH waveform between CP OFDM (Transform Precoder disabled) and DFT-s-OFDM (Transform Precoder enabled) as described in the state machine defined below.
  * State machine description:



[CB008148-B]The informative diagram in ([12977638](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_9ECYELXZEfCQT7hYUxERAg)) illustrates semi-static TP On/Off switching for DCI 0_1.[End CB008148-B]

  * State Machine start: Initial state determined at user setup. Dynamic state transitions begin after user setup.
  * Applicable UL DCIs: The state machine applies for changing Transform Precoder setting associated with DCI 0_1 transmissions.
  * Initial State: Selection between TP 0_0 OFF & 0_1 ON and TP 0_0 OFF & 0_1 OFF after UE Setup is as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3272_replaced([11140543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krumVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * State Definitions: 
  * states are defined in ([11140586](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krumWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * **TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off** state is defined by the same UL waveform behavior applicable when the PUSCH DFT-s-OFDM feature is disabled.
  * UE Setup here means UE Context setup and procedure through MSG3/MSG5
  * Determine TP Init State is as described in ([11140543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krumVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * Transitions
  * Definitions: Transition triggers, and associated event monitoring are defined by ([11140818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * Actions: Actions taken during transitions are defined by ([11140818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * Stay in current state: The UE's Transform Precoder state stays the same after the following events:
  * Bearer Add/Modify/Release
  * UL Scell addition or release
  * Internal User Modify procedure failure.
  * onLine modification of NRCELL.actUlDftSOfdm
  * [CB008148-B]onLine modification of NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh relating to 'DCI01_TpOnOff_StartTpOn' 
    * For onLine modification of NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh to containing 'DCI01_noTpOffToOn, if UE was in a TP Off state, it stays there per exception specified in ([11140818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If UE was in TP On state, it stays there until algorithm triggers a change to TP Off.[End CB008148-B]
  * State entry actions:
  * Upon entry to Transform Precoder Enabled state after transition from Transform Precoder Disabled state: Resume using the UL rank stored at the beginning of the transition.



Notes:

  * [CB008148-B]Items related to NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh are not supported in ABIL[End CB008148-B]

---

##### 3.9.2.6.2.0-2 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 Initial Transform Precoder State (ID: 11140543)

**3.9.2.6.2.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `12977646`)

Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 The gNB-DU shall select the initial Transform Precoder state for PUSCH transmissions with DCI 0_1 as follows::

  * L2-PS Based Decision:
  * For Initial Access:
    * If NRCELL.actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is true AND the UE is configured for a 'VoNR DRB', then the state is TP On
    * [CB008148-B] ElseIf, when the NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh parameter contains the 'DCI01_TpOnOff_StartTpOn' enumerated value, then the state shall be TP On  
Note: This is applicable only for baseband boards ABIN or later.[End CB008148-B]
    * Else, the state is TP Off
  * L3 Based Decision:
  * Follow indication from L3 intended for HO or RRE target cell.



[CB008148-B-UPD005] Follow the decisions above, even if UE starts with or adds a DRB which is associated to NRBTS/NRPDSCHHRLA.nrPdschHRLaDN or NRBTS/NRPUSCHHRLA.nrPuschHRLaDN per ([11125162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_CympYPvKEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB008148-B-UPD005]

Notes:

  * System level point of view:
  * For Handover (HO):
    * If the target cell's NRCELL.actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is true AND the UE is configured for a 'VoNR DRB', then the state is TP On.
    * [CB008148-B]Else If the target cell's NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh parameter contains the 'DCI01_TpOnOff_StartTpOn' enumerated value, then the state is 'TP On, regardless of the source cell TP state.
    * Note: This setting overrides the NRCELL.ulTransPreEnhHo parameter.[End CB008148-B]
    * Else If, when the target cell's NRCELL.ulTransPreEnhHo parameter is true, then the gNB-DU shall maintain the TP state from the source cell as indicated by L3 signaling (i.e., TP On remains TP On, and TP Off remains TP Off).
    * Else, the state is TP Off
  * [CB008148-B] For RRC Re-Establishment (RRE):
    * If the target cell's NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh parameter contains the 'DCI01_TpOnOff_StartTpOn' enumerated value, then the state is TP On, regardless of the source cell TP state.[End CB008148-B]
    * Else, the state is TP Off
  * [CB008148-B-UPD005] Interaction with HR UL LA mode:
  * When a UE is configured at RRC with a 64QAM LowSE table in support of HR, it is for CP OFDM and not DFT-s-OFDM (TP On)
  * Preference for starting with TP On for DCI 0_1 (if selected) over HR mode. UE can “recover” HR per ([11138358](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_NoBeUPvLEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) once UE is switched to TP Off. [End CB008148-B-UPD005]

---

##### 3.9.2.6.2.0-3 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 Transform Precoder While in a State Transition (ID: 11140653)

**3.9.2.6.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12977650`)

Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 The gNB-DU shall support, as follows, PUSCH scheduling during the transient phase of a User Reconfiguration procedure triggered for changing the UE's Transform Precoder state, per ([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Yx1rYPvLEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) ) for DCI 0_1 TP On/Off switching when NRBTS.actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom = False 

  * If NRBTS.actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom = false:
  * The DCI allowed, MCS used for TBS calculation, max PRB allocation, number of layers, dmrs-AdditionalPosition, and number of CDM groups without data (nb_cdm_no_data) shall be per ([11203479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfKhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))



[PR877697]

  * When a UE has TP On for DCI 0_0 or starts on TP On for DCI 0_1 [Before CB008148-A-UPD006]due to NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh setting (not 'disabled')[End CB008148-A-UPD006]:
  * TP related details on decode request for a PUSCH transmissions associated with a HARQ process started before the transient phase follow those of the corresponding grant.
  * Note: This is in regard to inital Tx with a sufficiently large K2 value (like for aCSI request in a DCI 0_1 grant) such that grant was sent prior to transient phase but actual transmission lands within transient phase. Only DCI 0_0 grants initiated during transient phase will follow the NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEn setting.



[End PR877697]

  * If NRBTS.actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom = true, there is no reconfiguration transient phase and DCI 0_1 is used for scheduling (if needed) while reconfiguration procedure is ongoing and this requirement does not apply.

---

##### 3.9.2.6.2.0-4 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 Triggers for Changing from TP Disabled to TP Enabled (ID: 11140672)

**3.9.2.6.2.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `11140743`)

Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 11140743: Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 **{ Requirement Refactoring } This requirement is being superceeded in 24R3 by refactoring under CNI-108976. It is replaced by 5G_UP_ALG_26586_replaced([11140818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_26588_replaced([11140853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0dvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **{ Requirement Refactoring }**_* L2-PS shall trigger transition to Transform Precoder enable state when rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch is lower than rrmThresholdTpOn for N consecutive observation periods; where: Applicability: * Incrementing counter N due to comparisons of rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch to rrmThresholdTpOn (for Transform Precoder Disable to Transform Precoder Enable state) and to rrmThresholdTpOff (for Transform Precoder Enable to Transform Precoder Disable) are started whenever a UE enters either TP ON or TP OFF state_ *[Before CNI-108786]** Exceptions: * Incrementing counter N due to comparisons of rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch to rrmThresholdTpOn (described in 5G_UP_ALG_3280_replaced([11140653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krvNY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and to rrmThresholdTpOff (described in 5G_UP_ALG_3284_replaced([11140751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krvNbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are suspended while in the transient phase of the User ReConfiguration procedure for either a Transform Precoder Disable to Transform Precoder Enable or a Transform Precoder Enable to Transform Precoder Disable transition. Exception: If UE is SAg Eligible per 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **and has a 5QI-1 DRB, then trigger transition per 5G_UP_ALG_19242_replaced([11204811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** **[CNI-108786]** Exceptions: * Incrementing counter N due to comparisons of rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch to rrmThresholdTpOn: \+ Is suspended while in the transient phase of the User ReConfiguration procedure for any User ReConfiguration procedure. \+ Is suspended while UE is in UL Rank 2 (as evaluated in if CNI-108786 is enabled (NRCELL/ulTransPreEnhRankIwk = true), This means that UE must be in Rank 1 first before UE can be switched to Transform Precoder Enabled state * Trigger mechanism for SAg: If UE is SAg Eligible per 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and has a 5QI-1 DRB, then trigger transition per 5G_UP_ALG_19242_replaced([11204811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) * For a UE configured with UL CA on Scell, once the activation status defined by 5G_UP_ALG_2804_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) changes to "inactive" from "active" on the Scell, the counter for SINR observation shall be reset to 0. **[End CNI-108786]** rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch = rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb + rrmOffsetTpSwitch ; where: * If PUSCH is in Rank_2 and PUSCH PRBs <= SRS PRBs and SINR source for Rank_1 is SRS (5G_UP_ALG_3081_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): \+ rrmOffsetTpSwitch = 10 * log( rrmMaxSinrPrbs / rrmMinSinrPrbs ) + 3 dB * Else: \+ rrmOffsetTpSwitch = 0 Applicability of rrmOffsetTpSwitch : non-zero rrmOffsetTpSwitch is applied only while in UL rank2 Definitions: * N = rdTransPrecodeHystThresh (5G_L2_1459_replaced([11186412](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_275VmvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and "observation periods" refers to SINR measurements * rrmMaxSinrPrbs = max (next PUSCH PRB, SRS PRB) * rrmMinSinrPrbs = min (next PUSCH PRB, SRS PRB) * rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb is derived from rrmRescaledCorrAvgSinr per 5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced([11131515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), re-corrected as needed by either UL FDM (if active) for evaluated number of PRBs or DFT-S-OFDM maximum allowed PRBs less than maximum number of PRBs allowed by bandwith * rrmThresholdTpOn = \+ MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/_ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThresh_ _[CB007103-A] + rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset_ _[End CB007103-A] for non-RedCap UEs;_**_* \+ MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/_ ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThrRedCap ****[CB009568-B] + rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset**[End CB009568-B] for RedCap UEs** _*_** \- **[CB007103-A] Where rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset is set to rdUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshR16DmrsOffset (see 5G_UP_ALG_22800_replaced([11141650](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) if UE is configured as R16 DMRS for transform precoding (dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding-r16 is present in RRC setup/reconfiguration), set to 0 otherwise. **[End CB007103-A]**__Notes: * In Rank2, SINR is 3dB less than for Rank1 so rrmOffsetTpSwitch is further adjusted by 3dB to further reduce chances of UL waveform switching ping-pong * If CB006086 is enabled, the SINR source for Rank_1 can still be SRS : it happens when UL waveform switch from CP-OFDM to DFT-s-OFDM occurs before change of number of SRS ports * The rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb metric may be used by other functions besides PUSCH waveform switching between CP OFDM and DFT-S-OFDM. The rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch metric is exclusive for PUSCH waveform switching and it is not used for link adaptation * PUSCH PRB <= SRS PRB applies when wideband SRS is used and can lead to rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb with Rank1 and DFT-S-OFDM being much larger than rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb with Rank2 prior to switch to DFT-S-OFDM. This causes UL waveform switching ping-pongs because rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb is immediately above NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeOffSinrThresh. Using rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch (which has a positive offset in Rank2), means that when switch to DFT-S-OFDM occurs while UE is in Rank2 the value of rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch remains bellow NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeOffSinrThresh once in DFT-S-OFDM. * If UL SINR source is RANK_1_SRS (TDD FR1, NRBTS/NRCELL-ulSinrSourceForRank1SuMimo=0, and ulPmiRank1Sinr from SRS is NOT DTX) or If UL SINR source is RANK_1_SINGLE_TX : {FDD or (TDD FR1, NRBTS/NRCELL-ulSinrSourceForRank1SuMimo=1 or NRBTS/NRCELL-ulSinrSourceForRank1SuMimo=0 and SRS is DTX)}, rrmOffsetTpSwitch = 0 (offset is not needed) * Supported RedCap UE has only single transmit antenna configuration and is power-limited comparing to non-RedCap UE (20 dBm vs 23 dBm), thus dedicated parameter: MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/_ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThrRedCap is introduced to allow different configuration strategies for RedCap and non-RedCap UEs._ * In diagram below, TP = Transform Precoder * There are two strategies for setting NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThresh, which is the parameter controlling when a UE is configured for DFT-s-OFDM: \+ If the goal is to keep cell DFT-s-OFDM usage ratio down (focus on UEs at cell edge) and interest is on feature benefit for low resource usage UEs (like for VoNR UEs), then ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThresh should be set to a low value. For example, ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThresh equal to -8dB would result in a cell DFT-s-OFDM usage ratio of about 20% or less. The KPI NR_1470a (5G Ratio of PDUs using DFT-s-OFDM in uplink) is an example of a cell level DFT-s-OFDM usage ratio affected by setting of ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThresh. \+ If goal is to provide benefit of DFT-s-OFDM for high resource usage UEs (high data transfer), then ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThresh can be set to higher values such as default of 1.5dB or values recommended by Golden SCF. [image-0][image_desc]The image is a graph illustrating a signal over time, with different regions labeled "TP Disabled" and "TP Enabled". The graph shows a blue line representing a signal that fluctuates over time. A dashed blue line indicates a threshold labeled "rrmThresholdTpOn". In the "TP Disabled" region, the signal starts high, peaks, and then dips below the threshold, exhibiting several oscillations. Several green upward-pointing arrows are shown below the signal in this region, indicating some event or measurement. Before the UE is reconfigured from CP-OFDM to DFT-s-OFDM L2-PS shall start monitoring the UL channel as above while UE is in BR mode in order to switch from CP-OFDM (Transform Precoder disable state) to DFT-s-OFDM(Transform Precoder enable state).

##### 3.9.2.6.2.0-5 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 Triggers for Changing from TP Enabled to TP Disabled (ID: 11140751)

**3.9.2.6.2.0-5.0-5**  (ID: `11140812`)

Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 11140812: Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 **{ Requirement Refactoring } This requirement is being superceeded in 24R3 by refactoring under CNI-108976. It is replaced by 5G_UP_ALG_26586_replaced([11140818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_26588_replaced([11140853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0dvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **{ Requirement Refactoring }****

L2-PS shall trigger a transition to Transform Precoder disable state when rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch is higher than rrmThresholdTpOff for N consecutive observation periods; where:

Applicability:

  * Incrementing counter N due to comparisons of rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch to rrmThresholdTpOn (for Transform Precoder Disable to Transform Precoder Enable state) and to rrmThresholdTpOff (for Transform Precoder Enable to Transform Precoder Disable) are started whenever a UE enters either TP ON or TP OFF state



Exceptions:

  * Incrementing counter N due to comparisons of rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch to rrmThresholdTpOff (described in 5G_UP_ALG_3284_replaced([11140751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krvNbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is suspended while in the transient phase of any User ReConfiguration procedure.
  * If UE is SAg Eligible per 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and has a 5QI-1 DRB, then trigger transition per 5G_UP_ALG_19242_replaced([11204811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * For a UE configured with UL CA on Scell, once the activation status defined by 5G_UP_ALG_2804_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) changes to "inactive" from "active" on the Scell, the counter for SINR observation shall be reset to 0.



rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch = rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb + rrmOffsetWaveformSw; where:

Definitions:

  * N = rdTransPrecodeHystThresh (5G_L2_1459_replaced([11186412](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_275VmvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and "observation periods" refers to SINR measurements
  * Definition and applicability for rrmOffsetWaveformSw is defined by 5G_UP_ALG_3282_replaced([11140672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krvNZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). In a transition to TP disabled schenario, rrmOffsetWaveformSw = 0 both before and after transition because of only Rank1
  * rrmThresholdTpOff =
  * MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/_ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOffSinrThresh_ _[CB007103-A] + rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset_ _[End CB007103-A] for non-RedCap UEs;_ ****
  * MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/_ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOffSinrThrRedCap_ _[CB009568-B] + rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset_ _[End CB009568-B] for RedCap UEs_ ****
    * **_*[CB007103-A] Where rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset is set to rdUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshR16DmrsOffset (see 5G_UP_ALG_22802_replaced([11141661](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if UE is configured as R16 DMRS for transform precoding (dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding-r16 is present in RRC setup/reconfiguration), set to 0 otherwise. Note: 5G-CP-RT would already configure transform precoding parameters (e.g. R15 or R16 DMRS) to UE and 5G-L2-PS, even before transform precoding is activated (which is signalled seperately via RRC reconfiguration). _*[End CB007103-A]******



Notes

  * UE is restricted to Rank1 while using DFT-S-OFDM. Upon switch back to CP OFDM, Rank1 is used right after transition (see 5G_UP_ALG_3270_replaced([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Normal rank selection then resumes.

##### 3.9.2.6.2.0-6 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 Transform Precoder State Transition Triggers (ID: 11140818)

Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 12977655: Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 The gNB-DU shall trigger transitions out of Transform Precoder states within the PUSCH Transform Precoder state machine defined at ([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) per the description below: * Exceptions for all transitions: If UE is SAg Eligible per ([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and has a 5QI-1 or 5QI65/66 DRB, UL waveform transitions are managed per ([11204811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) * Transitions: \+ TP Off to TP On: From TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off to TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On . \- Preconditions: * NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlDftSOfdm = true (even if L3 indicates UE support for Transform Precoder at UE setup/reconfiguration) * If UE has a HR DRB ([11125150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsrnPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ([11125162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsrnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then it must be in BR mode. only PUSCH DTX has been received since last decoded SR(s) (ie N > 0 in rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch is lower than rrmThresholdTpOn for rrmTpOnHystThreshold consecutive monitored events * Hysteresis: Keep a count of times rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch meets the threshold condition. \+ Reset rrmTpOnHystThreshold * Exceptions: \+ If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl set to TRUE and UE has a 5QI1 DRB configured \- Actions: * During transition: \+ If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to FALSE, OR (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND 5QI1 DRB is not configured for the UE) \- Start a "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure to change Transform Precoder state at RRC layer. * Requests transformPrecoderInd = enabled in the reconfiguration required message \+ Else if actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl set to TRUE and UE has a 5QI1 DRB configured \- Select the TP 0_0 OFF & 0_1 ON state defined in ([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) * State Exit: From Transport Precoder disabled state. \+ Interworking with Number of SRS ports: \- If SRS Port Switching is active for FDD/TDD FR1 (NRBTS\actCoverageNonCoherentUes = true) and UE is noncoherent: * Save current rank and current number of SRS ports. \- Failure: UE is returned to Transform Precoder Disabled state upon any gNB internal failure for the "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure * TP On to TP Off : TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 On to TP 0_0 On/Off & 0_1 Off \+ Monitored events: \- rrmTpOffHystThreshold \- Exceptions: * If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl set to TRUE, Metric comparison is not done, when UE is configured with 5QI1/65/66 DRB \+ Actions: \- During Transition: Start a "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure to change Transform Precoder state at RRC layer. * Requests transformPrecoderInd = disabled in the reconfiguration required message \- State Entry: To Transport Precoder Disabled state. * Interworking with Number of SRS ports: If UE is noncoherent and SRS Port Switching is active : \+ Resume using rank and number of SRS ports stored during the TP Off to On transition. \+ If rank stored during the TP Off to On transition =2, prevent reconfiguration for number of SRS ports to 1 \+ Failure: UE is returned to Transform Precoder Disabled state upon any gNB internal failure for the "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure. * + TP On to TP On: Stay in same state \- Trigger:Cell reconfiguration has NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlDftSOfdm = False * Definitions: All of the terms used in the state transition definitions in this requirement are defined in ([11140853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0dvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Notes: * See ([12977638](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_9ECYELXZEfCQT7hYUxERAg) ) for a reference state machine diagram \+ States referenced here are in that diagram. \+ The diagram also shows substates to clarify VoNR vs nonVoNR behavior. the diagram is meant to be consistent with this requirement. \+ However in case of conflict, this requirement governs. Illustration: The following figure illustrates the state transition triggers, unless trigger is exempted as above: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a line graph that plots "rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch" against "Time". The graph shows a blue line representing the "rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch" value over time. There are two horizontal dashed lines, one green labeled "rrmThresholdTpOff" and one orange labeled "rrmThresholdTpOn". The graph is divided into segments indicated by vertical dashed lines and colored arrows with text labels. The first segment, from the left, shows an orange arrow above the graph with the text "TP Disabled". Below the graph in this segment, there are several orange upward-pointing arrows clustered together, and a bracket labeled "rrmTpOnHystThreshold". The second segment, starting from the first vertical dashed line, shows a green arrow above the graph with the text "TP Enabled". The blue line fluctuates above the "rrmThresholdTpOff" line in this segment. The third segment, starting from the second vertical dashed line, shows another orange arrow above the graph with the text "TP Disabled". The blue line drops below the "rrmThresholdTpOn" line in this segment. Below the graph in this segment, there are several blue upward-pointing arrows and a dotted purple line, with a bracket labeled "rrmTpOnHystThreshold". The x-axis is labeled "Time" and has an arrow indicating the direction of time progression.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_8737.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Diagram can be found at: File: Diagrams for PIST CNIs on PUSCH Transform Precoder Enhancements.pptx Folder:

---

##### 3.9.2.6.2.0-7 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 Terminology for Transform Precoder State Transitions (ID: 11140853)

**3.9.2.6.2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `12977656`)

Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 The gNB-DU shall follow the definitions below for terms used in defining PUSCH Transform Precoder state transitions at 5G_UP_ALG_26586_replaced([11140818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * Common Definitions:
  * **rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch =rrmTpSinrMetric + rrmOffsetTpSwitch**
  * rrmTpSinrMetric: 
    * If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPreEnhSinrMetric = true (CNI-108976 is enabled):
    * rrmTpSinrMetric = **rrmCorrAvgSinr, the average WB-SINR corrected by OLLA (as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3087_replaced([11130243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq_mhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**
    * Else:
  * rrmTpSinrMetric = **rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb (derived from rrmRescaledCorrAvgSinr per 5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced([11131515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), re-corrected as needed by either UL FDM (if active) for evaluated number of PRBs or DFT-S-OFDM maximum allowed PRBs less than maximum number of PRBs allowed by bandwith)**
  * rrmOffsetTpSwitch:
    * If PUSCH is in Rank_2 and PUSCH PRBs <= SRS PRBs and SINR source for Rank_1 is SRS (5G_UP_ALG_3081_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):
    * rrmOffsetTpSwitch = 10 * log( rrmMaxSinrPrbs / rrmMinSinrPrbs ) + 3 dB (non-zero only in UL Rank 2)
    * Else: rrmOffsetTpSwitch = 0
  * rrmMaxSinrPrbs = max (next PUSCH PRB, SRS PRB) and rrmMinSinrPrbs = min (next PUSCH PRB, SRS PRB)
  * TP On Definitions:
  * **rrmThresholdTpOn : rrmThresholdTpOn = rrmTpOnThresh** \+ rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset****
  * rrmTpOnThresh:
    * If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPreEnhSinrMetric = true:
    * For Red Cap UE: rrmTpOnThresh = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOnTotPwrThreshRedCap
    * IfElse: 
    * rrmTpOnThresh = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOnTotPwrThresh
    * Else:
    * For Red Cap UE: rrmTpOnThresh = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThrRedCap
    * Else: rrmTpOnThresh = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThresh
    * rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset:
    * If UE is configured as R16 DMRS for transform precoding (dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding-r16 is present in RRC setup/reconfiguration):
      * If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPreEnhSinrMetric = true:
      * rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset = rdUlTransPrecodeOnTotPwrThreshR16DmrsOffset (see 5G_UP_ALG_26616_replaced([11141778](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
    * IfElse: 
      * rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset = rdUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshR16DmrsOffset (see 5G_UP_ALG_22800_replaced([11141650](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
    * Else: rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset = 0
      * Note: for Red Cap UE: rrmUlTransPrecodeOnSinrThreshOffset is also added to rrmTpOnThresh for deriving rrmThresholdTpOn
  * **rrmTpOnHystThreshold:
    * [Before CB008148-D]
    * If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPreEnhSinrMetric = true:
    * rrmTpOnHystThreshold = rdTpOnHystThresh (5G_UP_ALG_26590_replaced([11141749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
    * Else:
    * rrmTpOnHystThreshold = rdTransPrecodeHystThresh (5G_L2_1459_replaced([11186412](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_275VmvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))​
    * [CB008148-D]
    * rrmTpOnHystThreshold = NRCELL.ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTpOffOnTriggerSpeedThresh
    * Note: this change applies to both L2-PS Baseline and L2-PS NewFR1**
  * [End CB008148-D]
  * TP Off Definitions:
  * **rrmThresholdTpOff :** rrmThresholdTpOff = rrmTpOffThresh + rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset****
  * rrmTpOffThresh:
    * If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPreEnhSinrMetric = true:
    * For Red Cap UE: rrmTpOffThresh = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOffTotPwrThreshRedCap
    * IfElse:
    * rrmTpOffThresh = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOffTotPwrThresh
    * Else:
    * For Red Cap UE: rrmTpOffThresh = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOffSinrThrRedCap
    * Else: rrmTpOffThresh = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOffSinrThresh
  * rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset:
    * If UE is configured as R16 DMRS for transform precoding (dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding-r16 is present in RRC setup/reconfiguration):
    * If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPreEnhSinrMetric = true:
      * rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset = rdUlTransPrecodeOffTotPwrThreshR16DmrsOffset (see 5G_UP_ALG_26617_replaced([11141794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
    * IfElse:
      * rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset = rdUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshR16DmrsOffset (see 5G_UP_ALG_22802_replaced([11141661](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr0s8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
    * Else: rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset = 0
    * Note: for Red Cap UE: rrmUlTransPrecodeOffSinrThreshOffset is also added to rrmTpOffThresh for deriving rrmThresholdTpOff
  * **rrmTpOffHystThreshold:
    * [Before CB008148-D]
    * If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPreEnhSinrMetric = true:
    * rrmTpOffHystThreshold = rdTpOffHystThresh (5G_UP_ALG_26592_replaced([11141764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr1UAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
    * Else:
    * rrmTpOffHystThreshold = rdTransPrecodeHystThresh (5G_L2_1459_replaced([11186412](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_275VmvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
    * [CB008148-D]
    * rrmTpOffHystThreshold = NRCELL.ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTpOnOffTriggerSpeedThresh
    * Note: this change applies to both L2-PS Baseline and L2-PS NewFR1**
  * [End CB008148-D]​​​​​​​​​​​​



Notes:

  * rrmCorrAvgSinr is rrmAvgSinrUl, adjusted by the delta SINR from UL OLLA.
  * The rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb metric may be used by other functions besides PUSCH waveform switching between CP OFDM and DFT-S-OFDM. The rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch metric is exclusive for PUSCH waveform switching and it is not used for link adaptation.
  * In Rank2, SINR is 3dB less than for Rank1 so rrmOffsetTpSwitch is further adjusted by 3dB to further reduce chances of UL waveform switching ping-pong.
  * If CB006086 is enabled, the SINR source for Rank_1 can still be SRS : it happens when UL waveform switch from CP-OFDM to DFT-s-OFDM occurs before change of number of SRS ports.
  * PUSCH PRB <= SRS PRB applies when wideband SRS is used and can lead to rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb with Rank1 and DFT-S-OFDM being much larger than rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb with Rank2 prior to switch to DFT-S-OFDM. This causes UL waveform switching ping-pongs because rrmReScaledCorrAvgSinrFullPrb is immediately above NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeOffSinrThresh. Using rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch (which has a positive offset in Rank2), means that when switch to DFT-S-OFDM occurs while UE is in Rank2 the value of rrmAvgSinrTpSwitch remains bellow NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeOffSinrThresh once in DFT-S-OFDM.
  * If UL SINR source is RANK_1_SRS (TDD FR1, NRBTS/NRCELL-ulSinrSourceForRank1SuMimo=0, and ulPmiRank1Sinr from SRS is NOT DTX) or If UL SINR source is RANK_1_SINGLE_TX : {FDD or (TDD FR1, NRBTS/NRCELL-ulSinrSourceForRank1SuMimo=1 or NRBTS/NRCELL-ulSinrSourceForRank1SuMimo=0 and SRS is DTX)}, rrmOffsetTpSwitch = 0 (offset is not needed)
  * Supported RedCap UE has only single transmit antenna configuration and is power-limited comparing to non-RedCap UE (20 dBm vs 23 dBm), thus dedicated parameter: MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulTransPrecodeOnSinrThrRedCap is introduced to allow different configuration strategies for RedCap and non-RedCap UEs.

---

##### 3.9.2.6.2.0-8 Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 Handling Transform Precoder State Transition Rejections (ID: 12977668)

**3.9.2.6.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `12977669`)

Transform Precoder for DCI 0_1 The gNB-DU shall respond to a rejection (for any reason) of a reconfiguration request indication sent to L3 for a PUSCH Transform Precoder (TP) purpose as follows:

  *     * Use a threshold value equal to the following on any subsequent ‘reconfiguration request indication’ associated with TP switching 
    * **rrmTpOnHystThreshold** slowed down version = min (1000, 2 * **rrmTpOnHystThreshold** )
    * **rrmTpOffHystThreshold** slowed down version = min (1000, 2 * **rrmTpOffHystThreshold**)
  * Reset the value of the hysteresis threshold upon an acceptance response from L3 to reconfiguration request indication (use **rrmTpOnHystThreshold and rrmTpOffHystThreshold** without modification)



Notes:

  * This reqirement applies to both L2-PS Baseline and L2-PS NewFR1
  * **rrmTpOnHystThreshold and rrmTpOffHystThreshold** are defined in ([11140853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_aVqOkPvLEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * 1000 is the max vale in the now deprecated R&D parameters (in favor of OAM parameters) for **rrmTpOnHystThreshold and rrmTpOffHystThreshold** and it's selection by operator would be very rare . Intent is to keep the slowed down threshold at or below this value.
  * All DCI 0_1 Transform Precoder related transitions based on SINR criteria require a gNB-DU triggered RRC ReConfiguration procedure. That procedure starts with an ‘reconfiguration request indication’ to L3 and formally ends with a ‘reconfiguration complete indication’ from L3. It is also possible that L3 rejects a ‘reconfiguration request indication’ because it is busy with other procedures for that UE.
  * L2-PS sends a ‘reconfiguration request indication’ associated with TP based on SINR metric threshold criteria being met. If L3 is busy for a long period of time, the resulting rejection message exchange between gNB-DU and gNB-CU over F1P can add up to many messages (in the neighborhood of 60 messages seen in field logs). This needs to be managed better, which leads for specification above to double the hysteresis threshold used for deriving the SINR threshold criteria to slow down the rate of L2-PS attempting these transitions while L3 is busy.

---

#### 3.9.2.6.3 Applying Transform Precoder

##### 3.9.2.6.3.0-1 Applying Transform Precoder UL Waveform Settings While in Transform Precoder Enabled State (ID: 11140586)

**3.9.2.6.3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12977667`)

Applying Transform Precoder The gNB-DU shall schedule PUSCH transmissions with Transform Precoder having the following characteristics:

  * MCS Table:
  * Allocated PRBs
  * Total allocated sub-carriers (12 * total allocated PRBs) must be divisible by product of , where a2, a3, and a5 are positive integers.
  * PUSCH VRB-to-PRB mapping is set to non-interleaved
  * Resource Allocation Type: RAT1 only 
  * This is regardless of' resourceAllocation' indication from CP-RT.
  * MIMO:
  * UL SU MIMO
    * Rank: Forced to Rank 1, per 3GPP
    * Rank measurements for noncoherent UEs which are in a Transform Precoder enabled state (TP On):
    * If UE is configured for always TP On while configured with a VoNR DRB (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE):
      * Rank measurements are as per ([11139943](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq79fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
    * Else:
      * Rank measurements may continue
  * UL Frequency Hopping: Not supported
  * UL LA: ILLA uses MCS-to-SINR mapping tables for Transform Precoder. See ([11137031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krYBCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
  * Rank / number of layers: forced to 1
  * Number of CDM groups without data: 2
  * DMRS:
  * 3 OFDM symbols
  * Additional DMRS position: 2



Exceptions:

  * Associated PUSCH Transmission grants:
  * Msg3 (RAR): TP On is applied to all Msg3 transmissions with the characteristics shown above (except for pi/2-BPSK which is not supported) if [Before CB008148-A-UPD006]NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains ‘Msg3_TPOn’[CB008148-A-UPD006] NRCELL.actMsg3TP = TRUE[End CB008148-A-UPD006]
    * Default Transform Precoder specific 64QAM MCS table is always used
    * Note: All UEs are made aware by L3 in SIB1 content (msg3-transformPrecoder field of RACH-CommonConfig IE) and L3 will notify L2-PS
  * DCI 0_0: TP On is applied to all DCI 0_0 transmissions with the characteristics shown above if [Before CB008148-A-UPD006]NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains ‘Dci00_TPOn’[CB008148-A-UPD006] NRCELL.actMsg3TP = TRUE[End CB008148-A-UPD006]
    * Default Transform Precoder specific 64QAM MCS table is always used
    * [Before CB008148-A-UPD006]Note: Specific UEs are made aware by L3 in a DL RRC message during UE setup (msg3-transformPrecoder field of RACH-CommonConfig IE) and L3 will notify L2-PS[End CB008148-A-UPD006]
    * pi/2-BPSK which is supported, but it applies after first RRC ReConfiguration in UE setup
  * DCI 0_1: TP On can be applied to all DCI 0_1 transmissions with the characteristics shown above



Notes:

  * Msg3 and DCI 0_0 aspects above are only for L2-Ps NewFR1
  * pi/2-BPSK (q=1) is used if all of the following are true:
  * CP-RT indicates UE support at user setup
  * CP-RT indicates gNB support at cell setup
  * UE is configured with Transform Precoder specific 64QAM MCS table
  * Power boosting for pi/2-BPSK is supported based on UE Capabilities, and indicated by CP-RT at user setup (TDD only, per 3GPP)
  * UE is noncoherent means pusch-TransCoherence = noncoherent
  * VoNR DRB means configured with 5QI-1,5QI-65, or 5QI-66

---

##### 3.9.2.6.3.0-2 Applying Transform Precoder MPR-Aware LA While in Transform Precoder Enabled State (ID: 11140627)

**3.9.2.6.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11140646`)

Applying Transform Precoder When UL waveform selection is in the TP 0_0 OFF & 0_1 ON state (see 5G_UP_ALG_3270_replaced([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), UL Link Adaptation should consider MPR by UE in same way as done for CP OFDM. Main points:

  * Determination if UE is power limited, per PHR as in 5G_UP_ALG_9755_replaced([11130171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_ffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * PRB allocation regions per 5G_UP_ALG_9755_replaced([11130171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_ffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * MPR values **[Before CB006449-AB] per rdMprFdd and rdMprTddFr1**[End CB006449-AB], used in same way as for:
  * scaled PHR calculation (5G_UP_ALG_9755_replaced([11130171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_ffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),
  * avg UL SINR derivation (5G_UP_ALG_3078_replaced([11130719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krANl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),
  * corrected SINR derivation (5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced([11131515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),
  * MCS swich point derivation and usage (5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced([11131515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))****
  * Max PRBs allocated: as in 5G_UP_ALG_5010_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * MCS switch points table override by parameter ​rdMcsStartConsiderMPR (5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced([11131515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

##### 3.9.2.6.3.0-3 Applying Transform Precoder PUSCH half-Pi BPSK power boosting determination for transform precoding (ID: 11140882)

**3.9.2.6.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11140889`)

Applying Transform Precoder gNB-DU shall determine UE is capable of PUSCH power boosting for transform precoding in a specific serving cell if:

\- UE is configured by RRC setup/reconfiguration with powerBoostPi2BPSK and tp-pi2BPSK enabled.

\- and UE is power class 3 in this cell

\- and UE is in Transform Precoding Enabled status

Note:

  1. UE may report different power class for different band, then different cell may have different power class.

  2. An UE configured with powerBoostPi2BPSK enabled doesn't mean UE is capable of power boosting in a specific cell, for example the power class 2 UE can be also configured as powerBoostPi2BPSK enabled, and the power boosting could be in principle triggered when UE falls back to power class 3 (e.g. due to more than 50% symbols used in UL transmission according to 38.101-1). gNB-DU assumes UE with power class 2 is not capable of power boosting as for all existing TDD FR1 frame structure, UE cannot fullfill the condition to fallback to power class 3.

  3. An UE determined by gNB-DU as capable of power boosting doesn't mean the power boosting can be always triggered even when Pi/2 BPSK modulation order is used. According to 38.101-1, UE can apply power boost only when some certain requirement is achieved, e.g. no more than 40% symbols are used on UL transmission in a certain measurement period; As the measurement period is unknown, gNB has no accurate information whether UE applied power boosting, therefore gNB-DU does not measure the actual trigger of power boosting based on UL transmissions.

  4. In current system design, power class check is not mandatory in gNB-DU SW, i.e. gNB-DU could assume power class 3 is used in this requirement. This requirement is always used together with 5G_UP_ALG_22733_replaced([11140870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0ePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), i.e. when R16 DMRS is used, while gNB-CU already ensured R16 DMRS is configured to power class 3 UE.

---

#### 3.9.2.6.4 Transform Precoder for PUSCH DMRS

##### 3.9.2.6.4.0-1 Transform Precoder for PUSCH DMRS PUSCH DMRS sequence determination for transform precoding (ID: 11140870)

**3.9.2.6.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11140877`)

Transform Precoder for PUSCH DMRS gNB-DU shall determine R16 DMRS is used in a specific PUSCH transmission if:

\- UE is configured by RRC setup/reconfiguration with dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding-r16

\- and UE is in Transform Precoding Enabled status

\- and DCI 0-1 is used

\- and MCS is 0 or 1 [CB007103-F] or 28 [End CB007103-F]

otherwise R15 DMRS is used.

---

##### 3.9.2.6.4.0-2 Transform Precoder for PUSCH DMRS Transient phase handling for PUCCH format 3 DMRS sequence reconfiguration (ID: 11140896)

**3.9.2.6.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11140901`)

Transform Precoder for PUSCH DMRS In RRC [Before PR773425] reconfiguration [PR773425] procedure which modifies UE dedicated configuration [End PR773425], gNB-CU may reconfigure PUCCH format 3 DMRS sequence, i.e. from R15 DMRS to R16 DMRS, or from R16 DMRS to R15 DMRS; In such scenario, gNB-DU shall

\- avoid transmit harq-ack on PUCCH format 3 during the RRC reconfiguration transient phase by

\- Restrict Pcell DL scheduling according to 5G_UP_ALG_4196_replaced([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- [CB007103-D]If Scell is activated, Suspend and resume DPA for Scell according to 5G_UP_ALG_22730_replaced([11123985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB007103-D]

\- and use old configuration to decode periodic PUCCH format 3 but

\-- Ignore PUCCH format 3 measurements used for TA (5G_UP_ALG_3313_replaced([11150163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksSnAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), CFO (5G_UP_ALG_3324_replaced([11150688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksVDQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UL power control (5G_UP_ALG_2647_replaced([11119377](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[PR773425]Note: This requirement is not performed for RRC Reestablishment or RRC Resume where PUCCH format 3 is added by new dedicated configuration.[End PR773425]

---

### 3.9.2.7 Support 256 QAM for PUSCH

#### 3.9.2.7.1 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling

#### 3.9.2.7.1-1 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling

##### 3.9.2.7.1-1.0-2 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling L2-PS shall consider 256QAM for PUSCH enabled and with defined restrictions only if corresponding L1 hardware type supports it, as referenced by 5G_UP_ALG_1015_replaced( 11103515 ). [CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A] (ID: 13461446)

#### 3.9.2.7.1-2 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling

##### 3.9.2.7.1-2.0-2 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling The O&amp;M parameter 'actUl256Qam' for UL 256QAM activation/deactivation shall be designed as “on-line” modification without requiring to lock a cell. A change of the O&amp;M parameter setting shall be applied only for newly instantiated UEs. The change of the feature activation parameter shall not lead a UL 256QAM capable UE in the cell to have UL 256QAM mode transition, i.e., gNB shall not re-configure the UE’s 256QAM mode (either from UL 256QAM mode to UL non-256QAM mode or versa). When the feature is switched from “de-activated” to “activated”, if a UL 256QAM capable UEs which is new admitted to the cell by ICS, HO , Scell addition or re-establishment  shall be configured according to 5G_UP_ALG_3288_replaced( 11140921 ). if a UL 256QAM capable UE is already attached to the cell, the UE shall keep the same as before and shall not be reconfigured, they shall continue to be scheduled based on the legacy modulation table. When the feature is switched from “activated” to “de-activated”, all already admitted UL 256QAM capable UEs (either the UEs are in UL 256QAM mode or not) shall not be re-configured until the respective RRC connections are released (e.g, due to HO or transition to idle[CB008225-I]/Inactive[End CB008225-I]) or re-established. MAC continues to schedule these UEs according to their modes (UL 256QAM or UL non-256QAM). No special action is required for UL 256QAM related PMO counters. (ID: 11140993)

#### 3.9.2.7.1-3 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling

##### 3.9.2.7.1-3.0-2 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling When UE is in UL 256QAM mode (see 5G_UP_ALG_9481_replaced( 11140938 ) and 5G_UP_ALG_9487_replaced( 11140953 )), UL Link Adaptation should consider MPR by UE in same way as done before. Main points: Determination if UE is power limited, per PHR as in 5G_UP_ALG_9755_replaced( 11130171 ) PRB allocation regions per 5G_UP_ALG_9755_replaced( 11130171 ) MPR values [Before CB006449-AB] per rdMprFdd and rdMprTddFr1[End CB006449-AB], used in same way as for: - scaled PHR calculation (5G_UP_ALG_9755_replaced( 11130171 )), - avg UL SINR derivation (5G_UP_ALG_3078_replaced( 11130719 )), - corrected SINR derivation (5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced( 11131515 )), - MCS swich point derivation and usage (5G_UP_ALG_3090_replaced( 11131515 )) Max PRBs allocated: as in 5G_UP_ALG_5010_replaced( 11201008 ) MCS switch points table override by parameter ​rdMcsStartConsiderMPR (5G_UP_ALG_9487_replaced( 11140953 )) (ID: 11141014)

##### 3.9.2.7.1.0-1 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling UE with UL 256QAM capability or a UL 256QAM capable UE  (Informative) (ID: 11140921)

**3.9.2.7.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11140928`)

UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling A UE with UL 256QAM capability or a UL 256QAM capable UE is defined as:

  * The UE has reported UE capability of IE ModulationOrder "qam256" and IE RF-Parameters/BandNR/pusch-256QAM "supported" on a single component carrier within a band combination



See 3GPP 38.331 for detail definitions

---

##### 3.9.2.7.1.0-2 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling UE in UL 256QAM mode(Informative) (ID: 11140938)

**3.9.2.7.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11140944`)

UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling A UE with UL 256QAM mode on a serving cell (P(S)cell or Scell) is defined as:

  * The UE has UL 256QAM capability, and has been configured by gNB using RRCReconfiguration message with IE: RRC element PUSCH-Config/mcs-Table to “qam256” without transform precoder on the serving cell (see 3GPP 38.331 for detail field definitions).



Otherwise UE will be treated as UL non-256QAM mode on the serving cell. (Note if transformPrecoder is enabled on the serving cell, a UE with transform precoder capability will be regarded as UL non-256QAM mode even if this UE has UL 256QAM capability.)

A UE in UL 256QAM mode without transform precoder shall use 3GPP 38.214 table 5.1.3.1-2 to determine the modulation order, MCS.

A UE in non-256QAM mode without transform precoder shall use 3GPP 38.214 table 5.1.3.1-1 to determine the modulation order, MCS.

A UE in UL 256QAM mode with transform precoder shall still follow 5G_UP_ALG_3274_replaced([11140586](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krumWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (which is defined as a UE in UL non-256QAM mode with transform precoder) to use 64QAM table only (38.214 Table 6.1.4.1-1). RRCReconfiguration regarding PUSCH-Config/mcs-TableTransformPrecoder shall follow 5G_CP_IF_RRC_4003_replaced([11349520](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wXwf4_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.9.2.7.1.0-3 UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling Eligibility for UL 256QAM scheduling (ID: 11140953)

**3.9.2.7.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11140958`)

UE Eligibility for DCI 0_1 UL 256QAM scheduling UE is eligible for dynamic UL 256QAM scheduling when 256QAM for PUSCH is activated and if all of the following are true:

  * CP-RT indicates that 256QAM for PUSCH feature is activated online

  * CP-RT indicates that specific UE is in UL 256QAM mode as defined by 5G_UP_ALG_9481_replaced([11140938](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krwbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




A UE not meeting the criteria above shall only use up to 64QAM.

Notes:

  * 256QAM for PUSCH is activated when OAM parameter NRCELL\ actUl256Qam = TRUE, which is online modifiable.

  * 256QAM for PUSCH eligibility applies onwards from initial access after the transient phase when the UE capability is known or incoming Handover or Scell addition.

  * UL LA:




\- ILLA uses MCS-to-SINR mapping tables for 256QAM. See 5G_UP_ALG_3122_replaced([11133298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krIwcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for TDD FR1 and 5G_UP_ALG_3134_replaced([11136423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krUWrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for FDD respectively.

---

#### 3.9.2.7.2 RRC Reconfiguration Transition Phase Handling for SA Mode and 256QAM for PUSCH Feature

##### 3.9.2.7.2.0-1 RRC Reconfiguration Transition Phase Handling for SA Mode and 256QAM for PUSCH Feature UL scheduling of UL 256QAM capable UEs before/after "RRC Connection Reconfiguration" procedure (ID: 11141029)

**3.9.2.7.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11141042`)

RRC Reconfiguration Transition Phase Handling for SA Mode and 256QAM for PUSCH Feature Rationale: Before UL 256QAM capable UE reconfigure to UL 256QAM mode, UL scheduler perform link adaptation according to 64QAM MCS index table (3GPP TS38.214 5.1.3.1-1); After Cat-M1 UE reconfigure to UL 256QAM mode, UL scheduler perform link adaptation according to 256QAM MCS index table (3GPP TS38.214 5.1.3.1-2). To avoid ambiguous MCS/TBS LA, a transient phase which means the period between gNB sending "RRC Connection Reconfiguration" and receiving "RRC Connection Reconfiguration Complete" need to be considered. 

UL 256QAM capable UE have two different phases/periods of LA.

During the first phase, i.e., before gNB send "RRC CONNECTION RECONFIGURATION" message, UL scheduler shall perform link adaptation according to SINR to MCS mapping table for 64QAM.

During the second phase, i.e., after gNB receive "RRC CONNECTION RECONFIGURATION COMPLETE" message, UL scheduler shall perform link adaptation according to SINR to MCS mapping table for 256QAM. 

[CB013742-A] When NRBTS/actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom is set to disable,[End CB013742-A]between gNB sending "RRC Connection Reconfiguration" and receiving "RRC Connection Reconfiguration Complete" message, there is a period of time while gNB might have ambiguous MCS LA problem. The LA handling for this transient phase has to be modified. There are two options of LA handling during the transient phase:

Option 1: use MCS 0 which leads to same unambiguous assignment no matter whether UE is using 64QAM or 256QAM MCS index table.

Option 2: In UL scheduler CSS (Common Search Space) DCI 0_0 is being used to schedule which shalll use 64QAM MCS index table (3GPP TS38.214 5.1.3.1-1).

Normally "RRC Connection Reconfiguration Complete" message have 2bytes payload, plus 2bytes MAC header and 4 bytes RLC header, it is reasonable to use MCS0 to schedule this message, which is more robustness and assigned same unambiguous MCS.

If option1 is adapted, then LA including MCS/TBS adjustment is suspended during the transient phase. So Option 2 is adopted, please refer to 5G_UP_3196_replaced([11397111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uf04dvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_5097_replaced([11203479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfKhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

UL scheduler shall use last equivalent MCS/TBS during transient phase (i.e., in DCI 0_0) to schedule UL 256QAM capable UE when the UE is making initial context setup.

[CB013742-A]When NRBTS/actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom is set to enable, UL transmission is suspended (Refer 5G_UL_ALG_29060), hence there is no ambiguity in LA due to MCS [End CB013742-A]

Note: When UE trigger re-RACH procedure where C-RNTI is pre-assigned to the UE, if the UE has configured as UL 256QAM capable UE before call release, gNB shall schedule and do link adaptation from UL Grant over PDCCH after Msg3 during contention resolution using last MCS with new MCS index table as defined in TS38.214 5.1.3.1-2.

Please note that there is no transient phase for HO, RRC Reestablishment and re-RACH.

---

##### 3.9.2.7.2.0-2 RRC Reconfiguration Transition Phase Handling for SA Mode and 256QAM for PUSCH Feature Mapping table of MCS/TBS in Table 5.1.3.1-1 to MCS/TBS in Table 5.1.3.1-2 after transient phase (ID: 11141049)

**3.9.2.7.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11141056`)

RRC Reconfiguration Transition Phase Handling for SA Mode and 256QAM for PUSCH Feature Please note the last MCS/SE(Spectral Efficency) during DCI 0_0 is the MCS according to Table 5.1.3.1-1 in TS38.214 while MAC PS shall use last equivalent MCS/SE(Spectral Efficency during DCI 0_0 (please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3298_replaced([11141029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxCkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to schedule UL 256QAM capable UE (Table 5.1.3.1-2 in TS38.214) after transient phase when the UE is making initial context setup. Thus, a mapping table of MCS/TBS in Table 5.1.3.1-1 to MCS/SE(Spectral Efficency in Table 5.1.3.1-2 shall be defined as the following when using DCI 0_1 after transient phase. The general idea is to find an equivalent SE(Spectral Efficency or a maximum lower one if an equivalent one cannot be found and also match the modulation order between two tables.

##### 3.9.2.7.3.0-2 Interworking with Transform Precoder Switching from Transform Precoder to CP OFDM (ID: 11141105)

**3.9.2.7.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11141113`)

Thus, the same mapping table of MCS/SE(Spectral Efficency) in Table 5.1.3.1-1 to MCS/SE(Spectral Efficency) in Table 5.1.3.1-2 defined by 5G_UP_ALG_3299_replaced([11141049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxClPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be used as the following when using DCI 0_1 after transient phase. ### 3.9.2.8 Support 64QAMLowSE for PUSCH

#### 3.9.2.8.1 RRC Reconfiguration Transition Phase Handling for SA Mode and 64QAMLowSE for PUSCH Feature

##### 3.9.2.8.1.0-1 RRC Reconfiguration Transition Phase Handling for SA Mode and 64QAMLowSE for PUSCH Feature ... (ID: 11141133)

### 3.9.2.9 Antenna Port(s) in DCI 0_1

#### 3.9.2.9.0-1 Antenna Port(s) in DCI 0_1 Procedure in DCI_1 (ID: 13336778)

**3.9.2.9.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12516908`)

Antenna Port(s) in DCI 0_1 Step 1: Extract RRC Configuration Parameters

L2RT first obtains the following parameters from the RRC configuration per UE:

  * dmrs-Type (type1 or type2)
  * maxLength (len1 indicates 1 front loaded DMRS symbol, len2 indicates 2 front loaded symbols)
  * transformPrecoding (indicates whether transform precoding is enabled which is applicable to uplink)
  * rank



These parameters are derived from the PUSCH-Config, specifically from:

  * dmrs-UplinkForPUSCH-MapTypeA/B for uplink



Step 2: Locate the Corresponding Mapping Table in 3GPP TS 38.212

L2RT should refer to the relevant tables in Section 7.3.1.1.2 of 3GPP TS 38.212 to determine the specific Antenna port(s).

These tables define the Antenna port(s) that the UE should used based on the specific combination of the above configuration parameters.

Step3: Decide "Antenna Port(s)" for SU-MIMO UE

Step3.1 If the UE UL capability supports maxLength = len2 (as identified in step1), and the current slot is scheduled in UL SU-MIMO mode, the L2RT shall refer to the maxLength = 2 antenna port mapping table (as identified in Step 2), and narrow down to the rows where the "Number of front-loaded symbols" equals 1.

Then, based on the configured values for:

  * "Number of DMRS CDM groups without data", and
  * "DMRS port(s)",



L2RT shall determine the appropriate value to be signaled in the DCI 0_1.

Step3.2 If the UE UL capability supports maxLength = len1 (as identified in step1), L2RT shall refer to the maxLength = 1 antenna port mapping table (as identified in Step 2) and based on the configured values for :

  * "Number of DMRS CDM groups without data", and
  * "DMRS port(s)",



L2RT shall determine the appropriate value to be signaled in the DCI 0_1.

---

## 3.9.3 R&amp;D Parameters

### 3.9.3.0-1 R&amp;D Parameters rdNumSrsFreqHops (ID: 11141147)

**3.9.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11141155`)

R&D Parameters This Value is used to the number of frequency hops used to compute minimum rank for subband SRS.

Value range: 0..70

Default value: 3

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G_UP_ALG_3238_replaced([11155604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3240_replaced([11155613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3242_replaced([11155624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.9.3.0-2 R&amp;D Parameters rdAdaptiveSrsPortsFallbackRank2Timer (ID: 11141162)

**3.9.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11141170`)

R&D Parameters Description: When a RRC Reconfiguration with number of SRS Ports equal to "port1" failes: L2 PS starts a "fallbackRank2" timer whose duration is defined by this R&D parameter if NRCELL.actUlDftSOfdm = false. When the timer is running and UL rank selection algorithm outputs Rank2, the timer is stopped and the "adaptive number of SRS ports" state is "ulRank 2". When the timer expires, the "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure with number of SRS Ports equal to "port1" is restarted.

Value range: 0..4000

Default value: 2000

Unit: ms

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G_UP_ALG_3260_replaced([11157847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks-jgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.9.3.0-3 R&amp;D Parameters rdAdaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer (ID: 11141177)

**3.9.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11141182`)

R&D Parameters Description: When the L2-PS changes the UE "adaptive number of SRS ports" state to “ulRank 2” it starts a “adaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer” timer whose duration is defined by this R&D parameter if DFT-S-OFDM is deactivated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = false)

Value range: 0..3000

Default value: 1750

Unit: ms

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 50

Specified in: 5G_UP_ALG_10760_replaced([11157805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks98f_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.9.3.0-4 R&amp;D Parameters rdAdaptiveSrsPortsRankPollingTimer (ID: 11141189)

**3.9.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11141196`)

R&D Parameters Description: When the “adaptive number of SRS ports” state is “ulRank 2 ” and the “adaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer” timer is not running, L2-PS, once every period defined by this R&D parameter if DFT-S-OFDM is deactivated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = false) , checks the rank selection for the next transmission computation result

Value range: 0..500

Default value: 100

Unit: ms

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 10

Specified in: 5G_UP_ALG_10760_replaced([11157805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks98f_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.9.3.0-5 R&amp;D Parameters rdAdaptiveSrsPortsNbConsecutiveForReconf (ID: 11141204)

**3.9.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11141211`)

### 3.9.3.0-9 R&amp;D Parameters rdTPinteractionAdaptSrsPortsFallbackRank2Timer (ID: 11141254)

**3.9.3.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11141262`)

R&D Parameters Description: When a RRC Reconfiguration with number of SRS Ports equal to "port1" failes: L2 PS starts a "fallbackRank2" timer whose duration is defined by this R&D parameter if NRCELL.actUlDftSOfdm = true. When the timer is running and UL rank selection algorithm outputs Rank2, the timer is stopped and the "adaptive number of SRS ports" state is "ulRank 2". When the timer expires, the "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure with number of SRS Ports equal to "port1" is restarted.

Value range:

Default value: 150

Unit: ms

Online modifiable: No

Step Size:

Specified in: 5G_UP_ALG_3260_replaced([11157847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks-jgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
